[\[1b\]]
[\[1b.1\]{D2014}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_shrI ya mAn+ta ka badzra pra b+hed nA ma mU la man+t+rAr+tha/_bod skad du/_dpal gshin rje gshed po'i rtsa ba'i sngags don rdo rje rab tu 'byed pa zhes bya ba/_dpal
[\[1b.2\]]'jam mgon la phyag 'tshal lo/_/'jam rgyal khro bo'i gsang sngags gang /_/rgyud gzhan kun du sbas byas shing /_/ma byung 'byung bar mi 'gyur ba/_/rgya mtsho rgya dang rdo rje ltar/_/brtag dang 'da'
[\[1b.3\]]dka' mi phyed pa/_/ded dpon nyi ma bcud len bzhin/_/'dren sel rnam par sbyong ba'o/_/dri za'i grong dang sangs rgyas bzhin/_/sgo dang byin rlabs mtha' yas pa/_/ji ltar nam mkha' lding gi
[\[1b.4\]]rigs/_/gcig kyang skye ba'i bye brag gis/_/rigs kyi bye brag rnam pa bzhi/_/de dag nang gi dbye ba yis/_/stong phrag nyi shu gcig la sogs/_/mtha' yas bshad pa ji lta bar/_/rtsa ba'i snying po
[\[1b.5\]]la sogs pa'i/_/gsang sngags gang yin rigs gcig kyang /_/yi ge bsdu dang gtor ba dang /_/de bzhin rab tu gtor ba dang /_/yan lag so sor phye ba yis/_/sngags don sgo bzhir shes
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]par bya/_/sngags don de dag re re yang /_/rnam grangs sgo zhes bya ba yis/_/sgo mtha' yas par gyur pa ni/_/ye shes chags pa mi mnga' ba'i/_/'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis mkhyen pa las/_/nyan
[\[2a.2\]]thos rnams kyis mi shes na/_/'jig rten pa yis smos ci dgos/_/'di ltar sngags don mtha' yas shing /_/byin rlabs bsam gyis mi khyab kyang /_/thub pa bdag nyid chen po yis/_/gang gi don du gang sbyar
[\[2a.3\]]ba'i/_/gleng gzhi'i dbang du mdzad pa bzhin/_/gang gis de ltar sbyar byas pa/_/de la de yi dngos grub dag_/ngo bo nyid kyis myur bar gsungs/_/de phyir rgyal ba'i bstan pa la/_/bdud rnams 'dul bar byed pa yi/_/
[\[2a.4\]]khro bo'i mchog ni gshin rje gshed/_/las rnams grub par byed pa la/_/'khor lo sbyor ba rnams kyi mchog_/sngags kyi nang na rtsa ba ste/_/khro bo nyid yin mnyes byed cing /_/de yi bka' bzhin grub byed pa'o/_/gsang
[\[2a.5\]]sngags yi ge sum cu gnyis/_/bcu bdun yin te lngar yang shes/_/'di dag rab tu gtor tshul bshad/_/ya/_khro bo'i rgyal po gshin rje gshed/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi rdo rje thugs/_/ye shes rab tu mi g.yo ba/_/gzung
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]'dzin rnam shes dag pa'o/_/k+She/_zhing khams rnam par dag pa na/_/tshogs mchog gnyis las grub pa'i sku/_/mchog tu snang bas snang mdzad de/_/lus dang gnas gzugs dag pa'o/_/ma/_sa chen gter gyi 'byung khungs bzhin/_/yon tan zad med gter gyur pas/_/rin chen
[\[2b.2\]]'byung gnas zhes bya ste/_/longs spyod tshor ba rnams dag pa'o/_/me/_lhun po bzhin du bstan pa yi/_/chos mchog mi g.yo brnyes pa yang /_/chos 'od dpag med ston mdzad de/_/tha snyad 'du shes dag pa'o/_/da/_sbyin dang snyan smra la sogs pa/_/'gro don spyod pa'i mtshan nyid ni/_/
[\[2b.3\]]bde gshegs mdzad don grub pa ste/_/'du byed dag pa'i bdag nyid do/_/dus gsum 'byung ba'i rgyal ba kun/_/thugs sogs chos kyi bdag nyid de/_/de phyir mi bskyod rdo rje sogs/_/rgyal ba rnam pa lngar 'dod do/_/ya/_gzung dang 'dzin pa spong byed pa'i/_/ye shes zung mthar phyin
[\[2b.4\]]pa ste/_/lta dman spong ba'i dran pa ni/_/bde gshegs kun kyang 'gugs par byed/_/ts+tsha/_dpyod pa rnam par bral ba yi/_/ye shes shes rab mthar byed yin/_/yang dag spong ba'i brtson 'grus ni/_/rgyal ba'ang sems can don du 'jug_/ni/_nges tshig brjod pa mtha' yas pa/_/
[\[2b.5\]]brjod pa bral ba pad mthar 'byin/_/rdzu 'phrul ting 'dzin mi g.yo ba/_/rgyal ba'ang sems can don du 'ching /_/rA/_rdul bral rnam par mi rtog pa'i/_/ye shes bgegs mthar 'byin pa ste/_/dad sogs dbang du gyur pa ni/_/rgyal ba'ang sems can dbang du byed/_/byang chub phyogs
[\[2b.6\]]chos rang bzhin ni/_/thar pa'i grong khyer sgo yin te/_/sgrib pa spong ba'i ye shes ni/_/khro bo sgo skyong zhes bshad do/_/dzA/_'gro 'dzin shes bya stong nyid sa/_/byams pa chen po'i ngo bo nyid/_/gzigs pa rnam dag spyod yul phyir/_/sangs rgyas spyan zhes brjod pa yin/_/sa/_sems
[\[2b.7\]]can kun du sdud byed pa/_/snying rjes brlan pa chu yi khams/_/'gro ba bdag gir byed pa na/_/rgyal ba'i yum mchog mA ma kI/_/do/_/nyes pa sel byed shes rab me/_/dga' ba chen po'i bdag nyid de/_/dri ma kun nas dag pa'i phyir/_/gos dkar mo zhes 'dod pa yin/_/ru/_khro dang
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]chags pa gnyis med pa'i/_/btang snyoms ye shes chags bral rlung /_/'gro ba gnas nas 'don pa'i thabs/_/sgrol ma zhes su rnam par bshad/_/stong nyid dang ni snying rje dang /_/shes rab dang ni thabs rnams las/_/rgyal ba 'byung phyir spyod yul phyir/_/
[\[3a.2\]]'gro ba skyob phyir yum du 'dod/_/naM/_sna tshogs rnam par spras pa'i gzugs/_/phyag rgya'i mchod pa bla med pa/_/byang chub sems kyi ngo bo nyid/_/rgyal ba mnyes byed dam pa'o/_/yo/_/gang zhig rab tu gdangs snyan glu/_/sgra yi mchod pa bla med de/_/bstan pa dam pa'i
[\[3a.3\]]dngos nyid chos/_/mchod pa rgyal ba mnyes par byed/_/ni/_dri med rnam par dag pa'i dri/_/tshul khrims dag pa'i bdag nyid de/_/bla med dri yi mchod pa 'dis/_/sangs rgyas thams cad dgyes par byed/_/ra/_khu ba bcud len ro yi mchog_/ting 'dzin rab tu mi g.yo ba/_/
[\[3a.4\]]bde gshegs mdzad pa'i bdag nyid de/_/rgyal ba mnyes byed dam pa'o/_/gzugs sogs 'dod pa'i bdag nyid ni/_/byang chub sems sogs 'dod pa'i mchog_/longs spyod mchod pa'i rang bzhin 'di/_/bud med gzugs su rnam par brtags/_/lus dang gnas dang longs
[\[3a.5\]]spyod las/_/sgrib pa kun du 'byung bas na/_/'di dag tsam gyis zag bcas kyi/_/chos kun yongs su bsdus par 'dod/_/de dag nyid las bzlog pa'i chos/_/'bras bu dang ni don dam dang /_/lam dang bstan pa dam pa yis/_/zag pa med chos bsdus pa yin/_/gtso bo yum dang
[\[3a.6\]]mchod pa dang /_/de bzhin sgo skyong bcas pa yi/_/zag bcas zag med dbyer med pa'i/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor thams cad bsdus/_/gang zhig yi ge phreng ba'i don/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bdag nyid du/_/bsgom dang bzlas la brtson byed pa/_/myur du rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor 'gyur/_/
[\[3a.7\]]de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha'i rgyud de/_/ya ni rdo rje gshin rje dgra'o/_/k+She ni rdo rje zhing ngo /_/ma ni rdo rje sa'o/_/me ni rdo rje lhun po'o/_/da ni rdo rje sbyin pa'o/_/ya ni rdo rje zung ngo /_/ts+tsha ni rdo rje dpyod pa'o/_/ni ni rdo rje nges tshig go/_/rA ni rdo rje rdul bral lo/_/dzA ni rdo rje 'gro 'dzin no/_/sa
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]ni rdo rje kun sdud do/_/do ni rdo rje nyes sel lo/_/ru ni rdo rje gnas med do/_/na ni rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs so/_/yo ni rdo rje gdangs so/_/ni ni rdo rje dri med do/_/ra ni rdo rje ro'o/_/de la 'di ni rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i rgyud de/_/rdo rje gshin rje'i sgra ni zhing dag pa'i rang bzhin no/_/rdo rje'i
[\[3b.2\]]zhing ni zhing dag pa'i gzugs so/_/rdo rje sa ni zhing dag pa'i yon tan gyi bdag nyid do/_/rdo rje lhun po ni zhing dag pa'i chos so/_/rdo rje sbyin pa ni zhing dag pa'i dpyod pa'o/_/rdo rje zung ni sgo dag pa'i dang po ste 'jug pa dang 'byung ba'i sgo'o/_/rdo rje dpyod pa ni sgo dag pa gnyis pa ste btang ba dang
[\[3b.3\]]len pa'i sgo'o/_/rdo rje nges tshig ni sgo dag pa gsum pa ste dpyod pa dang brtson pa'i sgo'o/_/rdo rje rdul bral ni sgo dag pa bzhi pa ste sbyong ba dang sbyor ba'i sgo'o/_/rdo rje 'gro 'dzin ni gnas dag pa bzhi'o/_/rdo rje kun sdud ni gnas dag pa'i bla gab bo/_/rdo rje nges tshig ni sgo dag pa'i gdan
[\[3b.4\]]no/_/rdo rje gnas med ni gnas dag pa'i snang ba'o/_/rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs ni longs spyod dag pa dang po ste/_rab tu spro ba'i kha dog dang dbyibs so/_/rdo rje gdangs ni longs spyod dag pa gnyis pa ste rab tu spro ba'i dbyangs dang tshig dag go/_/rdo rje dri med ni longs spyod dag pa gsum
[\[3b.5\]]pa ste rab tu spro ba'i dri sna tshogs so/_/rdo rje ro ni longs spyod dag pa bzhi pa ste/_rab tu spro ba'i ro sna tshogs so/_/de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi yan lag gi rgyud de/_rdo rje gshin rje'i dgra ni lus dang snying ga'i gnas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_nag po dang rdo rje ni kha dog dang mtshan
[\[3b.6\]]ma'o/_/rdo rje'i zhing ni mtshog ma byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dkar po dang 'khor lo ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje'i sa ni lte ba'i gnas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_ser po dang rin po che ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje lhun po ni mgrin pa'i gnas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dmar po dang pad+ma
[\[3b.7\]]ni kha dog dang mtshan pa'o/_/rdo rje byin pa ni rkang pa'i gnas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_ljang gu dang ral gri ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje zung ni lag pa g.yas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dkar po dang tho ba ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje dpyod pa ni lag pa g.yon byin gyis rlob pa
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]ste/_sngon po dang dbyug pa ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje nges tshig ni kha byin gyis rlob pa ste dmar po dang pad+ma ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje rdul ni gsal ba'i gnas byin gyis rlob pa ste/_ljang gu dang ral gri ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje 'gro 'dzin
[\[4a.2\]]ni mtshog ma'i gnas su g.yas phyogs byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dkar mo dang 'khor lo ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje kun sdud ni lte ba'i gnas su g.yon phyogs byin gyis rlob pa ste/_mthing ga dang rdo rje ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje nyes sel ni mgrin pa'i gnas su g.yon
[\[4a.3\]]phyogs byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dmar mo dang pad+ma ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje gnas med ni rkang pa'i gnas su g.yon phyogs byin gyis rlob pa ste/_ljang gu dang ut+pal ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs ni mig byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dkar mo dang me long
[\[4a.4\]]ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje gdangs ni rna ba byin gyis rlob pa ste/_dmar mo dang gling bu ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje dri med ni sna byin gyis rlob pa ste/_mthing ga dang spos phor ni kha dog dang mtshan ma'o/_/rdo rje ro ni lce byin gyis rlob pa ste/_ljang gu dang ro snod ni kha dog dang
[\[4a.5\]]mtshan ma'o/_/de la 'di ni rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi gsang sngags kyi rgyud de/_ya rdo rje gshin rje dgra'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra ya mA ri rdo rje gshin rje dgra'i gsang sngags so/_/k+She rdo rje zhing gi sa bon no/_/oM badzra k+She tra rdo rje zhing gi gsang sngags so/_/ma rdo rje sa'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra
[\[4a.6\]]ma hI n+d+ri/_rdo rje sa'i gsang sngags so/_/me rdo rje lhun po'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra me ru rdo rje lhun po'i gsang sngags so/_/dA rdo rje sbyin pa'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra dA na rdo rje sbyin pa'i gsang sngags so/_/ya rdo rje zung gi sa bon no/_/oM badzra ya ma rdo rje zung gi gsang sngags so/_/ts+tsha rdo rje
[\[4a.7\]]dpyod pa'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra tsartsa na rdo rje dpyod pa'i gsang sngags so/_/ni rdo rje nges tshig gi sa bon no/_/oM badzra me ruk+ti rdo rje nges tshig gi gsang sngags so/_/rA rdo rje rdul bral gyi sa bon no/_/oM badzra rA dza rdo rje rdul bral gyi gsang sngags so/_/dza rdo rje 'gro 'dzin gyi sa bon
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]no/_/oM badzra dza g+haM d+ha ra rdo rje 'gro 'dzin gyi gsang sngags so/_/sa rdo rje kun sdud kyi sa bon no/_/oM badzra saM ha ra ni/_rdo rje kun sdud kyi gsang sngags so/_/do rdo rje nyes sel gyi sa bon no/_/oM badzra do ra hi da rdo rje nyes sel gyi gsang sngags so/_/ru rdo rje gnas med kyi sa bon no/_/
[\[4b.2\]]oM badzra ru ni la rdo rje gnas med kyi gsang sngags so/_/Na rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs kyi sa bon no/_/oM badzra Na na rU pa/_rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs kyi gsang sngags so/_/yo rdo rje gdangs kyi sa bon no/_/oM badzra yo ya ge yaM rdo rje gdangs kyi gsang sngags so/_/ni rdo rje dri med kyi sa bon no/_/
[\[4b.3\]]oM badzra nir ma la rdo rje dri med kyi gsang sngags so/_/ra rdo rje ro'i sa bon no/_/oM badzra rA sa rdo rje ro'i gsang sngags so/_/gsang sngags kyi yi ge tshig 'di dag la brten nas/_rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo dang /_rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi yan lag rnams legs par byin gyis rlob
[\[4b.4\]]par 'gyur ro/_/de ni yi ge rab gtor ba/_/mdor bsdus nas ni bshad pa yin/_/de nas yi ge gtor ba yi/_/sbyor ba tshul bzhin bshad par bya/_/gsang sngags yi ge sum cu gnyis/_/bsdu ba bcu bdun dag tu shes/_/gdug pa 'dul ba'i las rnams la/_/gtor ba
[\[4b.5\]]'di ni bshad par bya/_/dang por ya zhes gang gsungs pa/_/gdug pa thams cad 'jigs par byed/_/k+She zhes bya bas dgra rnams kun/_/zad par byed par gdon mi za/_/ma zhes bya bas de bzhin du/_/de dag myur du gsod par byed/_/me zhes bya ba'i ngo bo yis/_/kun
[\[4b.6\]]nas gnon par byed par bshad/_/da zhes bya ba 'joms pa ste/_/lus dang yan lag ma rung byed/_/de nas phyi rol bshad bya ste/_/ya zhes bya bas de bzhin du/_/'jig cing rnam par g.yeng bar byed/_/ts+tsha zhes bya bas pags pa nas/_/snying gi mthar yang za bar byed/_/
[\[4b.7\]]ni zhes bya bas lhag ma nas/_/cung zad lus par mi byed do/_/rA zhes bya bas gzugs rnams kun/_/rdul bzhin du ni bsnyil bar byed/_/dzA zhes bya bas dbang po rnams/_/rmugs par byed par gdon mi za/_/sa zhes bya bas yi dwags bzhin/_/'khor nas 'khyams
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]par byed pa yin/_/do zhes bya bas bzang po yang /_/dman pa dag tu byed par 'gyur/_/ru zhes bya bas khrag rnams kun/_/sbu gu'i gnas nas rmongs par 'gyur/_/na zhes bya bas thams cad du/_/rnams par 'dren par byed par bshad/_/yo
[\[5a.2\]]zhes bya bas las dag la/_/kun nas sbyor bar byed pa'o/_/ni zhes bya bas de bzhin du/_/dbang po nyams par byed pa ste/_/ra zhes bya ba dran pa'i gnas/_/bral bar byed par bshad pa'o/_/sgrub par byed pas tshul bzhin du/_/rdo rje dkyil 'khor mchog bsgoms te/_/
[\[5a.3\]]gsang sngags yi ge bcu bdun 'di/_/tshul bzhin sbyor ba gang shes pa/_/de ni ring po mi thogs par/_/gdug pa 'dul ba gdon mi za/_/gzhan yang gsang sngags yi ge ni/_/dpag bsam shing dang nor bu bzhin/_/dgos pa thams cad sgrub byed de/_/sgra dang yid la
[\[5a.4\]]byed pa yis/_/rjes su mthun par 'gro ba yin/_/ya zhes bya bas 'gugs pa dang /_/bskrad dang dbye ba sogs kyang byed/_/k+She zhes bya bas bsrung ba dang /_/gtong dang 'khrug pa'i las kyang byed/_/ma zhes bya bas rmongs pa dang /_/bskyed dang shes pa'i las kyang byed/_/me zhes
[\[5a.5\]]bya bas bdag nyid la/_/gang dag dgos pa de sbyor byed/_/da zhes bya bas 'dzin pa dang /_/sbyin dang 'dul ba'i las kyang byed/_/ya zhes bya bas de bzhin du/_/gang dag bstan pa de sbyor byed/_/ts+tsha zhes bya bas g.yo ba dang /_/'gro 'ong spyod pa'i las kyang byed/_/ni zhes bya bas
[\[5a.6\]]'gog pa dang /_/ma lus gdon mi za bar byed/_/rA zhes bya bas dga' ba dang /_/chags dang grags la sogs pa'ang byed/_/dzA zhes bya bas mig 'phrul dang /_/bskyed dang bsgyur ba la sogs byed/_/sa zhes bya bas bde ba dang /_/rdzogs dang sdud pa'i las kyang byed/_/do
[\[5a.7\]]zhes bya bas ring 'gro zhing /_/sman la sbyor dang sel bar byed/_/ru zhes bya ba khro ba dang /_/chags dang kun nas sgra sgrogs byed/_/na zhes bya ba thob byed cing /_/mthong dang 'dod pa 'dren par byed/_/yo zhes bya ba gang dang gang /_/rigs pa kun la sbyor bar byed/_/ni zhes bya ba
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]snga ma bzhin/_/'gog pa la sogs sbyor bar byed/_/ra zhes bya ba de bzhin du/_/dga' dang chags la sogs pa byed/_/sgra yi rjes su zhugs pa yis/_/las rnams gang dang gang byed pa/_/yi ge gtor ba'i tshul gyis ni/_/de dag mdor bsdus bshad pa yin/_/de nas bshad
[\[5b.2\]]par bya ba ni/_/kun nas bsdu ba zhes bya ba'i/_/gsang sngags sbyor ba'i tshul gang yin/_/mdor bsdus 'dir ni bshad par bya/_/thog mar brjod pa'i yi ge ni/_/ya ma rA zhes gang gsungs pa/_/yi dgas bdag po bod pa ste/_/las la skul bar byed pa'o/_/dzA sa
[\[5b.3\]]zhes bya ba'i yi ge gnyis/_/rmugs shing 'khrul dang 'khor ba ste/_/rgyas btab nas ni rmongs 'gyur ba'o/_/de nyid myur du bskul ba ni/_/do me ya zhes brjod pa ste/_/gshin rje dgra yi gsang sngags 'dis/_/'bad nas bskul ba byas pa ste/_/rgyas 'debs rnams
[\[5b.4\]]kyis rgyas btab na/_/yi dgas bzhin du 'khyams par 'gyur/_/gsang sngags tshig rkang dang po 'di/_/'gro ba rgyas 'debs dam pa'o/_/gnyis pa dag tu brjod pa'i sngags/_/ya me do zhes gang gsungs pa/_/ma gdon bdag po bod pa ste/_/las la skul bar
[\[5b.5\]]byed par bshad/_/ru Na zhes bya ba'i yi ge gnyis/_/lus kyi gnas rnams thams cad kyi/_/sbu gu'i gnas rnams thams cad nas/_/khrag kun yongs su 'dren par bshad/_/de nyid myur du skul byed pa/_/yo da ya zhes brjod pa ste/_/gang zhig gshin rje gshed kyi
[\[5b.6\]]sngags/_/'bad nas zlos par byed pa des/_/ma gdon bzhin du 'gro kun gyi/_/khrag rnams 'dren par gdon mi za/_/gsang sngags tshig rkang gnyis pa 'dis/_/khrag 'dren rnams kyis khrag drangs nas/_/rmongs par bya ba la sbyor ba/_/gshin rje gshed kyi bka'
[\[5b.7\]]yis so/_/gsum pa dag du gsungs pa yi/_/ya da yo zhes gang brjod pa/_/'joms byed bdag po bod pa ste/_/las la skul bar byed pa'o/_/ni ra zhes bya'i yi ge gnyis/_/dbang po gnas rnams thams cad du/_/nus pa nyams shing 'gog pa yis/_/dran pa
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]bral bar byed pa ste/_/de nyid myur du bskul ba ni/_/ya k+She ya zhes brjod pa ste/_/gang zhig gshin rje gshed po'i sngags/_/'bad nas zlos par byed pa des/_/'joms byed rnams kyis bcom nas ni/_/brgyal bar 'gyur bar gdon mi za/_/gsang
[\[6a.2\]]sngags tshig rkang gsum pa 'dis/_/shin tu rmongs par byas par 'gyur/_/bzhi pa dag tu gsungs pa'i sngags/_/ya k+She ya zhes gang gsungs pa/_/za byed bdag po bod pa ste/_/las la skul bar byed par bshad/_/ts+tsha ni zhes bya'i yi ge gnyis/_/pags pa mig dang
[\[6a.3\]]snying gi mthar/_/gzhib dang myang dang bza' ba yis/_/lhag ma cung zad ma lus byed/_/de nyid myur du bskul ba ni/_/rA ma ya zhes brjod pa ste/_/gang zhig gshin rje gshed po'i sngags/_/'bad nas zlos par byed pa des/_/gdug pa za bar bya ba la/_/za byed rnams
[\[6a.4\]]kyis za bar 'gyur/_/gsang sngags tshig rkang bzhi pa 'dis/_/gdug pa za ba'i mchog tu bshad/_/bstan pa dag la gnod byed pa'i/_/gdug pa tshar gcod bya ba'i phyir/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bsgoms nas ni/_/gsang sngags tshul bzhin gang zlos pa/_/de yis
[\[6a.5\]]gdug pa 'jig pa la/_/gsang sngags bsdu ba bshad pa'o/_/gzhan yang rgyal ba'i bstan pa la/_/kun nas dang ba'i 'gro ba rnams/_/de la phan gdags bskyab pa'i phyir/_/yi ge bsdu ba tshul bzhin bshad/_/gsang sngags yi ge sum cu gnyis/_/tshul bzhin

[\[6b.1\]]gsang sngags gnyis pa 'di yis ni/_/grags pa nyams pa gso bar byed/_/gsum pa dag tu gsungs pa'i sngags/_/da yo ra k+She zhes brjod pas/_/gang dag ji snyed yod pa yi/_/nor rnams kun du srung byed pa'o/_/gsum par gyur pa'i gsang sngags 'dis/_/
[\[6b.2\]]longs spyod nyams pa gso bar byed/_/bzhi par gyur pa'i gsang sngags gang /_/k+She ts+tsha ra ma zhes brjod pa/_/dga' ba'i spyod yul phun sum tshogs/_/yongs su srung bar byed pa ste/_/gsang sngags bzhi par gyur pa 'dis/_/dga' ba'i spyod yul thams cad la/_/
[\[6b.3\]]spyod par rang dbang thob pa ste/_/rgyal po chom rkun me la sogs/_/'jigs pa dag las thar bar 'gyur/_/dad ldan sems can bsrung ba'i phyir/_/gsang sngags bsdu ba bshad pa'o/_/de dag tsam gyis rtsa ba yi/_/sngags don kun nas bsdu ba bshad/_/de nas gzhan

[\[6b.5\]]'phrul 'byung ba'i sgo/_/oM ni mngon par rdzogs byang chub/_/de bas yi ge oM zhes bya/_/bkra shis phun sum tshogs pa'i phyir/_/phyag 'tshal yi ge zhes bya ste/_/gsang sngags gang dag brjod pa yi/_/thog mar yi ge 'di bzhag na/_/rab tu bsngags zhes bshad
[\[6b.6\]]pa yin/_/tha mar phyag 'tshal brjod pa las/_/ha ni mi phyed rdo rje ste/_/u ni byang chub sems bskyed pa/_/aM ni mngon par rdzogs byang chub/_/de phyir yi ge hUM zhes pa/_/thugs kyi rdo rje rten byed pa'o/_/gzhan yang bkra shis yi ge ni/_/sa ni yang dag mnyam pa

[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]de phyir sngags rnams thams cad kyi/_/mjug tu tshig 'di bsngags pa yin/_/de la sogs pa'i sngags tshig la/_/yi ge yan lag gang ldan pa/_/de dag bye brag rnam phye ste/_/chos don lha dang las rnams dag_/bye brag so sor sbyar byas pa/_/

[\[7a.3\]]ge bzhi/_byang dang shar dang lho dang nub rnams su rim pa bzhin du sngon po dang ser po dang dmar po dang dkar po'i kha dog dang ldan pa/_'od dang ldan pa bsam par bya'o/_/de nas yi ge maM de las oM badzra maM s+pha ra Na zhes bya bas bskul bas/_yi ge maM de las ye shes kyi rdo rje
[\[7a.4\]]byung nas 'jigs rten gyi khams thams cad du khyab ste/_'gro ba thams cad kyi ma rig pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i nga rgyal dang bcas pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang /_phyi rol dang /_nang gis thams cad la phog pas/_de dag gi dri ma thams cad yongs su dag par byas

[\[7a.7\]]bar gyur to/_/de nas yi ge raM de las oM badzra raM sba ra Na zhes bya bas bskul bas/_raM de las ye shes kyi me byung nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du khyab ste/_'gro ba thams cad kyi ma rig pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i zhe sdang dang bcas pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang phyi
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]rol dang nang gi me thams cad la phog pas dri ma thams cad dag par byas te/_ye shes kyi me dang dbyer med par gyur nas/_ye shes kyi me de yang de nyid du mi snang bar gyur to/_/de nas yi ge yaM de las oM badzra yaM sba ra Na zhes bskul bas/_de las ye shes kyi rlung byung nas/

[\[7b.3\]]gyur nas/_ye shes kyi rlung de yang de nyid du mi snang bar gyur to/_/de nas dri ma thams cad yongs su dag pa'i bdag nyid bdag dang gzhan gyi rgyud kyi dbyer med pa'i ngo bo nyid ye shes rang rig pa tsam sgyu ma lta bu chos kyi dbyings kyi bdag nyid du ro gcig par gyur pa ji ltar nus pa
[\[7b.4\]]de tsam du bsgom par bya'o/_/de nas snying rje chen po'i sems skyes pas/_de ma thag tu byang chub sems kyi rang bzhin de nyid nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gcig tu gyur to/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor de yang dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bzhin du dbus sa'i cha dgu dang ldan pa/_gru bzhi sgo
[\[7b.5\]]dang ldan pa'i phyi rol 'khor yug kun nas zlum pa/_'od zer rab tu 'phro ba dang ldan pa dang /_dbus kyi cha la yi ge ya kha dog mthing ga 'od zer gyi phreng bas kun nas bskor ba bsam par bya'o/_/shar phyogs kyi cha la yi ge k+She kha dog dkar po 'od zer gyi phreng bas kun nas
[\[7b.6\]]bskor ba bsam par bya'o/_/lho phyogs kyi cha la yi ge ma kha dog ser po 'od zer gyi phreng bas kun nas bskor ba bsam par bya'o/_/nub phyogs kyi cha la yi ge me kha dog dmar po 'od zer gyi phreng bas kun nas bskor ba bsam par bya'o/_/byang phyogs kyi cha la yi ge
[\[7b.7\]]da kha dog ljang gu 'od zer gyi phreng bas kun nas bskor ba bsam par bya'o/_/'od zer gyi phreng ba de dag kyang dang po rang rang gi kha dog dang 'dra ba'i 'od las/_phyi rol nyi ma'i 'od zer lta bu rab tu gsal bar 'phro ba'o/_/de nas shar lho'i cha la yi ge dzA kha dog dkar po 'od
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/lho nub kyi cha la yi ge sa kha dog sngon po 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/nub byang gi cha la yi ge dza kha dog dmar po 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/byang shar gyi cha la yi ge ru kha dog ljang gu 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/de'i phyi
[\[8a.2\]]rol gyi grwa rnams la/_shar lhor yi ge Na kha dog dkar po 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/lho nub tu yi ge yo kha dog mthing ga 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/nub byang du yi ge ni kha dog dmar po 'od zer gyi phreng ba can no/_/byang shar du yi ge rA kha dog ljang gu 'od zer gyi phreng ba can
[\[8a.3\]]no/_/'od zer gyi phreng ba brgyad po de dag kyang /_dang po rang rang 'dra ba'i 'od zer las phyi rol zla ba'i 'od zer lta bur gyur pa'o/_/shar gyi sgor yi ge ya kha dog dkar po/_/lho phyogs kyi sgor yi ge tsa kha dog mthing ga_/nub phyogs kyi sgor yi ge ni kha dog dmar po/_/byang phyogs

[\[8b\]]
[\[8b.1\]]byung nas chos 'byung ba'i phyag rgya thams cad gang bar byas te/_yi ge de dag kyang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku sha stag tu gyur nas/_chos 'byung ba'i phyag rgya yongs su gang bar byas so/_/de nas sku de dag kyang 'od du zhu bar gyur pa las bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho chen

[\[8b.3\]]'od zer byung bas pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng thams cad yongs su gang bar byas so/_/de nas yi ge de dag kyang bcom ldan 'das rin chen 'byung ba'i sku sha stag tu gyur nas pad+ma'i snying po la 'dus par gyur pas 'og tu zhu bar gyur nas/_rin po che gser gyi rang bzhin du

[\[8b.5\]]dpag med kyi sku sha stag tu gyur te pad+ma'i snying po gser gyi rang bzhin gyi gzhi la 'dus par gyur pas 'od du gyur nas rin po che sna bzhi las grub pa'i ri'i rgyal po lhun po rab tu brtan par gyur par bsam par bya'o/_/de nas yi ge da la dmigs te/_oM badzra da na zhes bya ba'i

[\[9a\]]
[\[9a.1\]]la sogs pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyang kha dog dang /_dbyibs dang /_reg bya dang gnas pas khyad par du byas pa'o/_/bdud rtsi'i chu dang /_btung ba'i chu dang /_khrus kyi chu dag kyang kha dog dang dbyibs dang dri dang ro dang yan lag dang gnas pas khyad par

[\[9a.3\]]ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_dza las dza'i 'od zer byung ste/_phyogs kun du gang bar byas nas de dag kyang sangs rgyas spyan gyi sku sha stag tu gyur te slar 'dus nas 'od du gyur pa las gzhal med khang gi gzhir gyur pa ni/_'di lta ste/_gzhi sna tshogs rdo rje las
[\[9a.4\]]grub cing /_phyogs kun du yang sna tshogs rdo rje ra ba dang /_dra ba 'ang 'khrigs par gyur pa de'i nang du/_rin po che sna bzhi'i rgyu las grub pa'i gzhal med khang gi gzhi grub par bsam mo/_/de nas yi ge sa la dmigs te/_oM badzra saM ha ra Ni zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags [(]gyis [,]kyis [)]

[\[9a.6\]]po dang /_phyam phran dang /_lan kan gyi dra ba dang /_rten ma dang /_gzer mig la sogs pas spras pa'i dbus na gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa gnas pa/_phyi rol rdo rje gur gyis yongs su 'khrigs par gtams pa'o/_/de nas yi ge do la dmigs te/_oM

[\[9b.4\]]sgo phun sum tshogs par gyur pa ni 'di lta ste/_sgo de yang sgo khang dang bcas pa/_sgo glegs dang /_them skas dang rta babs dang bcas pa/_'gro ba 'jug pa dang thugs rje 'byung ba'i mthu phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa'i sgor gyur pa'o/_/de nas yi ge tsa la dmigs

[\[9b.6\]]tshogs par gyur pa ni 'di lta ste/_gtong ba dang len pa'i mthu phun sum tshogs pa'i sgo'o/_/de nas yi ge ni la dmigs te/_oM badzra ni ru ka ti zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_ni las ni'i 'od zer byung nas nub phyogs su 'phros te de dag kyang pad+ma mthar

[\[10a\]]
[\[10a.1\]]dmigs te/_oM badzra rA dza zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_rA las rA'i 'od zer byung nas byang phyogs su 'phros te/_de yang bgegs mthar byed kyi sku sha stag tu gyur nas byang phyogs kyi sgor 'dus pa las 'od du gyur nas byang phyogs
[\[10a.2\]]kyi sgo de yang phun sum tshogs pa'i sgor gyur pa ni 'di lta ste/_sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyong ba dang /_sems can yongs su sgrol ba la sbyor ba'i mthu phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa'i sgo'o/_/de nas yi ge Na la dmigs te/_oM badzra Na na rU pa zhes bya ba'i gsang
[\[10a.3\]]sngags kyis bskul bas/_Na las Na'i 'od zer byung nas phyogs thams cad du 'phros te de dag kyang gzugs kyi rdo rje zhes bya ba'i lha mo'i sku sha stag tu gyur te slar gzhal yas khang gi 'khor yug tu 'dus nas gzugs kyi mchod pa thams cad byin gyis rlob par mdzad
[\[10a.4\]]par gyur to/_/de nas yi ge yo la dmigs te/_oM badzra yo ya ge yaM zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_yo las yo'i 'od zer byung nas phyogs thams cad du 'phros te de dag kyang sgra'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i lha mo'i sku sha stag tu gyur nas/_slar gzhal yas khang gi
[\[10a.5\]]'khor yug tu 'dus te/_sgra'i mchod pa thams cad byin gyis rlob par mdzad par gyur to/_/de nas yi ge ni la dmigs te/_oM badzra ni ra ma la zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_ni las ni'i 'od zer byung nas phyogs thams cad du 'phros te de dag kyang di'i rdo rje
[\[10a.6\]]zhes bya ba'i lha mo'i sku sha stag tu gyur nas/_slar gzhal yas khang gi 'khor yug tu 'dus te dri sna tshogs kyi mchod pa byin gyis rlob par mdzad par gyur to/_/de nas yi ge rA la dmigs te/_oM badzra rA sa zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_ra las ra'i 'od zer
[\[10a.7\]]byung nas phyogs thams cad du 'phros te de dag kyang ro'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i lha mo'i sku sha stag tu gyur te/_slar gzhal yas khang gi 'khor yug tu 'dus nas ro sna tshogs kyi mchod pa byin gyis rlob par gyur to/_/de nas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i bsgom pa bshad pa yin/
[\[10b\]]
[\[10b.1\]]de nas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi/_/yan lag bsgom pa bshad par bya/_/dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i dbus gnas par/_/sa bon bcu bdun gyis gang ba'i/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gnas pa las/_/cung zad tsam zhig bltas nas ni/_/de las 'od zer spro bya ste/_/phyogs
[\[10b.2\]]bcu'i 'jig rten khams kun du/_/rgyal ba kun dang de yi sras/_/rigs sngags rgyal po rgyal mor bcas/_/yi ge'i 'od kyis spyan drangs nas/_/snga ma'i gnas su thim par gyur/_/de yi nyi ma sa bon bcas/_/nyi ma'i nor bu 'bar 'dra ba'i/_/ye shes 'od kyi gong bur gyur/_/
[\[10b.3\]]chos sku dag pa'i rang bzhin du/_/gnyis med ye shes brtan pa las/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyis bskul ba dang /_/snying rje chen po'i mthus bslangs nas/_/gshin rje gshed ni bzhengs par bya/_/sku ni ri sngon 'dra ba 'am/_/yang na char sprin 'dra ba'i mdog_/sngo rang dag
[\[10b.4\]]gam stag zil bzhin/_/yang na las kyi bye brag gis/_/dkar dang dmar dang ser yang rung /_/zhal drug phyag drug zhabs kyang drug_/sbrul gyi rgyan gyis bzhugs pa la/_/stag lpags rlon pa na bzar gsol/_/smin ma spyan dang skra yang ser/_/sen mo spu dang pags
[\[10b.5\]]pa dang /_/lus kyang rdo rje'i rang bzhin can/_/'bar zhing mtshan ma'ang rab 'bar ba/_/be con ral gri dgra sta rnams/_/g.yas pa'i phyag na bsnams pa ste/_/b+han+d+ha sdigs mdzub zhags pa ni/_/g.yon pa'i phyag na bsnams pa la/_/dpa' bo g.yas brkyang stabs kyis
[\[10b.6\]]ni/_/ma he ro dang bcas pa brdzis/_/mi bzad 'bar ba'i skur gyur pa'o/_/yang na zhal gcig phyag gnyis te/_/g.yas pas mtshon cha be con gdengs/_/g.yon pas sdigs mdzub thugs kar 'dzin/_/gang dag phyag bzhi 'dod pa na/_/g.yas na be con ral gri
[\[10b.7\]]ste/_/g.yon na b+han+d+ha zhags pa bsnams/_/'di la sogs pa'i phyag mtshan ni/_/bcu gnyis dag gam bco brgyad dam/_/yang na brgya dang stong dag dang /_/'bum dang bye ba rdul snyed du/_/ji ltar 'dod par bsgom par bya/_/ji ltar 'dod pa de nyid kyis/_/dngos
[\[11a\]]
[\[11a.1\]]grub thob par gdon mi za/_/de nas snying ga'i gnas dag la/_/sa bon bcu bdun gyis gang ba'i/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor snga ma bzhin/_/'dir yang gnas par blta bar bya/_/de nas sa bon yaM yig la/_/sngon bzhin gsang sngags kyis
[\[11a.2\]]bskul bas/_/gshin rje'i dgra ru gyur nas ni/_/slar 'dus thugs kyi rdo rjer gyur/_/sngon po rdo rje mtshon cha can/_/snying ga'i gnas phyogs nyid du ni/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gdan la bzhugs/_/de nas sa bon gyis gang ba'i/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor de nyid kyang /_/
[\[11a.3\]]thugs kyi rdo rje thugs kar gnas/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra ya mA ri/_de nas k+She yi sa bon de/_/snga ma bzhin du sngags kyis bskul/_/rdo rje'i zhing du gyur nas ni/_/dkar po 'khor lo'i mtshon cha can/_/mtshog mar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la/_/sku
[\[11a.4\]]yi rdo rje bzhugs par gyur/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra k+She tra/_de nas sa bon ma las ni/_/rang gi gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_/rdo rje sa zhes bya bar gyur/_/gser 'dra rin chen mtshan ma can/_/lte bar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la/_/mnyam pa'i rdo rje nyid
[\[11a.5\]]du gyur/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra ma hI n+d+ri/_/de nas me zhes bya ba la/_/gsang ba'i sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/rdo rje lhun po zhes byar bshad/_/pad+ma rA ga 'dra ba la/_/me tog pad+ma'i mtshan ma can/_/mgul bar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la/_/gsung gi
[\[11a.6\]]rdo rje nyid du gyur/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra me ru/_de nas sa bon da zhes pa/_/de bzhin gsang ba'i sngags kyis bskul/_/rdo rje sbyin pa zhes byar gyur/_/rin chen margata 'dra ba la/_/ral gri 'bar ba'i mtshon cha can/_/rkang pa g.yas su nyi ma la/_/las kyi
[\[11a.7\]]rdo rje nyid du gyur/_/de la sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra da na/_de nas dza la bltas nas ni/_/rang gi sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/rdo rje 'gro 'dzin zhes byar gyur/_/dkar mo 'khor lo'i mtshon cha can/_/rdo rje zhing gi g.yon phyogs su/_/zla ba'i gdan la gnas nas ni/_/rdo rje
[\[11b\]]
[\[11b.1\]]zhing la gzigs par mdzad/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra dzA gad+d+ha ra/_de nas sa la bltas byas te/_/de bzhin sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/rdo rje kun sdud ces byar gyur/_/bai DU ra rdo rje mtshan ma can/_/rdo rje sa yi g.yon phyogs su/_/zla ba'i gdan la gnas
[\[11b.2\]]nas ni/_/rdo rje sa la gzigs par mdzad/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra saM ha ra Ni/_yi ge do la dmigs byas te/_/de nyid gsang sngags kyis bskul bas/_/rdo rje nyes sel zhes byar gyur/_/dmar mo lag na pad+ma can/_/rdo rje lhun po'i g.yon phyogs su/_/
[\[11b.3\]]zla ba'i gdan la gnas nas ni/_/rdo rje lhun po la gzigs mdzad/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra do ra hi ta/_yi ge ru la dmigs byas te/_/de bzhin sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/rdo rje gnas med ces bya ba/_/ma rgad ut+pal shes rab mtshan/_/rdo rje sbyin
[\[11b.4\]]pa'i g.yon phyogs su/_/zla ba'i gdan la gnas nas ni/_/rdo rje sbyin pa la gzigs mdzad/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra ru ni la/_de nas na la dmigs byas te/_/rang gi sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/rdo rje sna tshogs gzugs su gyur/_/dkar mo lag
[\[11b.5\]]na me long can/_/zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gdan la ni/_/mig gi gnas su bsam par bya/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/badzra Na na rU pa/_yi ge yo la dmigs byas te/_/sngon bzhin gsang ba'i sngags kyis bskul/_/lha mo rdo rje gdangs su gyur/_/dmar mo lag na pi

[\[12a\]]
[\[12a.1\]]can/_/mkhas pas lce yi gnas la bsam/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra rA sa/_de nas yi ge ya la dmigs/_/sngags kyis bskul bas de bzhin du/_/rdo rje zung du gyur nas ni/_/dkar po rdo rje tho ba can/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la

[\[12a.4\]]mkhas pas rkan la bsam par bya/_/de la gsang sngags ni 'di'o/_/oM badzra ni ru ka ti/_yi ge ra la dmigs byas te/_/de bzhin gsang ba'i sngags kyis bskul/_/rdo rje rdul bral zhes bya ba/_/ljang gu lag na ral gri can/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gnas pa/_/

[\[12b\]]
[\[12b.1\]]dang /_/gsar dang rnying dang tshig pa dang /_/dri yang phyogs su ldang bar gyur/_/keng rus dag las me yang 'bar/_/'bu dang sbrang ma mang po dang /_/kang ka rgod dang bya rog dang /_/sha la dga' ba'i 'dab chags kun/_/kun nas za zhing 'thab par byed/_/seng ge stag dang wa dang

[\[12b.3\]]gshin rje gshed la thim par gyur/_/de nas khro bo gshin rje gshed/_/lus ni ri rab lta bu'i tshad/_/sku las khro tshogs rngam pa'i tshogs/_/rgya mtsho'i rlabs bzhin 'phro zhing 'du/_/pho nya mngag gzhug mngag gzhug ma/_/mgyogs shing rab tu mi srun pa/_/go cha sra zhing

[\[13a.1\]]bya/_/sngags pas de tshe bsam pa ni/_/chos kun rang bzhin 'od gsal ba/_/gdod nas dag pa nam mkha' bzhin/_/ming dang mtshan ma bral ba ni/_/blo gros brtan pas bsgom par bya/_/de nas snying rje las byung ba/_/snga ma'i gnas bzhin bsgom bya

[\[13a.3\]]yang na sku dang lhan cig tu/_/mkhas pas rdzogs par bskyed par bya/_/rtog pa gzhan las gsungs pa bzhin/_/gdan la yi ge'am mtshan ma rnams/_/gnyis gnyis dag gam gsum las kyang /_/bskyed kyang nyes par mi 'gyur te/_/dngos grub 'bras bu

[\[13a.6\]]dkyil 'khor dag dang mi ldan zhing /_/ri mo la sogs cho ga dang /_/brtul zhugs drag po med kyang rung /_/legs par bsgom dang bzlas pa dang /_/sbyin sreg 'khor lo'i sbyor ba la/_/sogs pa'i sbyor ba phra mo la/_/brten nas mchod la brtson pa yis/_/las rnams sna

[\[13b.1\]]gdon rnams skrag byed na/_/gang zhig bzlas brjod brtson pa yis/_/gdug pa 'dul ba la sogs pa'i/_/las rnams grub pa smos ci dgos/_/de bas sngags kyi bzlas brjod kyi/_/cho ga tshul bzhin bshad par bya/_/thog mar rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dag_/snga ma bzhin du

[\[13b.3\]]'jig rten khyab par spros byas te/_/rgyal ba sras bcas spyan drangs te/_/gshin rje gshed du gyur nas ni/_/'khor yug yongs su gang bar bsam/_/de nas Na yo ni ra yi/_/yi ge bzhi la dmigs byas te/_/rang rang sngags kyis bskul ba yis/_/gzugs sogs lha mo
[\[13b.4\]]spros nas ni/_/la la gshin rje gshed po yi/_/dbang po rnams la thim par gyur/_/la la phyogs bcu thams cad na/_/mchod pa la sogs cho ga byed/_/la la me tog bdug pa dang /_/mar me dri dang zhal zas dang /_/sil snyan rdzas la thim par gyur/_/spyi ru byin gyis
[\[13b.5\]]brlabs byas nas/_/khyad par dag tu byin brlab par/_/me tog dang ni mar me la/_/gzugs kyi rdo rje thim byas te/_/gzugs kyis khyad par phye bar bya/_/de bzhin bdug pa byug pa la/_/dri yi rdo rjes phye ba yis/_/yon chab bshos dang gtor ma rnams/_/de bzhin ro yi
[\[13b.6\]]rdo rjes phye/_/sil snyan rnam pa sna tshogs ni/_/sgra yi rdo rjes phye ba'o/_/spyi dang bye brag dbye ba yis/_/rdzas dang de bzhin shes bya ste/_/lha mo'i lus nyid phul ba yis/_/reg bya'i mchod par gyur pa'o/_/de ltar ting 'dzin sa bon dang /_/sngags dang rdzas dang ldan pa yis/_/
[\[13b.7\]]gshin rje gshed po mnyes byas te/_/rdo rje dpyod pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/bdag gi lus la 'jug par bya/_/de nas rdo rje'i nges tshig gi_/sbyor bas shin tu brtan par bya/_/rdo rje rdul bral sbyor ba yis/_/shin tu dbang du gyur byas te/_/bzlas pa la ni 'jug par bya/_/de nas
[\[14a\]]
[\[14a.1\]]snying ga'i sa bon rnams/_/rab tu gsal bar dmigs nas ni/_/ji srid brtan par ma gyur tshe/_/gsang sngags spro bar mi bya zhing /_/ting 'dzin 'bad de bzlas pa brtsam/_/gsang sngags yi ge sum cu gnyis/_/thog mar oM dang ldan byas te/_/tha mar
[\[14a.2\]]phaT gnyis ldan byas pa/_/gsang sngags kun gyi rgyal po ste/_/ma yengs pa yi yid kyis bzlas/_/dmigs pa brtan par ma gyur tshe/_/lha dang yi ge zhes bya ba/_/dmigs pa gnyis las ma gtogs pa/_/rtog pa thams cad spang bar bya/_/de ltar ci nus bzlas nas ni/_/
[\[14a.3\]]bzlas pa btong bar 'dod pa na/_/gshin rje gshed po zhes bya ba/_/bdag gi lus las phyung nas ni/_/mdun na dgyes bzhin bzhugs pa la/_/bshags dang smon lam btab byas te/_/de nyid du ni mi snang gyur/_/de nas rang lus la bltas te/_/chos kun skye med dran byas
[\[14a.4\]]nas/_/bdag kyang de bzhin mi snang gyur/_/yang na lha dang mi dbye bar/_/bzod pa yid kyis gsol nas ni/_/lhan cig mi snang gyur par bya/_/de nas stong nyid dran pa yis/_/langs te rang gi spyod lam bya/_/stong nyid blo dang ldan pa na/_/srung ba dag kyang bya mi dgos/_/dngos
[\[14a.5\]]grub dag kyang myur du 'byung /_/byang chub mchog la nye bar 'gyur/_/gal te sngon gyi bag chags kyis/_/tha mal lus su mthong gyur na/_/gsang sngags yi ge bcu bdun po/_/snying ga mtshog ma la sogs par/_/'od 'bar gdan dang bcas pa dang /_/rang rang gnas su
[\[14a.6\]]bsam byas te/_/rdo rje 'bar ba'i mig gis kyang /_/bsrung ba'i bsam pa ldan byas te/_/lus dang gnas dang grogs po dang /_/rdzas la bltas nas bsrung bar 'gyur/_/de ltar nyin re cho ga bzhin/_/yang na dus bzhir sbyor ba bya/_/'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yis/_/gshin rje
[\[14a.7\]]gshed po mnyes par 'gyur/_/de yi bka' nyan thams cad kyang /_/sgrub pa po la dga' bar 'gyur/_/gal te 'chag gam khrus byed dam/_/kha zas za dang nyal ba dang /_/de bzhin spyod lam kun du yang /_/ji srid g.yeng 'gyur thams cad la/_/stong pa nyid dam bsrung ba'i
[\[14b\]]
[\[14b.1\]]shugs/_/nam kyang btang bar mi bya ste/_/shugs btang na ni srung ba nyams/_/gal te shugs dang ldan pa na/_/glo bur yid ni g.yeng gyur kyang /_/srung ba bral ba ma yin no/_/nam zhig yid ni brtan gyur na/_/lha dang yig 'bru gsal ba'i tshe/_/de tshe g.yo ba brtsam par bya/_/
[\[14b.2\]]gal te dngos grub mchog 'dod na/_/'od zer yi ge'am mtshan ma'am/_/sku yi tshul gyis spros byas te/_/rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa kun/_/bsdus nas bdag la thim par bya/_/gal te bsod nams mchog 'dod na/_/khams gsum gnas pa'i sems can kun/_/
[\[14b.3\]]'od zer tshul du bsdus pa ni/_/sangs rgyas kun la thim byas te/_/sku gsum rdo rjer gyur par ni/_/'dod na gnyis ka'ang lhan cig tu/_/'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yis/_/yi dam bcas pa rdzogs par bya/_/gal te sgrub par byed pa ste/_/bzlas pa'i grangs la mos pa na/_/rtog
[\[14b.4\]]pa las gsungs ji bzhin du/_/yi dam bcas pa rdzogs byas pa/_/de nas sgrub la 'jug par bya/_/gal te dus la dga' ba na/_/de bzhin lo grangs ji nus par/_/dam bcas nas ni sgrub la 'jug_/gal te sgrub par byed pa ste/_/shin tu brtson dang ldan pa na/_/mtshan ma
[\[14b.5\]]thob la dam bcas nas/_/ting 'dzin shin tu gsal ba yis/_/mtshan ma thob par gyur pa'am/_/gal te lha yis lung bstan pa/_/rigs pa dang ldan thob pa'am/_/mtshan ma rab 'bring bye brag rnams/_/rtog las gsungs pa ji bzhin du/_/sgrub pa la ni 'jug par bya/_/
[\[14b.6\]]sngags pas bzlas brjod bya ba'i tshul/_/legs par phye ba bshad zin to/_/de nas las rnams sna tshogs kyi/_/dngos grub cho ga bshad par bya/_/thog mar shes rab cho ga ni/_/mdor bsdus nas ni bshad par bya/_/sngags pas bsnyen pa rdzogs byas pas/_/gtsang ma'i
[\[14b.7\]]gnas su song nas ni/_/ras dkar gtsang ma'i gos byas nas/_/rin chen 'bar 'dra'i gnas la 'dug_/khrus kyang legs par byas nas ni/_/mngar gsum ldan pa'i kha zas dang /_/sman dang ldan pa'i mar dag kyang /_/sngags dang ldan pas ci ran bza'/_/mchod pa dag
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]kyang byas nas ni/_/snying gar shes rab 'khor lo dag_/zla ba 'dra dang shel 'dra dang /_/de bzhin nyi ma 'dra yang rung /_/rtsibs bzhi'am yang na rtsibs bcu gnyis/_/bcu drug sum cu gnyis kyang rung /_/de la rang gi sa bon ni/_/gsang sngags yi ge
[\[15a.2\]]sum cu gnyis/_/dkar po cung zad rtsa dmar ba/_/'od dang ldan pa bsgom par bya/_/A li kA li phreng ba yang /_/'khor lo'i tshul du bsgom par bya/_/de yang 'phro dang g.yo ba dang /_/myur du rab tu 'khor ba rnams/_/ci dga' bar ni bsgom par bya/_/de ltar zla drug zla ba gsum/_/
[\[15a.3\]]gcig dang phyed du bsgom byas nams/_/blo gros rab tu rgyas par 'gyur/_/de nas srung ba'i cho ga yang /_/mdor bsdus nas ni bshad par bya/_/shes rab cho ga ji bzhin du/_/sbyor ba legs par byas pa las/_/yi ge ya dang ni bsal nas/_/lhag ma'i yi ge bsgom par bya/_/zla
[\[15a.4\]]ba'i dkyil 'khor 'dra ba yi/_/maN+Dal byas nas de steng du/_/bum pa lnga ni gzhag par bya/_/de bzhin gsang sngags bzlas pa'i mthar/_/che ge mo zhes bya ba la/_/rak+Sha rak+Sha zhes pa dang /_/swA hA ldan pa bzlas pa yi/_/bum pa yis ni spyi bor yang /_/bsrung bar 'dod la dbang
[\[15a.5\]]bskur bya/_/de ltar lan cig lan gsum mam/_/lan bdun gyis ni srung bar 'gyur/_/de nas bshad par bya ba ni/_/'byung chen bzhi yi dkyil 'khor gyis/_/las rnams sna tshogs grub 'gyur ba/_/mdor bsdus nas ni bshad par bya/_/gang zhig dbang du byed 'dod na/_/chu
[\[15a.6\]]bgram dag du song nas ni/_/zla ba phyed pa 'dra ba yi/_/kha dog dmar po'i gnas la 'dug_/zla ba phyed pa'i dus dag la/_/sngags pas sbyor ba brtsom par bya/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya/_/de bzhin mchod pa byas nas ni/_/snying gar ya las byung ba yi/_/rlung gi
[\[15a.7\]]dkyil 'khor bsgom bya ba/_/kha dog sngo la rtsa dmar po/_/de yi steng du pad+ma ni/_/sum cu rtsa gnyis 'dab ldan pa/_/rtse la ba dan g.yo ba dag_/legs par bsam par byas na ni/_/de yi steng du yi ge yang /_/sum cu rtsa gnyis go rims bzhin/_/kha dog dmar skyar bsgom
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]par bya/_/de nas bsgrub bya mdun gnas pa/_/kha dog dmar zhing gos kyang dmar/_/myos bzhin thal mo sbyor byed pa/_/'di ltar bsam pa byas nas ni/_/de nas rang gi yi ge las/_/me tog la ni grub pa'i mda'/_/rlung gi shugs kyis 'phangs nas ni/_/bsgrub bya'i dpral ba
[\[15b.2\]]mgul ba dang /_/snying ga lte ba gsang gnas su/_/rgyun mi 'chad par phog par bsam/_/bud med la ni khyad par du/_/gsang ba'i gnas la phog par bsam/_/'di ltar sbyor ba brtan pa yis/_/brgya byin dbang chen grags pa yang /_/de la dga' zhing dbang du gyur/_/de
[\[15b.3\]]bzhin lha dang bdud la sogs/_/bram ze rgyal po blon por bcas/_/kun nas dbang du byed par 'gyur/_/lha mo'am ni gnod sbyin mo/_/mngon par shes pa ldan pa dag_/dbang du bya ba sgrub pa ni/_/ring por mi thogs 'grub par 'gyur/_/mthu chen bsgrub par dka' ba dang /_/
[\[15b.4\]]rang gi 'dod pa mi ldan dang /_/rags las grub pa'i gzugs can dang /_/mngon par shes pa mi ldan pa/_/dbang du bya bar dka' bar bshad/_/lha mo gnod sbyin mo la sogs/_/phra ba'i lus can mngon shes ldan/_/rang gi 'dod pa ldan pa dang /_/mthu che ba yang dbang 'gyur
[\[15b.5\]]bar/_/rab tu dka' ba ma yin no/_/gal te bsgrub par bya ba dag_/sngags pas dgug par 'dod pa ni/_/sbyor ba de nyid bsgom byas te/_/lcags kyu rlung dang ldan pa dag_/sa bon rnams las nges spros te/_/bsgrub par bya ba'i snying ga nas/_/drangs te dgug pa'i sbyor ba bya/_/
[\[15b.6\]]gal te bskrad par 'dod na yang /_/sbyor ba de nyid bsgom byas te/_/rlung dang ldan pa'i rnga mo dag_/rab tu gnag cing mgyogs pa ni/_/rang gis bon gnas las 'thon/_/de la bsgrub bya bskyon byas te/_/myur du lho phyogs bda' bar bya/_/gal te dbye bar 'dod pa na/_/sbyor ba de nyid
[\[15b.7\]]bsgom byas te/_/sbrul dang ne'u le mang po dag_/rang gi sa bon gnas las 'thon/_/de dag bsgrub bya gnyi ga yi/_/so sor lus la zhugs par bya/_/de nas bsgrub bya de dag kyang /_/sbrul dang sre mo'i rang bzhin du/_/gyur nas phan tshun 'thab par bsam/_/sbyor ba 'di ni
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]brtan pa yis/_/bsgrub bya dbye zhing 'thab par 'gyur/_/de nas bsgrub par bya ba dag_/gnon cing rmongs par byed 'dod na/_/rdo rje dkyil 'khor bsgoms pa yi/_/snying gar sa yi dkyil 'khor ni/_/gru bzhi ser po ma las byung /_/de steng sna tshogs rdo rje
[\[16a.2\]]ni/_/rtse mo sum cu gnyis dang ldan/_/de la rang gi sa bon yang /_/kha dog ser po ldan pa dag_/sum cu rtsa gnyis tshang bar bsgom/_/de nas de 'dra spro bya ste/_/bsgrub bya gang na gnas pa yi/_/steng du yang dang yang mnan na/_/skye 'gro mnan cing rmongs par 'gyur/_/gal te
[\[16a.3\]]rgyas par byed 'dod na/_/sbyor ba de nyid bsgom pa las/_/de las cung zad mi 'dra ba/_/rdo rje gnas su rin chen bsgom/_/de la 'od zer 'phro ba yis/_/rin chen lta bus 'od zer dag_/bsgrub bya la ni thim pa yis/_/bsod nams yongs su rgyas par bya/_/gzhan yang drag
[\[16a.4\]]po'i sbyor ba la/_/me yi dkyil 'khor ra las byung /_/rdo rje rtse gsum 'od 'bar ba/_/rang gi yi ges mtshan pa yis/_/rdo rje me ltar 'phro ba dag_/gang dang gang du bsams pa der/_/gsad pa'i las la sngags pa yin/_/gzhan yang zhi bar bya 'dod na/_/chu yi dkyil 'khor
[\[16a.5\]]dza las byung /_/zlum zhing dkar la bum pa ni/_/shel dang 'dra ba nyi shus brgyan/_/de yi nang du yi ge'i tshogs/_/ya ni gsal ba nyi shu bsam/_/yi ge dag la bdud rtsi chu/_/'dzags pas bum pa gang bar bsam/_/de nas ma rungs bgegs la sogs/_/rab tu
[\[16a.6\]]gdug pa'i sems ldan la/_/de la bdud rtsi 'od zer dag_/kun nas thim par gyur pa yis/_/gdug pa'i tshogs ni zhi bar 'gyur/_/'byung chen bzhi yi dkyil 'khor gyi/_/ting nge 'dzin gyi sbyor ba yis/_/las kyi sbyor ba gang sgrub pa/_/so sor phye ste bshad pa yin/_/bsgom
[\[16a.7\]]pa dang ni bzlas ba dag_/gal te 'bad nas byas pa yang /_/skal dang mos pa dman pa yis/_/las rnams grub par ma gyur ba'i/_/sgrub pa po la phan gdags phyir/_/sbyor ba la ni brten par bshad/_/sangs rgyas bstan la gnod byed pa'i/_/rgyal po ngan pa byung
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]gyur tam/_/blon po la sogs de bzhin te/_/skye bo ngan pa'i tshogs byung nas/_/thabs gzhan dag gis ma dul na/_/bstan pa yongs su bsrung ba'i phyir/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi bka' bzhin du/_/byang chub sems dang ldan byas te/_/de tshe drag po'i sbyor ba brtsam/_/
[\[16b.2\]]gdug pa gzhig par bya ba'i thabs/_/drag po'i sbyor ba gang gsungs pa/_/rgyal ba'i bka' nyid bsrung ba'i phyir/_/mdor bsdus nas ni bshad par bya/_/sbu gu rig par bya ba dang /_/gnad kyi gnas rnams gzir ba dang /_/byug dang gtor ba la sogs kyis/_/rul sogs
[\[16b.3\]]ma rungs bya ba dang /_/bskam zhing sreg pa'i cho ga dang /_/lus kun yongs su gzhom pa dang /_/byad kyis phog par bya ba dang /_/'khrugs shing myos par 'gyur ba yis/_/gdug pa brlag par 'gyur ba yi/_/cho ga mdor bsdus 'di zhes bya/_/de la sbu gu rig pa yi/_/
[\[16b.4\]]cho ga dag kyang bshad par bya/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bsgom byas te/_/srog dang yi ge gnyis med par/_/kha dog lnga ru gyur byas te/_/sbrang bu trai la'i mchu 'dra ba/_/bdag gi sna nas dbyung bar bya/_/bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i pad+ma las/_/skud pa 'dra ba'i sbu gu nas/_/srog gi yi ge
[\[16b.5\]]drang bar bya/_/de nas bsgrub bya'i rdul dag dang /_/rjes dang dri ma sna tshogs dang /_/grog mkhar sa sogs sbyar byas te/_/kha sbyar ldan pa'i gzugs brnyan bya/_/gzhan yang chu'am dur khrod dam/_/'byung po gnas pa'i sa dag las/_/klu 'am sa yi bdag po 'am/_/ma mo'i
[\[16b.6\]]tshogs sam 'byung po dag_/kha dog bzhir ldan gzugs byas te/_/rang rang gnas su sbas byas nas/_/chu yi hom dang de bzhin du/_/sa dang me yi hom dag gis/_/tshim par byas nas des gzung 'gyur/_/de la sbu gu rig pa'i thabs kyi cho ga ni 'di yin te/_thog ma nyid sbu
[\[16b.7\]]gu rig pa'i cho ga gang gis bsgrub bya klu yis zin par 'gyur ba'i thabs kyi cho ga bshad par bya'o/_/de la dang por sngags pas rdo rje dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du bsgoms te/_rang gi snying gar yi ge'i tshogs ji lta ba bzhin du bsgoms pa dag srog ces bya ba'i rlung dang 'dres par
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]gyur bas 'od zer kha dog lnga pa'am bzhi pa sbrang bu trai la'i mchu ltar bcud thams cad 'byin par nus pa rab tu rno ba gdug pa sna'i bu ga gnyis nas byung bar bsam mo/_/de bzhin du dmigs pa byas pas rang gi snas de'i reg pa myong bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas
[\[17a.2\]]ting nge 'dzin de dbang du gyur na ni dang por rdzi rno bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas dbugs rngub cing drangs pas gzhan gyi ro dag kyang nyams su myong bar 'gyur ro/_/de nas ting nge 'dzin de shin tu dbang du gyur na ni bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i gnas na pad+ma kha sbyor gyi dbus srog gnas pa'i rtsa skud pa 'dra ba
[\[17a.3\]]'dus pa'i rtsa na srog gi rang bzhin yi ge a'i dbyibs su gnas pa ni rtsa kha dog dmar skyar gnas pa zhig yod de/_de bzhin du gsal bar bsgoms nas de nas bdag gi sna nas dbugs kyi 'od zer rab tu rno ba de dag phyung ste bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i ba spu'i bu ga nas zhugs nas/
[\[17a.4\]]sbu gu skud pa 'dra ba'i nang du zhugs te srog gi rang bzhin gyi yi ge la zug nas/_yi ge de dag thams cad gzhibs te/_yi ge nyid kyang blangs nas drangs pas/_dper na pags pa rlon pa las byas pa'i snod zhabs nas thon nas slog pa bzhin du srog gi gnas pad+ma kha sbyar te nang
[\[17a.5\]]phyir bzlog par gyur par byas nas rab tu drangs par byas na sbyor ba de 'ba' zhig gis kyang gang su yang rung ste de 'chi bar 'gyur ro/_/ting nge 'dzin ma thob pa rnams kyis ni sbyor ba dang bcas pa brtsam par mi bya ste/_thog ma nyid du ting nge 'dzin de nyid kyang 'bad pas goms par
[\[17a.6\]]byas nas gsang sngags kyi bzlas brjod kyang byas la/_de nas bsgrub bya de'i rkang rjes kyi sa dang /_phyi sa che chung gi rjes dag dang /_gzhan yang mchil ma dang skra dang gos kyi dum bu dag dang /_gzhan yang de'i khyim gyi sa dang /_/them pa rtsa'i sa dag ji ltar rnyed pa blangs te/
[\[17a.7\]]grog mkhar gyi sa dang /_'bru sna tshogs kyi phye dang /_sa bzang po gzhan dag dang sbyar te legs par btags nas bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan sor brgyad pa zhig bya'o/_/de nas gro ga 'am/_'dab ma gang yang rung ba la pad+ma kha sbyor dong tse tsam gyi dbus su/_a dmar pos
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]mtshan pa kha dog dmar po zhig bya'o/_/de nas tshon sna lnga 'am/_sna bzhi'i skud pa mtho do pa'i tshad bya ste de dag gi rtse mo gcig tu bsgril nas zangs kyi sbu gu sog ma'i mgrin pa tsam zhig byas te/_de'i nang nas skud pa de dag phyung nas pad+ma kha sbyor gyi snying po'i yi ge a la phug ste _
[\[17b.2\]]gdags par bya'o/_/de nas pad+ma de bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan gyi lte ba'i dkyil du lus ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du gzhug par bya'o/_/zangs kyi sbu gu de yang lte ba la zug par gzir bar bya'o/_/de nas gzugs brnyan de ba lang gi pags pa zhig tu dril te skud pa de dag phyir
[\[17b.3\]]phyung nas de cung zad bskam par bya'o/_/de nas bskams par gyur pa dang gzugs brnyan de khyer te bsgrub bya'i khang pa mthong ba'i sa phyogs bsgrub bya'i khang pa la zug pa'i lam yod pa zhig tu dong brkos te de'i nang du sbas nas sa skam pos bkang ste gzhag go/_/de nas rang gi
[\[17b.4\]]khyim du 'ongs te ting nge 'dzin snga ma bzhin du bsgrub bya'i srog rengs nas gzugs brnyan la thim par bya'o/_/de ltar sbyor ba 'di zhag gcig gam gnyis sam gsum du byas nas/_de nas sgrub pa pos dgug pa'i sbyor ba ji ltar nus pa byas te/_sgrub pa'i grogs mchog dag gis
[\[17b.5\]]lha'i ting nge 'dzin dang ldan pas lha'i cha lugs bzung ste/_bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan blangs la rang gi gnas su 'ong bar bya'o/_/de nas stegs bu'i steng du btsag gam rdo rgyus sam sol ba dag gis rlung gi dkyil 'khor zla gam bsgrub bya'i phyogs su blta ba zhags pa dang lcags
[\[17b.6\]]kyu mang pos mtshan pa zhig bris la/_de'i steng du bzhag la zhag bdun gyi bar du dgug pa'i sbyor ba bya zhing gzugs brnyan la bstims te/_skud pa nag po la rang gi gsang sngags bzlas pas shin tu bsdams par bsam zhing /_tshon skud lag pas bzung ste bzlas pa la brtson
[\[17b.7\]]par bya'o/_/de nas zhag bdun lon pa dang rgya mtsho'i sa'am/_de bzhin du chu chen po'i 'gram dang /_lteng ka dang rdzing chen po dang /_chu mig sna tshogs nas sa dang chu blangs te/_de nas sa de dag dang /_sman dang spos dang /_me tog bzang po dag dang legs par btags te 'bras
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]sam gro'i phye ma dag dang yang sbyar nas klu chen po'i gzugs byas nas/_'di ltar sbrul rab tu 'bar ba'i kha gdangs pa bzhi byas te/_de dag gi snying gar oM phu zhes bya ba'i snying po bris la gzhug go/_/khar khaM nag po bris la gzhug_/sbrul de dag
[\[18a.2\]]kyang gtsug na nor bu yod pa lce gnyis pa so phreng ba 'dra bar gnas pa'o/_/kha dog ni dang por gu gul dkar po dang ba'i mar bsres te bskol nas byug par bya'o/_/de nas tshon sna bzhis kha dog bsgyur bar bya ste/_gcig ni dkar po'o/_/gcig ni ser po'o/_/gcig ni dmar
[\[18a.3\]]po'o/_/gcig ni nag po'o/_/de dag gi lce gnyis gnyis po de dag kyang tshon skud legs par bsgril ba mtho re ba gnyis gnyis la/_oM pa na nA ga bi Sha khaM/_zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags bzlas te rtsa ba sbrul gyi khar bcug la/_dug 'bar ba'i lcer gyur par bsam par bya'o/_/
[\[18a.4\]]de nas sa phyogs gtsang ma zhig tu ras sam gos gtsang ma'i gur phub la/_der maN+Dal ba'i rnam lnga dang ldan pa zhig byas te/_der pad+ma 'dab ma bzhi pa zhig bris nas ge sar sngon por byas nas de'i steng du bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed po nyid khams gsum rnam par
[\[18a.5\]]rgyal ba'i gzugs su gzhag par bya'o/_/shar phyogs kyi 'dab ma dkar por bya ste/_der sbrul dkar po gzhag go/_/de bzhin du lho ser por bya ste/_sbrul ser po gzhag go/_/nub kyi dmar por bya ste sbrul dmar po gzhag go/_/byang gi nag por byas te sbrul nag po
[\[18a.6\]]gzhag go/_/sbrul de dag kyang mgo dbus su blta bar bya'o/_/de nas sngags pa bdag nyid khrus legs par byas nas gos gtsang ma bgos te lag pa dri bzang pos byugs nas nub phyogs kyi sgor 'dug ste/_rang gi lha'i ting nge 'dzin du zhugs nas/_maN+Dal gyi dbus su
[\[18a.7\]]bcom ldan 'das spyan drangs te/_legs par bsams nas/_ar+g+ha dang me tog la sogs pa'i mchod pas mnyes par bya'o/_/de nas sbrul chen po bzhi'i mdun du sa las byas pa'i snod gtsang ma bzhi'i nang du rgya mtsho'i chu la sogs pa chu sna tshogs dang /_ba'i 'o ma
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]dang /_/me tog dri nga ba med pa rnams blugs te bzhag la/_der chu'i hom byas te klu rnams tshim par bya'o/_/de la chu'i hom bya ba'i cho ga ni 'di lta ste/_de lta bu'i chu'i gzhi bshams nas gzhan yang mchod pa'i rdzas su gyur pa/_ba las byung ba'i dkar gsum dang /_mngar
[\[18b.2\]]gsum dang /_khre dkar po dang /_til dkar po dang /_'bras dkar po la sogs pa 'bru kha dog dkar po sna tshogs dang /_rin po che sna tshogs dang /_ga pur dang tsan+dan dkar po la sogs te spos dang sman sna tshogs dang /_gzhan yang chu dag dkar po la sogs pa de dag
[\[18b.3\]]dang mthun pa'i rdzas ji snyed pa dang /_me tog dri nga ba med pa rnams dang /_'o ma dang 'bras chan dang /_sha kha ra gsum du sbyar ba'i kha zas kyang gzhag par bya'o/_/de nas sngags pa lha'i nga rgyal dang ldan pas snod kyi chu rnams kyi nang du yi ge pa las byung ba'i pad+ma'i steng du/_yang yi ge pa rang
[\[18b.4\]]rang gi kha dog can bsams pa las de yongs su gyur pa'i chu lha rang rang gi mdog can/_sbrul mgo'i gdengs ka dang ldan pa/_lag na zhags pa dang ut+pal bsnams pa re re bsam par bya'o/_/de nas bdag gi snying ga nas so so'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i 'od zer 'phros pas/
[\[18b.5\]]phyogs bzhi nas chu'i lha tshul snga ma dang mthun pa dag spyan drangs par bsam zhing /_oM ba ru Na de ba dAd+ta A kaR+Sha ya dzaH_hUM baM hoH/_zhes brjod nas/_mchod snod du me tog gtor nas/_chu lha de dag sngar bsams pa'i chu lha dang gnyis su med par gyur nas 'o ma'i rgya mtsho'i nang du pad+ma'i
[\[18b.6\]]gdan la bzhugs par bsam mo/_/de nas dri bzang po'i spos rnams bsregs pa yang phyogs bzhir btang /_ba'i mar sar las byas pa'i mar me yang phyogs bzhir bltams te/_tsan+dan dkar po dang sbyar ba'i dri chab kyang phyogs kun du gtor nas/_de nas dang por me tog gtor
[\[18b.7\]]te/_/oM ba ru Na de ba dA t+tA ya swA hA/_zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis phul bas/_'o ma'i rgya mtsho la me tog gi tshal chen po chags par bsam mo/_/gsang sngags de nyid kyis spos phul bas/_gnas der rin po che'i rang bzhin gyi sprin chags par bsam mo/_/de nas gsang
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]sngags de nyid kyis byugs la gtor te/_sprin de las bdud rtsi'i char bab pas/_de dag shin tu dga' ba dang rangs pa skyes par bsam mo/_/de bzhin du mar me phul bas spyi bo la yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che 'od 'bar ba gnas par gyur te/_nam mkha'
[\[19a.2\]]lding gi 'jigs pa dang bral bar bsam mo/_/de bzhin du dkar gsum dang /_mngar gsum la sogs pa'i rdzas rnams la gsang sngags de nyid kyis phul bas/_rang rang gi rdzas dang mthun pa'i 'dod pa'i yon tan gyi tshogs su gyur te mnyes par gyur par bsam mo/_/de
[\[19a.3\]]nas me tog chu la gtor te/_chu'i lha chen po khyod mkhyen par mdzod cig_/chu thams cad khyed kyi rang bzhin lags te/_bdag gis chu la ci mchod pa thams cad khyed kyi 'khor du bcas pa thams cad mnyes par gyur nas/_bdag cag la yang dgyes shing dngos grub
[\[19a.4\]]gsol bar mdzod cig ces brjod do/_/de nas yang rang gi snying ga nas ye shes kyi 'od zer 'phros pas phyogs bzhi nas klu'i tshogs bkug ste/_de yang shar phyogs su rgyal po phru gu 'dra ba kha dog dkar po pho dang mo'i cha byad 'dzin pa mang po 'dus par 'gyur bar bsam mo/_/de
[\[19a.5\]]bzhin du lho phyogs su ni kha dog ser skya bram ze'i cha byad can no/_/nub phyogs su ni kha dog dmar skya byis pa gzhon nu'i cha byad can no/_/byang phyogs su ni dud 'gro'i cha byad can de 'di ltar sbrul nag po dang sbal pa nag po dang /_glang nag po la sogs pa 'dus par bsam zhing /_oM
[\[19a.6\]]sarba pan nA ga phuH/_phuH/_A kaR+Sha ya dzaHhUM baM hoH/_zhes brjod cing lag pa thal mo sbyar ba las gung mo gnyis gshibs te bsgreng /_lhag ma phyir bkyed de ut+pal ltar byas pa 'di ni klu thams cad dga' bar byed pa'i dam tshig gi phyag rgya ste/_'dis spyan drangs pas
[\[19a.7\]]phyogs bzhi'i 'o ma'i mtsho chen po bzhi'i nang du 'dus par bsam mo/_/de nas de dag chu lha dang rang bzhin gcig par yang gyur cing 'khor dang gtso bo'i tshul du 'dug par yang dmigs la/_dri chab kyis gtor te phyogs shin tu gtsang bar gyur par bsams la/_de nas chu lha
[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]mchod pa'i rim pa ji lta ba bzhin du mchod par bya zhing phyag rgya de nyid dang ldan pas/_oM sarba pan nA ga phuH/_phuH/_sarba pU dza me g+ha sa ma ye swA hA/_zhes brjod cing sngon du brjod pa'i bsam rgyud dang ldan pas mnyes par 'gyur bar bya'o/_/de nas gshegs su mi gsol bar/_de
[\[19b.2\]]bzhin du zhag_gsum mam lnga'am bdun gyi bar du byas la/_de nas sgrub pa'i grogs mchog zhig gis sngon gyi rang gi gnas su song ste/_gro ga'am shog bu la bsgrub bya'i ming rus bri bar bya'o/_/'di ltar yul che ge mo na gnas pa'i mi che ge mo zhes bya ba 'di/_rang bzhin
[\[19b.3\]]ngan pa bstan pa la gnod pa nga rgyal can zhig ste/_sngon yang 'dis bdag cag la bar chad byas/_/da ltar yang bdag cag klu chen po khyed rnams mchod pa la bar chad byed de/_'di ni bdag cag la brnyas par ma zad kyi/_/khyed cag lta bu mthu dang ldan pa rnams la yang brnyas
[\[19b.4\]]par byed khyad du gsod par byed 'tshe bar byed pas/_de bas na mi 'di khyed rnams kyis gzung bar rigs so zhes bya ba bris la zangs sam lcags kyi sbu gu zhig la dril te skud pa nag pos dkris nas/_de nas gu gul nag po dang rgya skyegs su sbyar ba'i me la bzhu bas dril te/_bsgrub bya'i tshon skud
[\[19b.5\]]la gzhug par bya'o/_/de nas gzugs brnyan de blangs nas klu mchod pa'i gnas su khyer te maN+Dal gyi lho phyogs su bzhag nas/_sgrub pa po dang grogs mchog rnams kyis me tog mang po thogs te/_mchod snod dang phyogs thams cad du gtor la thal mo sbyar te/_sngon du bris pa'i tshig
[\[19b.6\]]snga ma de lan bdun nam/_nyi shu rtsa gcig gi bar du brjod par bya'o/_/de nas chu de dag snod gtsang ma cig gi nang du bsdus la sbrul de rnams kyang rim pa bzhin du phyogs gcig nas bsdus nas/_sbrul gyi lce'i tshon skud re re dang /_bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i tshon skud re re kha dog mthun par sbrel te/
[\[19b.7\]]de nas snod bzang po sbrul gyi gzugs brnyan chag par mi 'gyur ba zhig gi nang du bcug ste/_klu chen po ma rungs pa zhig yod pa'i sa phyogs zhig tu khyer te dong khru gang tsam pa gnyis brus nas de'i bar yang 'brel mar brus te/_bsgrub bya'i ngos su bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan gzhag_/
[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]gcig tu sbrul gyi gzugs brnyan bcug ste/_der chu yang blugs te legs par kha bcad la sbas te gzhag_/de nas de phan chad sa phyogs der song ste sbrul gyis phyogs kyi steng du snod gtsang ma'i nang du snga ma bzhin du chu'i hom byas te/_snga ma'i tshig gis de
[\[20a.2\]]bzhin du bsgo ba byas nas klu rnams ni phra ma la dga' ba dang /_sngon du 'dris pa gtsor byed pa yin pas bsgrub bya de dag klu rnams kyis 'dzin par 'gyur ro/_/de yang sgrub pa po rab rnams kyis ni rjes su bskul bas zhag bdun byas pas 'dzin par 'gyur ro/_/tha ma rnams kyis kyang
[\[20a.3\]]rjes su bskul ba zla ba drug byas pas 'dzin par 'gyur ro/_/sngon du gtang pa'i cho ga ni bye brag med do/_/sbu gu rig par bya ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga las bsgrub bya klu'i gdon gyis zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba rdzogs so//_//da ni sbu gu rig par bya ba'i thabs kyi cho ga las/_bsgrub bya sa'i
[\[20a.4\]]bdag pos zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba bshad de/_de la thog mar sngon du brjod pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang ldan pas bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan snga ma bzhin du bya'o/_/de las cung zad bye brag tu na bsgrub bya'i khang pa las sa blangs te/_grog mkhar gyi sa dang sa gzhan du yang sbyar nas/_bsgrub bya'i
[\[20a.5\]]khang pa'i gzugs brnyan sor bcu drug pa chu zheng gab pa zhig bya'o/_/gzugs brnyan de gnyis ka la yang srog chags skye bas thob pa'i dgrar gyur pa rnams las mthu rtsal chung ba rnams kyi spu rnams ji ltar rnyed pa blangs te sbyar bar bya'o/_/de nas bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan de'i snying
[\[20a.6\]]gar bsgrub bya skyes pa dang bud med dang khye'u dang bu mo la sogs pa 'khor dang bcas pa'i ming dang rus dag bris te gzhug par bya'o/_/de nas bsgrub bya de khang pa'i dkyil du gzhug par bya'o/_/khang pa de yang glo skar bzhi dang bcas pa mda' yab dang bcas par bya'o/_/sgo ngos kyi glo skar gyi nang
[\[20a.7\]]nas lte ba'i tshon skud drangs te/_snga ma bzhin du rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyi steng du bzhag nas/_bsgrub bya dgug pa'i sbyor ba yang nas yang du bya'o/_/de'i tshe sa'i bdag po ma rungs pa gnas pa'i gnas sna tshogs nas sa blangs la cha gsum du bcad de/_cha gcig dang sa bzang po
[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]gzhan du sbyar nas bum pa bzang po khru gang ba'i tshad tsam zhig bya'o/_/cha gcig las sdig pa'i gzugs brnyan khru gang gi tshad tsam zhig byas te/_de yang sa bzang po gzhan dang grog mkhar gyi dang yang sbyar bar bya'o/_/cha gcig las dum bu gsum du bgos te/_dum bu gcig las
[\[20b.2\]]phag gi gzugs brnyan bya'o/_/dum bu gcig las bud med skra lhug par bshig pa zhig gi gzugs brnyan bya'o/_/dum bu gcig ni sa nyid du gzhag go/_/de la bum pa ni kha dog ser por bya'o/_/sdig pa ni nag po la sngon po'i thig le can du bya'o/_/phag ni ser po la nag po'i thig le
[\[20b.3\]]can du bya'o/_/bud med ni ser po la sngon po'i thig le can du bya'o/_/de nas phag dang bud med kyi gzugs gnyis bum pa'i nang du gzhag go/_/gzugs brnyan gsum po de dag la yang srog chags skye bas thob pa dang nang mi mthun pa rnams las gnyen por gyur pa rnams kyi sbu ji ltar rnyed pa
[\[20b.4\]]dang yang ldan par bya'o/_/gzhan yang 'byung khungs sna tshogs pa 'di lta ste/_gser gyi 'byung khungs kyi sa dang /_gser dang de bzhin du dngul dang /_zangs dang lcags la sogs pa rnams kyi 'byung khungs kyi sa dang /_de dag gi rgyu rdo nyid dang /_sngar gyi sa'i dum bu gcig bzhag pa rnams legs
[\[20b.5\]]par btags te/_de'i nang du byu ru dang shel dang dung la sogs te rin po che sna tshogs ji ltar rnyed pa dang sbyar nas bum pa'i nang du blugs par bya'o/_/de nas rang gi gnas nas mi mthong ba'i sa phyogs shig tu dong zhig brkos te/_der bum pa de bcug nas de'i mdun du sdig pa'i gzugs bzhag ste/_
[\[20b.6\]]bum pa dang mnyam pa tsam du dong de kha gcad par bya'o/_/de'i steng du maN+Dal pad+ma dang 'dra ba byas nas/_dbus kyi snying po kha cung zad tsam phye ste/_bum pa'i nang snang bar gyur pa tsam du bya'o/_/de'i steng du gur nag po zhig phub ste der 'dug nas/_sa'i hom gyi sa'i bdag po rnams tshim par bya'o/_/
[\[20b.7\]]de'i cho ga 'di yin te/_mchod pa'i rdzas sngon du brjod pa rnams dang /_khyad par du yang rin po che sna tshogs 'byung khungs kyi rdo rnams dang sbyar ba dang /_'bru sna tshogs dang gos kha dog mi mthun pa sna tshogs pa bsag par bya'o/_/de nas sngags pa bdag nyid shar phyogs su 'dug ste/_dri sna tshogs
[\[21a\]]
[\[21a.1\]]kyis lag pa byugs/_kha dog sna tshogs kyi gos gyon nas rang gi lha'i ting nge 'dzin bsgom par bya'o/_/de nas bum pa'i nang du yi ge ba kha dog ser po zhig las sa'i bdag po phag chen po zhes bya ba phag ser khra la zhon pa/_kha dog ser khra phag gi mgo can lag na
[\[21a.2\]]lcags kyu dang phag gi mche ba thogs pa bsam mo/_/de'i g.yon ngos su yang sa'i bdag mo pad+ma li zhes bya ba/_mdog dmar ser la ris bkra ba lag na gser gyi bum pa thogs pa zhig bsam mo/_/de dag gi mdun du dus thams cad kyi srung ma br-its+tshi ka zhes bya ba/_lus lcags kyi
[\[21a.3\]]sdig pa chen po rwa dang yan lag dang mjug ma rnams kyang gnam lcags 'bar ba las grub pa rno ba gdug pa sa thams cad bdag gir byed cing srung ba zhig yi ger bris la bsam par bya'o/_/de nas bdag gi ye shes kyi 'od zer 'og gi phyogs su 'phros pas/_'og gi phyogs nas
[\[21a.4\]]sa'i bdag po rnams ji ltar bsams pa de 'dra ba spyan drangs par bsam zhing /_oM b+hu a d+hi pa ti ma hA bA rA hA pad+ma mA li ni tsa A kaR+Sha ya dzaH_hUM baM hoH/_zhes brjod cing /_lcags kyu'am bum pa'i phyag rgya bcas te spyan drangs pas/_sngar bskyed pa dang gnyis su med par 'gyur bar
[\[21a.5\]]bsam mo/_/de nas ar+g+ha la sogs pa mchod pa'i rdzas rnams la bum pa'i phyag rgyas bzung ste/_gsang sngags gong ma nyid las/_A kaR+Sha ya/_la sogs pa'i gnas su ma hA pU dza me g+ha sa ma ye swA hA/_zhes bya ba'i gsang sngags kyis bskul bar bya'o/_/de ltar mchod pas bum
[\[21a.6\]]pa de nyid rin po che gter gyi sa gzhi chen po la/_'dod pa'i yon tan sna tshogs kyis phun sum tshogs par ldan pa'i gnas na/_sa'i bdag po rnams shin tu longs spyod par bsam mo/_/'di ltar zhag gsum mam lnga'am bdun gyi bar du byas na de nas bum pa dang sdig pa'i gzugs su
[\[21a.7\]]bcas pa de nas blangs te/_sngon gyi bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan dang bcas pa khyer nas/_sa bdag ma rungs pa yod pa'i gnas shig tu dong ring po brus te/_dang por bum pa bcug la bum pa dang mnyam po tsam du sas legs par dgang bar bya'o/_/de'i steng du sdig pa'i gzugs bsgrub bya'i
[\[21b\]]
[\[21b.1\]]yul phyogs su kha bstan te bzhag la/_de'i rwa bar du bsgrub bya mkhar dang bcas pa bcug nas/_bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i tshon skud rnams sdig pa'i khar bcug ste gzhag go/_/de'i bar du bsgrub bya'i pha dang ma dang mes po la sogs pa rnams kyi ming dang rus pa la sogs pa rnyed kyang rung /_de dag
[\[21b.2\]]ras kyi nang du dril te/_che ge mo rnams kyi gnas rtag tu 'dir 'cha' ba yin no zhes bya ba'i yi ge yang bris la de dag de'i rwa bar du lhan cig tu bcug ste/_legs par sbas te gzhag par bya'o/_/de nas rang gis khyim du 'ongs te srog chags skye bas thob pa'i nang mi mthun pa gnyis
[\[21b.3\]]kyi gzugs kha sprod du bris te/_de'i bar du thab khung gcan gzan khro bo'i kha 'dra ba byas nas/_de'i nang du shing rtsub pa brdzangs te mi nang mi mthun pa gnyis kyi khyim nas me blangs nas/_srog chags skye bas thob pa'i nang mi mthun pa rnams kyi sha dang khrag dang rus pa dang /_spu dang pags pa
[\[21b.4\]]rnams la rtsa ba'i sngags bskul ba dang bcas pa bzlas shing sbyin sreg byas na/_snying stobs can kha cig gis zhag bdun rjes su bskul bas bsgrub bya sa'i bdag pos gzung bar 'gyur ro/_/tha ma yang zla ba drug rjes su bskul ba byas pas de bzhin du gzung bar 'gyur ro/_/de la bskul ba'i
[\[21b.5\]]sngags ni 'di yin te/_che ge mo dang sa bdag rnams de sha ya dzu da ya phaT ces bya ba 'di rtsa ba'i sngags kyi rjes su bskul bas/_de dag shin tu 'khrug pas 'thab par bsam par bya'o/_/sbu gu rig par bya ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga las/_bsgrub bya sa'i bdag pos zin par bya ba zhes bya ba'i sbyor ba
[\[21b.6\]]bstan pa rdzogs so//_//da ni sbu gu rig par bya ba'i cho ga las/_bsgrub bya ma mo'i gdon gyis zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba bshad par bya ste/_dang po nyid du gang yang rung ba'i gnas su rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du bsgoms nas rtsa ba'i gsang sngags bzlas brjod byed cing sems
[\[21b.7\]]brtan par gyur par bya'o/_/de nas ma mo'i gnas su song nas/_thab khung zla gam du shing dmar po la me sbar te rdzas kha dog dmar po rnams kyis nyi ma re re sbyin sreg brgya rtsa brgyad bya'o/_/de ltar nyi ma brgya rtsa brgyad kyi bar du byas nas/_de nas bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan snga ma bzhin du
[\[22a\]]
[\[22a.1\]]byas te/_gro ga 'am shog shog la bud med kyi gzugs khros pa/_kha dog dkar po dang /_dmar po dang /_ser po dang /_nag po dang bzhi byas la lte ba'i tshon skud dang /_kha dog mthun par gu gul gyis bud med kyi kha dang sbyar te gzhag go/_/de nas bud med kyi
[\[22a.2\]]thod pa bkra mi shis pa zhig gi nang du bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan bcug ste/_de'i steng nas bud med kyi gzugs brnyan bzhag nas/_dug sna tshogs dang khrag kyang blugs par bya'o/_/skye tshe'am yungs kar nag la rtsa ba'i sngags bskul ba dang bcas pa ci nus bzlas te yang blugs par bya'o/_/de
[\[22a.3\]]nas rdo leb la rdo rje rgya gram bris pas kha bcad nas legs par sbas te/_de'i steng du thab khung gru gsum du 'dug pa'i shing las me sbar la/_sha sna tshogs kyi sbyin sreg nyi ma nyi shu rtsa gcig tu bya'o/_/de nas sha chen po'i sbyin sreg nyi ma bdun du bya'o/_/gsang sngags ni che ge mo gr-ih+NA ma mi
[\[22a.4\]]hA mA tri ga Ne na hUM phaT/_ces bya ba rtsa ba'i gsang sngags kyi rjes su brjod pa ni sha'i sbyin sreg gi gsang sngags so/_/mA tri ga Na ba shaM mA nA ya swA hA/_zhes bya ba rtsa ba'i gsang sngags kyi rjes su brjod pa ni dbang du bya ba'i sngags so/_/'di ni sngon du ma mo dbang du bya ba'i sbyin sreg la sbyar bar
[\[22a.5\]]bya'o/_/de nas ma mo'i gdon gyis zin par 'gyur ro/_/gal te des kyang 'dzin du ma btub na sngags pa gcer bur byung ste/_skra lhug par bshig nas/_lus khrag sna tshogs kyis bskus te/_gdong shin tu bsgyur bas gsang sngags zlos shing g.yon brkyang ba'i stabs kyis thod pa mnan
[\[22a.6\]]te/_/sems rab tu khros pas gshin rje gshed po'i skur bsgoms nas/_'di lta bu'i sbyor ba nyi ma bdun gyis de ma mo'i gdon gyis zin par 'gyur ro/_/tha ma rnams kyang zla ba drug gis zin par 'gyur ro/_/phyis las grub par gyur nas de dag phyung ste 'o mas bkru bar bya'o/_/sbu gu rig _
[\[22a.7\]]pa'i cho ga las/_bsgrub bya ma mo'i gdon gyis zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba rdzogs so//_//da ni sbu gu rig par bya ba'i cho ga dang /_bsgrub bya smyo 'dres zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba bshad de/_dang po sngags pa bdag nyid kyis rdo rje dkyil 'khor legs par brtan par bsgoms shing
[\[22b\]]
[\[22b.1\]]gsang sngags legs par bzlas te drod thob par byas nas de nas bsgrub bya'i ling+ga snga ma bzhin byas te/_'byung po smyo 'dre gnas pa'i sar song nas shing leb dkar po bzang po zhig la/_rtse mo ngos su smyo 'dre kha dog dkar po la lag na shing ring ri mo sna tshogs pa thogs shing gar byed pa
[\[22b.2\]]bzhin mtshal gyis byugs shing brkos pa/_snying ga nas yi ge b+hu zhes bya ba gnas pa zhig bri'o/_/sba ba'i rtsar bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan skud pa nag pos shing leb dang bcing bar bya'o/_/bsgrub bya'i lte ba'i tshon skud 'byung po'i rkang pa la gu gul gyis sbyar bar bya'o/_/de nas shing leb
[\[22b.3\]]de dong du bcug ste legs par kha gcad par bya'o/_/de'i steng du thab khung zla gam byas te/_shing sna tshogs la me spar nas kha zas sna tshogs kyi sbyin sreg byas te/_gsang sngags he ma hA b+hU ta che ge mo zhes bya ba i daM du Sh+TAM gr-ih+Na hUM phaT/_ces bya ba rtsa ba'i gsang sngags kyi rjes su bskul bas sbyin
[\[22b.4\]]sreg bya'o/_/'di yang snga ma bzhin du zhag bdun nam zla ba drug gis 'dzin par 'gyur te/_gal te sgrub pa po sems stobs chung ba'i dbang gis des 'dzin du ma btub na de phyin chad kyang 'dzin par mi byed do/_/sgrub pa po nyid kyang bkra mi shis par byed do/_/sbu gu rig par bya ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga
[\[22b.5\]]las/_bsgrub bya 'byung po smyo 'dres zin par bya ba'i sbyor ba rdzogs so//_//gdon chen po bzhi po 'di dag kyang sgrub pa pos sbyin sreg dang mchod pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas mgu bar gyur pas sgrub pa po la phan 'dogs pa 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi/_'di ltar klu'i gdon ni phra mo'i sgo nas gzhan la
[\[22b.6\]]gnod pa'i las byed do/_/sa'i gdon ni brnab sems dang phrag dog gi sgo nas gzhan la gnod pa'i sbyor ba byed do/_/ma mo'i gdon ni chags sems kyi sgo nas gzhan la gnod pa'i sbyor ba byed do/_/'byung po'i gdon ni gnod sems kyi sgo nas gzhan la gnod pa'i sbyor ba byed de/_de bas na gdon
[\[22b.7\]]chen po 'di dag las myur bar byed pa yin yang las rtag tu brtan par byed pa yang ma yin la/_sgrub pa po bkra shis par byed pa yang ma yin/_'on kyang bye brag ni yod pa yin te/_'byung po ni blo sna tshogs can te des legs pa brtan par mi byed do/_/sa bdag ni rang 'dzin can te 'grogs na bde
[\[23a\]]
[\[23a.1\]]bar byed pa ma yin no/_/klu ni blun zhing rgyud gcig pa ste/_thog mar 'dris shing dga' bar 'gyur ba dka' ba'o/_/ma mo ni dga' che ba ste/_rtag tu de'i sems gzung bar dka'o/_/de bas na sgrub pa po rnams kyis rang gi nus pa dang sbyar te cho ga rnams la sbyar bar bya'o/_/
[\[23a.2\]]sbu gu rig pa zhes bya ba'i thabs kyi cho ga sbyor ba dang bcas pa bstan pa rdzogs so//_//de nas gnad rnams gzir ba yi/_/cho ga yang ni bshad par bya/_/rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor bsgom byas te/_/gsang sngags tshul bzhin bzlas byas nas/_/yi dam bcas pa rdzogs nas kyang /_/dur
[\[23a.3\]]khrod la sogs song nas ni/_/phur bu dpal rtse mdung la sogs/_/khrag chen gyis ni bskus nas kyang /_/gu gul nag pos bdug par bya/_/rus pa dag gi rgyan yang gdags/_/maN+Dal khrag gis byugs pa yi/_/steng du legs par gzugs par bya/_/mi yi tshil las byas pa yi/_/
[\[23a.4\]]mar me dag kyang phul nas ni/_/me tog nag po gtor nas kyang /_/de nas gsang sngags bzlas pa brtsam/_/gal te grub par gyur na ni/_/de ni dngos grub can du 'gyur/_/grub pa dag tu ma gyur kyang /_/mnan rnams gzir bar gdon mi za/_/mnan dang gzir ba'i thabs kyi cho ga ni 'di
[\[23a.5\]]yin te/_dang por sngags pas bsnyen pa'i cho ga ji ltar nus pa bzhin du byas te/_ji ltar rang gi dam bcas pa rdzogs par gyur pa dang /_nag po'i phyogs kyi tshes brgyad dam bcu bzhi la dur khrod la sogs pa'i gnas su song ste/_khrag gis bsgos pa'i maN+Dal gru gsum zhig byas nas/
[\[23a.6\]]der phur bu'am rtsang chen nam/_mdung thung rnams bzo bo mkhas pas legs par byas pa gang yang rung ba lnga'am dgu gzhag par bya'o/_/de'i phyi rol du lcags kyi tsher ma'am/_po son cha'i tsher ma'am gdug pa rnams la dug dang khrag gis bsgos pa'ang gzhag par bya'o/_/phur bu la
[\[23a.7\]]sogs pa gang yod pa de la khrag chen pos bskus te/_mi rus kyi rgyan yang gdags shing /_gu gul nag po'i spos kyis kyang bdugs te gzhag go/_/phyogs rnams su yang tshil chen po'i mar me dang /_me tog dug gis bsgos pa dang /_chang dang mi'i khrag sbyar pa'i ar+g+ha dang /_khrag
[\[23b\]]
[\[23b.1\]]sna tshogs dang sbyar ba'i gtor ma rnams kyang gzhag go/_/de nas sngags pa bdag nyid gos nag po gon skra lhug par bshig ste/_lag pa khrag gis bskus nas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin bsgom par bya'o/_/de nas khro bo gshin rje gshed po yang mtshon cha la spyan drangs te mchod par bya'o/
[\[23b.2\]]yang na mtshon cha de dag la sbyin sreg gis kyang mchod par bya'o/_/de nas mtshon cha de'i spyi bor nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng du/_yi ge ya 'od 'bar ba kha dog nag po zhig bsgom par bya'o/_/de'i rked pa la shar phyogs su k+Sha dkar po/_lho phyogs su ma ser po/_nub phyogs su me dmar po/
[\[23b.3\]]byang phyogs su da ljang gu/_de dag kyang nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gnas pa 'od 'bar ba'o/_/rtse mo'i cha la shar phyogs su ya dkar po/_lho phyogs su ts+tsha ser po/_nub phyogs su ni dmar po/_byang phyogs su ra ljang gu/_de dag kyang nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor la gnas pa 'od 'bar ba'o/_/rtse mo nyid du phaT
[\[23b.4\]]nag po 'od 'bar ba bsam ste/_mtshon cha de dag kyang shin tu gzi byin dang ldan par byin gyis brlab par bya'o/_/de nas sngags pa bdag nyid rtsa ba'i gsang sngags ji lta ba bzhin du brjod pas bskul bas/_rang gi snying ga'i yi ge'i sa bon las 'od zer las mtshon cha ji 'dra ba de lta bur gyur te/_phyogs
[\[23b.5\]]thams cad du 'phros pas sangs rgyas rnams la phog ste/_'od du gyur nas mtshon cha la 'dus te slar dus nas/_mdun gyi mtshon cha la thim par bya'o/_/'di lta bu dang ldan pa'i bzlas brjod ji ltar dam bcas pa bzhin du byed pa ni mtshon cha sgrub pa'i cho ga'o/_/gal te mtshan ma byung na ni rang gi lha la
[\[23b.6\]]'dud pa'i bsam pas mtshon cha de lag tu blangs pas dngos grub can du 'gyur ro/_/gal te mtshan ma ma byung na yang tha mal bar mi gzhag par ji lta ba bzhin du blangs te/_snod bzang por sbas la phyis las la sbyar bar bya'o/_/gal te de nyid kyi tshe las la sbyor bar 'dod na/_mtshan ma thob pa rnams kyis
[\[23b.7\]]ni/_mtshon cha gzas pa tsam gyis las grub par 'gyur ro/_/mtshan ma ma thob pa rnams kyis bya ba'i cho ga ni 'di yin ste/_bsgrub bya'i rjes dang dri ma la sogs pa ji ltar rnyed pa'i rdzas rnams dang /_dur khrod kyi sa dang thal ba rnams su sbyar te/_bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan sor brgyad pa zhig bya'o/_/de'i
[\[24a\]]
[\[24a.1\]]nang du yang dug dang skye tshe dang /_lan tshwa dang /_mi dang khyi'i khrag rnams sbyar te blugs par bya'o/_/ming dang rus kyang gro ba'am shog shog la bris te gzhag par bya'o/_/phyi rol du 'ang dur khrod kyi sol ba dang dug dang khrag gis bsku bar bya'o/_/de nas gzugs brnyan de skud
[\[24a.2\]]pa nag pos btags te maN+Dal gyi dbus su gan rkyal du mgo lhor bstan te bzhag la dgug pa'i sbyor ba ji ltar nus pas bsgrub bya bkug ste/_gzugs brnyan la phab ste gzhug par bya'o/_/de nas dbus kyi mtshon cha blangs te snying gar gdab par bya'o/_/de bzhin du shar phyogs kyi blangs te dpral bar
[\[24a.3\]]gdab bo/_/lho phyogs kyi blangs te lte bar gdab bo/_/nub phyogs kyi blangs te mgrin par gdab po/_/byang phyogs kyi blangs te gsang gnas su gdab po/_/gal te dgu yod na ni lhag ma bzhi yan lag bzhi la gdab po/_/tsher ma'i tshogs thams cad ni dbang po'i gnas thams cad dang /_tshigs
[\[24a.4\]]chen po rnams nas brtsams nas tshigs phra mo thams cad dang mthar lus ma lus par yongs su gang bar bya'o/_/de nas dkyil 'khor gyi dbus sam phyi rol gyi grwa'am/_yang na ji ltar bde ba'i gnas shig tu dong gru gsum zhig brkos te/_de'i nang du bud med kyi b+han+d+ha bkra mi shis pa zhig gi nang du bcug
[\[24a.5\]]nas/_skyes pa'i b+han+d+ha bkra mi shis pa zhig gis steng nas bkab ste/_dong de yang mgal dum dang tsher ma dang sol ba dang /_rus pa sna tshogs brdungs pa'i dum bu dang /_dug gi lo ma dang /_smad 'tshong ma'i smad dkris dang /_lam po che'i rdul rnams kyis bkang nas/_legs par sbas pa'i
[\[24a.6\]]steng du sna tshogs rdo rje zhig bris te/_de'i 'og tu sngags pa g.yas brkyang ba'i sbyor ba gnas nas gzir cing gsang sngags de nyid bzlas na gnad kyi gnas yongs su gzir bar 'gyur te/_gang dang gang gi mi ldan pa de dang de thams cad brlag par 'gyur ro/_/ji srid las grub par ma gyur pa de srid du
[\[24a.7\]]sbyor ba gtang bar mi bya'o/_/las grub par gyur nas de dag slar phyung ste/_phur bu'am rtsang la sogs pa'i mtshon cha rnams ni phyung la 'o mas bkrus te/_sbyin sreg gis mchod nas gzhag go/_/ling+ga ni 'o mas bkrus la sdig pa sreg pa'i sbyin sreg gam/_yang na chu klung du dor te bsod nams
[\[24b\]]
[\[24b.1\]]spel pa'i las bya'o/_/thod pa dang sol ba la sogs pa'i rdzas gzhan rnams ni phyi rol gyi gnas shig tu sbas te/_dus phyis dgos na de nyid nas blang bar bya'o/_/dong de nyid sa bzang pos bkang ste gzhag go/_/sbyor ba 'di lta bu legs par byas kyang rjes su bskul ba zla ba drug gis kyang

[\[25a.1\]]bya rgod 'ug pa la sogs pa'i/_/spu'am 'dab ma ldan pa'i mda'/_/bcu drug dag kyang gzhag par bya/_/khro bo'i sngags kyis gzir byas pa'i/_/dug dang ma mo'i sngags dag dang /_/phra man sngags dang sbyar byas te/_/gdug pa gang na gnas pa der/_/gtor zhing
[\[25a.2\]]'phangs na ma rung 'gyur/_/de la byug pa dang gtor ba'i rdzas kyis bsgrub bya'i lus 'drul ba la sogs pa dang /_sgo kun nas ma rung par 'gyur ba'i thabs kyi cho ga bshad par bya ste/_dang por bsgom pa dang bzlas pa'i sgo nas sngon du legs par bsnyen pa byas la/_mar gyi ngo la dur khrod la sogs

[\[25a.5\]]brgya rtsa brgyad byas te/_dur khrod kyi sol bas nag por bskul la 'og ngos su yi ge ru dmar po bris te/_dug thams cad kyi rten khrag me long tsam rer 'gyur bar bsgom mo/_/steng gi dbus su dug thams cad kyi snying po yi ge kha nag po bris te dug nag po me ltar 'bar bar bsgom mo/_/gru gsum

[\[25b.1\]]la dug gi sngags dang /_phra men ma rang rang gi snying po bzlas pa blugs te shing gdug pa las byas pa'i mde'u dbyibs gru gsum dug dang khrag gis bskus pa bcug ste phyogs mtshams brgyad du gzhag_/phyogs bzhir gzhu bzhi dang mi ro'i skra las byas pa'i 'khrul 'khor bzhi yang

[\[25b.4\]]bkang ste bzhag nas bdag nyid lha'i rnal 'byor dang ldan pas khros te rtsa ba'i gsang sngags bzlas pa'i yungs kar gyis rdzas de dag thams cad la gtor bar bya'o/_/de nas rtsa ba'i gsang sngags kyi rjes su dug thams cad kyi rten gyi snying po yi ge ru zhes bya ba dang /_dug nyid kyi snying po'i yi ge kha
[\[25b.5\]]zhes bya ba dang /_dug gi ming gi sngags so sor byas te/_dug gzhug pa'i snying po dang bcas te spel nas yungs kar la bsngags te rdzas de dag thams cad la gtor bar bya'o/_/de nas ma mo dang phra men ma'i sngags kyang rtsa ba'i gsang sngags kyis gzir cing bzlas te gtor bar bya'o/_/de yang khrag
