[\[59a.3\]]'jam rgyal khro bo yi/_/brtul zhugs la sogs bstan par bya/_/bsnyen pa legs byas de 'og tu/_/khro bo'i brtul zhugs brtsam par bya/_/skra ni lhug par bshig byas shing /_/bzhin yang rnam par bsgyur byas te/_/be+e con ral gri tri shUl sogs/_/lag pa g.yas kyis
[\[59a.4\]]gzung bar bya/_/sdigs mdzub dag dang ldan par bya/_/smyung ba la yang gnas bzhin du/_/khro bo yid la dran byed cing /_/gsang sngags rgyal po bzla bar bya/_/gtam gzhan smra bar mi bya ste/_/khro bo dran pa ma gtogs pa/_/'jigs dang chags pa spang bar bya/_/tha mal mi dang
[\[59a.5\]]mi 'grogs par/_/gcig pu khyad par lam nas rgyu/_/'di ltar zla drug spyad nas ni/_/sgrub pa la ni 'jug par bya/_/dur khrod dben pa la sogs par/_/dkyil 'khor bzang po khyad par can/_/dur khrod thal ba'am de ldan par/_/legs par bri bar bya ba ni/_/sgo bzhir ldan zhing grwa bzhir
[\[59a.6\]]ldan/_/snying po re mig dgu pa la/_/yi ge bcu bdun legs par dgod/_/de yi dbus su gshin rje gshed/_/dur khrod ras la bris pa ni/_/mi bzad rab tu 'bar ba gzhag_/de yi mdun du be con dang /_/ral gri tri shUl la sogs pa/_/ji ltar sngon du brjod pa bzhin/_/
[\[59a.7\]]legs par brgyan te gzhag par bya/_/sngags pa lha yi 'byor ldan pas/_/gshin rje gshed po spyan drangs te/_/mchod pa'i cho gas mnyes byas nas/_/de nas bzlas la 'bad par bya/_/grub pa'i mtshan ma thob gyur na/_/dngos grub sngon dang mtshungs par 'gyur/_/de dag phyi rol
[\[59b\]]
[\[59b.1\]]brtul zhugs kyi/_/sbyor bar bcas pa bshad pa yin/_/de nas bshad par bya ba ni/_/de las mchog tu gyur pa ste/_/smyung bdag kyang bya mi dgos/_/kha zas dag kyang sdom mi dgos/_/phyag rgya sngags dang bsam pa dag_/snga ma bzhin du bsgrubs nas ni/_/sha chen za zhing
[\[59b.2\]]khrag chen 'thung /_/ba lang khyi sha de bzhin te/_/rta dang glang po la sogs pa'i/_/sha rnams rjen par bza' bar bya/_/khrag dang chang du sbyar ba yi/_/de bzhin bag dang ldan par btung /_/bshang gci khrag la sogs pa yi/_/bdud rtsi lnga po za byed cing /_/de bzhin lus kyang byug par
[\[59b.3\]]bya/_/skye bo med pa'i sa phyogs su/_/khro bo'i gad mo drag por dgod/_/kun la sdigs shing nyam nga med/_/'di ltar zla drug bsgrubs nas ni/_/sgrub pa la ni 'jug par bya/_/mtshan mo dur khrod dben par ni/_/dkyil 'khor snga ma bzhin bris te/_/de bzhin sku gzugs gzhag
[\[59b.4\]]par bya/_/mtshon cha la sogs de bzhin te/_/ci dga' ba dag bzhag nas ni/_/bdag nyid rnal 'byor ldan pa yis/_/gshin rje gshed po spyan drangs te/_/sha lnga dang ni bdud rtsi yis/_/nyin re rtag tu mchod byas nas/_/bzlas pa la ni rnam par 'bad/_/de ltar rab tu brtson pa
[\[59b.5\]]la/_/cho 'phrul sna tshogs 'byung 'gyur yang /_/ma nyams bzlas la 'bad par bya/_/de la gshin rje gshed po nyid/_/dgod cing dngos grub stsol bar byed/_/yang na mtshon cha 'bar ba dang /_/'bar dang du ba dro ba 'byung /_/gal te grub par ma gyur yang /_/las rnams grub pa
[\[59b.6\]]gdon mi za/_/'di ni brtul zhugs mchog ldan pas/_/dngos grub sgrub bar byed pa la/_/dpa' bo rnams kyis bsgrub bya ba/_/thun mong min pa bshad pa yin/_/'dir bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed po'i brtul zhugs spyad pas/_/dngos grub chen po rnams bsgrub par
[\[59b.7\]]bstan pa las/_brtul zhugs kyang rnam pa gnyis gsungs te/_'di ltar phyi rol dang nang gi'o/_/de la phyi rol ni smyung ba dang bcas shing phyi rol gyi bya ba srung ba dang bcas pa'o/_/nang gi phyi rol gyi smyung ba la gnas pa dang srung ba phra mo dag med de/_rnal 'byor ba'i dam tshig gi
[\[60a\]]
[\[60a.1\]]rdzas mi la sogs pa'i sha rnam pa lnga dang /_bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga la rol cing phyi rol gyi bya ba la nyam nga ba med pa'i spyod pa'o/_/de gnyis ka'i thun mong lus ngag yid gsum gyi sgo nas lha'i cha lugs 'dzin cing /_gsang sngags kyi bzlas pa dang lha yid la byed pa dang ldan
[\[60a.2\]]pa dag ni mtshungs par shes par bya'o/_/de la re zhig lus kyi spyod pa ni gos med pa'am yang na stag gi pags pa la sogs pa'am dur khrod kyi thal ba'am khrag lta bus bsgos pa'i ras gyon pa dang /_skra spyi bor bcing ba'am/_lhug par bshig pa'am/_lus dur khrod kyi sol ba
[\[60a.3\]]'am thal ba la sogs pas byugs pa'am/_bzhin rnam par bsgyur ba dang /_dbugs 'bud pa dang /_lag pa g.yas par mtshon cha be con dang /_ral gri dang tri shUl la sogs pa gang yang rung ba'i mtshon cha thogs pa dang /_g.yon pa'i sdigs mdzub dang ldan pas dung chen po
[\[60a.4\]]la sogs pa'i phreng ba thogs pa dang /_skye bo med pa'i lam du rgyu zhing phrad pa dag la yang lam mi 'dzur zhing phyag mi 'tshal ba dang /_mtshan mo yang dur khrod la sogs pa byis pa rnams nyam nga ba'i gnas su gnas shing rgyu bar byed pa ni khro bo chen po lus kyi brtul zhugs so/_/rtag tu gsang sngags
[\[60a.5\]]zlos shing tshig tha mal pa dag mi smra ba dang /_gal te bdud kyi rigs dag yid du 'ong ba'am mi 'ong ba dag sprul nas/_spro ba'i tshig dag gis dbugs 'byin tam ma rungs pa'i tshig gis skrag par byed kyang lan smra bar mi byed pa ni ngag gi brtul zhugs so/_/rtag tu bcom ldan 'das gshin rje
[\[60a.6\]]gshed po 'ba' zhig sems par byed cing /_rtog pa gzhan yongs su 'dor ba dang /_rang gi lha ma gtogs pa gzhan gang la yang ma chags shing /_rtag tu rang gi lha la sems dang ba dang /_gzugs mi sdug pa dag snang bar gyur cing /_sgra mi snyan pa dag thos kyang sems nyam nga ba med
[\[60a.7\]]cing /_de bzhin du yid du 'ong ba'i yul dag snang bar gyur kyang /_g.yeng zhing chags par mi 'gyur bar blo rab tu brtan par gnas pa ni yid kyi brtul zhugs so/_/brtul zhugs rnam pa 'di gsum dang ldan par spyad pa ni phyi dang nang gnyis ka la thun mong du 'gyur ro/_/de la khyad par ni 'di yin
[\[60b\]]
[\[60b.1\]]te phyi rol gyi brtul zhugs 'dzin pas ni kha zas mi za bar smyung ba la gnas pas dus gsum du khrus bya'o/_/ltogs par gyur na yang ba lang gi lci ba bza'o/_/des lus gnas par ma nus na ba'i 'o ma dang sbyar te btung bar bya'o/_/yang na ba'i rnam pa lnga legs par sbyar te btung
[\[60b.2\]]par bya'o/_/de la legs par sbyar ba'i cho ga ni 'di yin te/_dang po ba lang gi lci ba dang ba'i gcin du sbyar te/_legs par mnyes nas cung zad cig gzhag par bya'o/_/de nas steng gi dngas ma dang zhabs kyi snyigs ma gnyis bzhag ste/_cha bar ma ska sla ran par blangs te der ba'i 'o ma
[\[60b.3\]]dang ba'i mar dang ba'i kha chu rnams dang sbyar te legs par gdus nas dus dus su btung bar bya'o/_/gal te de ltar mi nus pa dag gis kyang dkar gsum la sogs te/_zas gtsang zhing bsngags pa zos nas khrus legs par byas te brtul zhugs spyad par bya'o/_/de la dus kyi
[\[60b.4\]]dus chen po gsum ni nang par langs ma thag dang /_nyi ma gung dang dgongs nyal ka rnam pa gsum yin no/_/lhag ma'i dus ni sa chen po byas ba'i dus su lus thams cad bkru bar bya'o/_/sa chung ngu dang snabs 'dor ba dag la ni kha dang lag pa gnyis bkru bar bya'o/_/stod smad kyi
[\[60b.5\]]dbugs ngan pa brgyus pa dang /_lud pa 'dor ba dang /_kha zas za ba dang /_zos pa'i rjes rnams su ni kha tsam bkru bar bya'o/_/gzhan yang bag bya bar 'os pa sangs rgyas kyis ma gnang ba ngag kyang bsrung bar bya ste/_'di ni phyi rol gyi brtul zhugs kyi mtshan nyid thun mong ma
[\[60b.6\]]yin pa'o/_/de la nang gi brtul zhugs thun mong ma yin pa'i mtshan nyid gang zhe na/_smyung ba la gnas pa med cing khrus med pa/_kha zas bsdams pa med cing gtsang sme med par bza' ba dang /_dam tshig gi zas su gyur pa mi dang /_glang po che dang /_rta dang /_ba glang dang /_khyi sha
[\[60b.7\]]rnams rjen par za ba dang /_snang mdzad dang /_dri chu dang /_sa bon dang /_pad+ma rak+ta dang /_sha chen po zhes bya ba bdud rtsi lnga po rnams za zhing las bya ba gang la yang 'dzem pa dang mi 'dzem pa zhes bya ba gnyis kyi bsam pa dang /_spyod pa dang bral bas gnas par byed cing brtul
[\[61a\]]
[\[61a.1\]]zhugs spyod par byed pa ni nang gi mtshan nyid do/_/de ltar brtul zhugs zla ba drug spyad nas sgrub pa la 'jug par gsungs te/_brtul zhugs spyod pa'i sngon rol du ni dus nges pa dang /_grangs nges pa dang /_mtshan ma thob pa zhes bya ba'i bsnyen pa rnam pa gsum gang
[\[61a.2\]]yang rung ba la sbyar dgos so zhes shes par bya'o/_/de ltar bsnyen pa dang brtul zhugs dang ldan pas sgrub pa la 'jug par bya ste/_re zhig 'byor ba bzang po la dur khrod la sogs pa'i gnas su song ste/_dur khrod kyi thal bas ji skad gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor mtshan mo bri bar bya'o/_/
[\[61a.3\]]de la 'dir re zhig bcom ldan 'das kyi rdo rje dkyil 'khor gyi mtshan nyid bstan pa ni/_snying po'i dkyil 'khor re'u mig dgu dang ldan pa sna tshogs rdo rjes mtshan pa/_de'i steng du sna tshogs pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad dam bcu drug gam brgya'am stong la sogs pa ci dga' ba bri bar bya'o/_/snying po'i
[\[61a.4\]]dkyil 'khor de'i phyi rol du grwa bzhi dang /_sgo bzhi dang rta babs dang bcas pa yang bri bar bya'o/_/de'i phyi rol 'khor yug tu 'khor lo rtsibs brgya stong gi rtse mo la rdo rje 'bar bas bskor ba las me 'bar ba 'phro bar bri'o/_/dbus dang phyogs mtshams dang sgo rnams su yang /_ji ltar sngon du
[\[61a.5\]]rang gi snying gar 'khor lo bsgom pa ji lta ba bzhin du/_nyi ma dang zla ba'i gnas la yi ge bcu bdun dgod par bya'o/_/me tog dang bdug pa la sogs pas mchod pa dang gtor ma la sogs pa rnams ni/_phyi nang gnyis ka la bye brag med par khrag gis gtor ba'i me tog dang sha chen po'i
[\[61a.6\]]bdug pa dang /_til chen po'i mar me'i phreng ba dang /_sha sna tshogs 'di ltar sha rnam pa lnga la sogs pa srog chags thams cad kyi sha rnams dang rjen pa dang /_btsos pa rnams dang bsregs pa dang /_skam po rnams dang ldan pa'i bshos dang gtor ma yang dbul bar bya'o/_/de la re zhig
[\[61a.7\]]'di'i cho ga ni dkyil 'khor legs par bri ste/_mchod pa'i rdzas kyang bsog ste sku gzugs bzang po yang dkyil 'khor du bkram nas/_ji skad du smos pa'i be con la sogs pa'i mtshon cha rus pa'i rgyan dang me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan te/_bdug pas bdugs te bcom ldan 'das dang /
[\[61b\]]
[\[61b.1\]]bdag nyid kyi mdun du legs par btsugs te gzhag go/_/gal te rdzas las bsgrub pa zhig na mtshon cha'i gnas su ldong ros sam/_any+tsa na la sogs pa snod bzang po'i nang du gzhug go/_/de nas bdag nyid lha'i sbyor ba dang ldan pas dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i gnas su bcom ldan 'das
[\[61b.2\]]gshin rje gshed por bsams te/_ji ltar sngon du brjod pa bzhin du der spyan drang ba dang mchod pa'i cho ga legs par bya'o/_/mtshon cha la yang mchod pa bya ste/_de nyid la me tog dang bdug pa'i sbyin sreg byas nas/_lag pa g.yas pas bzung ste bzlas brjod la 'jug par bya'o/_/de yang ji srid du mtshon
[\[61b.3\]]cha de me ltar 'bar bar ma gyur pa de srid du bzlas par bya ba'am/_yang na zla ba drug gi bar du bzlas par bya'o/_/de'i tshe mtshon cha de dag ji lta ba bzhin du 'bar ba la sogs pa'i mtshan ma byung na dang po lha la gus pas btud de/_bdag nyid phul nas dngos grub kyi rdzas de dag kyang bdag nyid dang lha dang slob
[\[61b.4\]]dpon dang /_grogs rnams la ci rigs su bsgo bar bya'o/_/gal te grub par ma gyur na yang slar spogs pa'i cho ga dag brtsam par bya'o/_/gal te grub pa las nyams par gyur na dngos grub slar dbrog pa'i cho ga dag bya'o/_/gal te dus ma yin par mtshan ma byung na srung ba byas te dus su
[\[61b.5\]]bslang bar bya'o/_/gal te grub par ma gyur na yang bgo ba la sogs pa de bzhin du byas te/_legs par bsrungs te bzhag na dngos grub 'bring po thob par 'gyur ro/_/de la slar spogs pa'i cho ga ni dang por sgrub pa nyid dang 'dra ste/_zla ba drug tu sgrub pa'i cho ga de nyid slar bskyar bar bya'o/_/
[\[61b.6\]]des grub par ma gyur na cho ga gnyis pa ni thabs de nyid zla ba gnyis su bskyar bar bya'o/_/des grub par ma gyur na yang thabs gsum pa la yang cho ga de nyid zla ba gnyis su bskyar ba yin no/_/de ltar spogs pa'i cho ga lan gsum du bsgrubs kyang sngon gyi las dang ting nge 'dzin dang /_dad pa'i bye
[\[61b.7\]]brag gis dngos grub kyi snod du cung zad ma gyur pa srid pas de nas drag shul gyi sbyor bas zhag bdun bsgrub par bya ste/_rang gi snying ga'i sa bon las sprul pa'i khro bo chen po lag na lcags kyu thogs pa zhig dang /_rdo rje thogs pa zhig sprul te/_lcags kyu can gyis ye shes kyi lha'i thugs
[\[62a\]]
[\[62a.1\]]ka nas drangs te/_rdo rje can gyis rgyab nas brdeg cing phul te dbang med par bkug nas/_sngon du smos pa'i dngos grub kyi rten rnams la thim par bsam zhing tshig 'dis yang bskul bar bya'o/_/sku gsung thugs su bdag sbyor bas/_/sangs rgyas thams cad bdag la gson/_/
[\[62a.2\]]nga ni dpal ldan ral gri 'chang /_/bka' yi 'khor lo rab sbyor bas/_/gal te dam las 'gal gyur cing /_/grub pa tshul bzhin ma stsal na/_/sangs rgyas sku gsung las byung ba'ang /_/dam tshig mchog gis 'gas par 'gyur/_/zhig par gyur par gdon mi za/_/zhes bya ba'i tshig dag
[\[62a.3\]]gis dam tshig rab tu bskul zhing /_zhag bdun du bar chad med par lha gzir ba'i cho ga byas pas gdon mi za bar 'grub par bshad do/_/'di ni bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i khro bo'i phyi nang brtul zhugs rnam pa gnyis 'dzin pas dngos grub chen po'i sgrub pa'i khyad par bstan pa ste/_cho ga 'di dag nyid
[\[62a.4\]]kyis lcags kyu dang zhags pa dang thod pa dang sdigs mdzub dang /_gzhan yang ldong ros dang /_mig sman dang ri lu dang bcud kyis len dang /_rkang pa byug pa la sogs pa rdzas thams cad sgrub pa la sbyar bar bya'o/_/gal te mchog gi dngos grub chen po bsgrub mi nus pa rnams kyis ni/_'o ma dang
[\[62a.5\]]zho dang mar dang chu gtsang dang rtsab mo la sogs pa las bsgrub par bya'o/_/de la 'o ma la sogs pa bsgrub pa la ni/_sngon du bsnyen pa 'bum phrag gsum mam zla ba drug tu bsnyen pa byas te bsgrub pa zla ba phyed byas nas tha ma zla ba gzas zin pa'i nub mo dkyil 'khor byas kyang rung ma byas kyang rung ste/_
[\[62a.6\]]zla ba gzas ma btang gi bar du mar la sogs pa lag pa g.yon pas bkab ste/_dngos grub la dmigs nas rtse gcig pas bzlas brjod byas na/_de zla ba btang bar gyur tsam na mtshan ma byung na ni/_de dag 'thungs pas shes rab 'phel ba la sogs pa dngos grub 'bring po 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/
[\[62a.7\]]mtshan ma ma byung na yang phan pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/de lta bu dag la yang ni brtul zhugs 'dzin pa med kyang sgrub tu rung ngo /_/'di ni re zhig zhar la brjod pa ste/_brtul zhugs dang ri mo dang dkyil 'khor la sogs pa dang ldan pas dngos grub chen po bsgrub pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pa rdzogs so//_//
[\[62b\]]
[\[62b.1\]]dngos grub pa dag gi spyod lam gyi mtshan nyid bya ba sna tshogs dag spyod pa la tshogs chen por 'gyur ba dang /_dngos grub kyi rgyur 'gyur ba dang /_bgegs la sogs pa'i bar chad du mi 'gyur zhing bkra shis par 'gyur ba dang /_kha na ma tho ba med pas 'gro ba rnams sdud par 'gyur ba'i cho ga rnams
[\[62b.2\]]bshad par bya ste/_de la spyod lam ni khrus dang /_kha zas za ba dang /_tha mal pa'i bya ba la 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid dang /_nyal ba dang ldang ba'i bya ba dang /_rnam par g.yeng bar bya ba'i spyod pa dag ste rtsed mo la sogs pa la 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid do/_/'di dag thams cad la yang thun mong du ni byang
[\[62b.3\]]chub kyi sems rnam pa gnyis dang ma bral ba ste/_'di chos thams cad skye ba med par rtogs pa dang /_sgyu ma tsam du snang ba'i 'gro ba rnams la yongs su bskyab pa'i phyir rang gi lha'i ting nge 'dzin mi gtong ba'o/_/bgegs bskrad cing srung ba yang de nyid kyis byas par 'gyur ro/_/khyad par du ni khrus byed
[\[62b.4\]]pa'i tshe sangs rgyas rnams kyi byang chub kyi sems kyi rang bzhin bdud rtsi'i chu yis dbang bskur bar bsam par bya ste/_/de yang mdun gyi nam mkha' la rang gi ye shes kyi lha bsams te de la yid kyis phyag byas nas/_ji skad smos pa'i khrus byas pas ye shes kyi bdud rtsi'i bum pas bdag
[\[62b.5\]]la spyi bo nas dbang bskur bas sgrib pa'i dri ma thams cad yongs su dag par bsam mo/_/de nas yang bdag nyid kyi snyim pas chu gtsang ma blangs te/_de yang bdud rtsir bsams nas bde bar gshegs pa rnams la lan gsum du phul te slar gshegs su gsol nas/_/de nas bdag
[\[62b.6\]]nyid ldang bar bya'o/_/de nas srung ba dang yang ldan par bya ste/_/'di ni re zhig khrus kyi cho ga bstan pa rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin mdor bsdus pa'o/_/kha zas za ba'i cho ga ni phyi rol dang nang gi bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis te/_de la phyi rol gyi ni sred cing chags pas longs spyad pa'i phyir ma yin
[\[62b.7\]]gyi/_phung po gnas pas bdag dang gzhan gyi don gyi phyir tshogs chen po bskyed par bya'o snyam du bsams te/_kha na ma tho ba med pa ci ran du za'o/_/nang gi dam tshig bdud rtsir byin gyis brlabs pa'i sbyor bas thams cad mchod pa ste/_/de la re zhig 'di'i cho ga ni kha zas kyi snod ni
[\[63a\]]
[\[63a.1\]]pad+ma'i snod du byin gyis brlab par bya'o/_/kha zas ni mi la sogs pa dam tshig gi sha rnam pa lnga dang /_snang mdzad la sogs pa dam tshig gi bdud rtsi lnga'i rang bzhin du brtags te/_ye shes kyi bdud rtsi'i rang bzhin sku gsung thugs kyi bdag nyid dang ldan pa 'dod pa'i yon tan sna tshogs 'byung ba yon tan dang
[\[63a.2\]]ldan par byin gyis brlab bo/_/yang na bza' ba'i bye brag rnams ni bde bar gshegs pa rnams 'od du zhu ba las gyur pa'i kha zas su bsam mo/_/btung ba'i bye brag rnams ni yul rnams 'od du zhu ba las gyur pa'i bdud rtsi btung bar bsam mo/_/de ltar yab yum gnyis su med pa'i bde ba chen po'i ros thams cad
[\[63a.3\]]mnyes par byed pa'i mthu dang ldan par byin gyis brlab bo/_/de la bdag nyid kyi lus lha'i dkyil 'khor du byin gyis brlabs te lce dang lag pa dag kyang sprul pa'i lus kyis mchod pa byed pa'i bdag nyid du bsam par bya'o/_/yang na lag pa'i sor mo lnga ni rigs lnga'i bdag nyid lag mthil gyi dkyil 'khor ni sangs rgyas
[\[63a.4\]]rnams bzhugs pa'i pho brang /_kha zas rnams lag tu blangs pa ni tshogs chen po la rol cing spyod pa ste mchod pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang po'o/_/de nas kha ni rnam par thar pa'i gzhal yas khang /_lce ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang dag pa'i ye shes/_kha zas zos pa ni byang chub kyi sems rnam par mi rtog pa'i ro myong ba'i
[\[63a.5\]]mtshan nyid la rol ba'i mchod pa ste/_de bzhin du mchod pa gnyis pa'o/_/de nas dbang po dang bcas pa'i khog pa ni rang gi lha'i dkyil 'khor/_kha zas kyis tshim par byas pa ni rang gi lha'i dkyil 'khor rgyun du mchod pa/_zhu zhing mi snang bar gyur pas chos thams cad ma skyes pa'i ngang du rnam par dag pa ste/_'di ltar kham gyi
[\[63a.6\]]zas kyi rdul phra rab gcig gis kyang mchod pa gsum byas par 'gyur la/_mchod pa gcig kyang byang chub kyi sems rnam pa gnyis dang ldan pas bdag dang gzhan gyi don du 'gyur zhing /_bsod nams dang ye shes dag kyang rdzogs pa ste 'di ni rgya che ba bla na med pa'i mchod pa zhes bshad do/_/za ba'i ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs dag kyang
[\[63a.7\]]'dir 'dus par dgongs so/_/de la kha zas za ba'i tshe phyag rgya rnam pa bzhi yin te/_nam mkha' lding gi phyag rgyas dug sbyangs shing bdud rtsir byin gyis brlab pa dang /_spyan 'dren pa'i phyag rgyas tshogs kyi 'khor lor sangs rgyas rnams spyan drangs pa dang /_pad+ma'i phyag rgyas tshogs kyi 'khor lo longs spyod pa dang /_slar gshegs
[\[63b\]]
[\[63b.1\]]su gsol ba'i phyag rgyas mchod pa zin nas sangs rgyas rnams rang gi gnas su gshegs par bya'o/_/de la nam mkha' lding gi phyag rgya ni/_mthe bong dang srin lag rtse sprad de nam mkha' lding gi mchu ltar byas lhag ma rnams sbrul mgo ltar brkyang ba 'di ni dug thams cad 'byin par byed cing /_bdud rtsi sbyin par byed pa'i nam
[\[63b.2\]]mkha' lding gi phyag rgya zhes bya ba ste/_'dir ni zas kyi steng du bzhag nas rang gi lha'i gsang sngags yang rung ba'am/_rdo rje bdud rtsi'i gsang sngags sam/_yum rnams kyi sngags sam/_ngo bo nyid kyis dag pa'i sngags sam/_rdo rje mkha' lding rang gi gsang sngags kyis bzlas nas byin gyis brlab par 'gyur ro/_/
[\[63b.3\]]yang na lha thams cad kyi de kho na nyid kyi snying po bsdus par gyur pa oM AHhUM zhes bya ba 'di nyid kyis thams cad byin gyis brlabs par 'gyur ro/_/de la nam mkha' lding gi snying po ni/_oM badzra ga ru Da a mr-i te hUM phaT/_ces bya ba 'di yin no/_/de la spyan 'dren pa'i phyag ni lag pa gnyis kyi sor mo g.yab pa'i tshul gyis
[\[63b.4\]]snying gar mkhrig ma bsnol te/_se gol lan gsum brdabs nas de nas zhi ba'i thal mo brdab pa'o/_/pad+ma'i phyag rgya ni lag pa gnyis rting pa sprad de/_mthe bo dang mthe'u chung ngos sbyar nas lhag ma pad+ma kha bye ba ltar byas te/_'dis kha zas kyi snod bzung ste bza' zhing sbyin par bya'o/_/slar gshegs su gsol ba'i phyag
[\[63b.5\]]rgya ni lag pa gnyis sor mo'i rgyab kyis phyir g.yab pa ste/_'dis lha rnams slar gshegs su gsol ba byas par 'gyur ro/_/phyi rol gyi dgos pa'i bya ba sna tshogs la 'jug pa'i tshe ni rang gi lha'i ting nge 'dzin gyis gzhan gyi don spyod pa'i phyag rgya ni nyid mi gtong ba tsam yin no/_/nyal ba'i dus na ni stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin
[\[63b.6\]]yid la byed pa yin no/_/ldang ba'i tshe na ni snying rje chen po'i stobs bskyed pa'o/_/rtsed mo la sogs pa'i rnam par g.yeng ba'i tshe na yang /_dang po byang chub sems kyi shugs ma btang ba nyid kyis nyams par mi 'gyur zhes bshad do/_/'di dag tu srung ba thams cad la yang /_bsrung ba'i bsam pa dang ldan pa tsam dang /_sngags
[\[63b.7\]]dang phyag rgya dang ldan pa dang /_gzhan yang mig bltas pa dang /_rdzas gtor ba dang /_thal mo drag tu brdabs pa dag gis kyang bgegs bskrad cing srung bar 'gyur ro/_/mchod rten gdab pa dang /_dam pa'i chos klog pa'i tshe na yang snying rje'i stobs kyis bdag dang gzhan gyi don bsgrub pa'i phyir/_dge ba 'di spyad par bya'o snyam du

[\[64a.1\]]byas pa'i yid la byed pas 'phags te bya'o/_/spyod lam bsdus pa'i mtshan nyid ces bya ba nye bar bstan pa'i mtshan nyid rdzogs so//_//nam mkha'i khams kyi mthas klas rab 'byam du/_/'jig rten dag na 'jigs byed ji snyed cig_/bdud dang srin po gnod sbyin la sogs pa/_/de dag kun las gshin rje

[\[64a.3\]]zhing gi rdul snyed kyang /_/gshin rje gshed dang mtshungs pa 'ga' ma mchis/_/de phyir rtog pa'i rgyal po 'di nyid las/_/gang bshad de ni cho ga kun gyi gtso/_/lha 'am bdud dam de bzhin gshegs kun la/_/log 'dren mu stegs skye bo ngan pa rnams/_/kun nas 'dus kyang bar du gcod mi nus/_/shes rab ting 'dzin dad pa dman

[\[67b.1\]]rnams la sbyar bar bya'o/_/de dag dang mchod pa gzhan rnams la yang thun mong du byin gyis rlob pa mchod pa'i sprin chen po 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i rig pa chen mo 'dis byin gyis brlab par bya'o/_/oM a nut+ta ra sarba pU dza me g+ha s+pha ra Na ma hA sa ma ye swA hA/_zhes bya ba 'di thams cad la sbyar bar bya'o/_/rdo rje dril bu la sogs te sil

[\[75b.3\]]lo 'di tsi tra ka dang /_dug dang /_a rka'i lo ma dang /_ske tshe dang khrag rnams kyis rdzogs par bris nas seng ldeng gi me la bsro zhing khros pa'i sems kyis brgya phrag lnga bzlas pa byas na/_rims kyis 'dzin par 'gyur ba ni bsgrub bya'i khyim mam/_lam gyi bzhi mdo'am/_dur khrod
[\[75b.4\]]du sbas na'o/_/thams cad las grol bar 'dod na 'o mas bkrus na grol bar 'gyur ro/_/rgyas pa la gro ga la bzhi mnyam gyis 'khor lo 'di bri/_tha ma gnyis su oM bri/_dbus su bsgrub bya'i ming /_skul bar byed pa'i tshig dang ldan par gzung bar bya zhing /_thang ka'i mdun du nyin re

[\[80a.2\]]mnan te/_sngags bzlas pas gong bu dgug pa'o/_/de bzhin du snying gar trIHdmar pos mtshan par bsgoms nas bzlas na/_rkang pa 'gugs par 'gyur ro/_/oM hrIHSh+T+rIHwi kraM tA na na tsA la ya pA da tsA la ne hUM hUM phaT phaT/_oM hrIHSh+T+r-iH wi kraM tA na na pa t+ya de pa data taM/_mA ra ya mA ra ya/_
[\[80a.3\]]ra raM ra raM haM hUM hUM phaT phaT/_oM hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na dzi baM ba ra ta hUM hUM phaT phaT/_oM rak+ta rU pa sar+b+ba satwa/_da ma ka_/s+t+waM b+ha ya/_mo ha ya ban+dA ya/_hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tAn na hUM hUM phaT phaT/_hrIHche ge mo bdag gi dbang du gyis shig_/hrIHtsheg drag dang bcas pa dzaHgnyis kyi bar du bcug pa
[\[80a.4\]]ni rkang pa dgug pa'o/_/rim pa ji lta bar sngags kyi tshig rnams go bar bya'o/_/oM hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na b+hU/_a mu kaM/_g+haHg+haHhUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA/_zho dang 'o ma 'dres pa'i zan la sogs pa'i sbyin sreg gis rgyas par 'gyur ro/_/oM hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na he he hUM hUM phaT phaT/
[\[80a.5\]]grong gi phyogs su gtor ma btang ste/_dbus su til gyi sbyin sreg byas na/_bdud kyi gnod pa thams cad zhi bar 'gyur ro/_/rnam dag gsung ste/_dmar ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa thams cad brlag par mdzad pa'i don to/_/'das dang ma 'ongs pa dang da
[\[80a.6\]]ltar byung ba'i dus gsum ni spyan gsum mo/_/phyag gnyis ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa'i rtog pa 'joms pa'o/_/stong pa dang snying rje dbyer med par ldan pas na shes rab ma la 'khyud pa'o/_/klu brgyad ni rnam par shes pa brgyad rab tu ston pa'o/_/mi mgo brgya phyed kyi phreng ba ni
[\[80a.7\]]yi ge lnga bcu dang ldan pa'o/_/g.yon pa'i thod pa ye shes kyi bdud rtsis bkang ba ni stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin no/_/g.yas pa'i dbyug to ni phung po dang nyon mongs pa dang /_lha'i bu dang 'chi bdag gi bdud bzhi bcom zhing snying rje'i rang bzhin no/_/zhabs g.yon brkyang bas ni khams
[\[80b\]]
[\[80b.1\]]gsum rab tu ston pa'o/_/bdud bzhi khrag gi ro dang bcud len dpag tu med pa myong bas na lha mo'i g.yon gyi phyag na thod pa'o/_/g.yas kyi gri gug gi dngos po dang /_dngos po med pa'i rnam par rtog pa rab tu gcod pa'i phyir ro/_/gdug pa can 'dul ba ni khro bo'i gzugs can no/_/gsus
[\[80b.2\]]pa 'phyang ba ni mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'o/_/dbu skra ser po gyen du brdzes pa ni/_sdug bsngal ba dang kun 'byung ba dang /_'gog pa dang /_lam gyi bden pa rab tu ston pa'o/_/sgo bzhi ni bdud bzhi skrag par mdzad pa'o/_/zur bzhi ni tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi rab tu gang ba'o/_/ka ba brgyad
[\[80b.3\]]ni rmi lam lta bu dang dri za'i grong khyer lta bu dang /_brag ca dang sgyu ma'i bdag nyid dang /_smig rgyu dang me long gi gzugs brnyan dang /_chu'i zla ba lta bu dang /_nam mkha'i 'ja' tshon te dngos po dang dngos po med pa'i nyon mongs pa 'joms pa'i phyir ro/_/nang gi rtog pa 'joms pa ni dra ba phyed
[\[80b.4\]]pa'o/_/rta babs bzhi ni sbyin pa dang snyan par smra ba dang /_don mthun pa dang don dpyod pa dang ldan zhing bab tu spang ba bzhi dang ldan pa'o/_/gshin rje gshed dmar sgrub pa'i thabs/_/byas pa'i bsod nams gang bsags pa/_/de yis 'gro ba ma lus kun/_/bdud bzhi las ni thar bar shog_/gshin rje gshed dmar _

[\[80b.7\]]bshad bzhin 'grub pa na/_/shin tu dad dang ldan pa yi/_/slob ma rjes su gzung bar bya/_/khrus sogs sngon 'gro bgegs bskrad la/_/thun mong pa dang khyad par gyi/_/yongs su rdzogs pa'i sdom pa sbyin/_/rang snying la gnas dbyug pa dkar/_/rdo rjes mtshan pa bsgom par
[\[81a\]]
[\[81a.1\]]bya/_/sna tshogs spros pa'i yid 'di nyid/_/spros dang bral bar gdod nas grub/_/spros dang spros med gzhan min phyir/_/zung du 'jug pa'i sems bskyed bya/_/oM badzra yo ga tsit+ta ut+pA da yA mi su ra ta sa ma ya s+t+waM ho/_/de nas 'jom dpal 'dus pa yi/_/dkyil
[\[81a.2\]]'khor cho ga la gsungs ltar/_/'byung ba lnga dang phung lnga la/_/gnas pa'i nyon mongs lnga sbyangs nas/_/bde gshegs lnga dang ye shes lnga/_/dbang bar byed pa dbang lnga sbyin /_/de nas bsrub dang bsrubs pa yi/_/bde ba thig le'i man ngag bya/_/rdo rjes rnam rtog gzhom pa
[\[81a.3\]]yi/_/g.yo 'dzin rlung gi man ngag dbab/_/de yi 'og tu zab mo ni/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs kyi gsang /_/mkha' 'gro'i bka' yis gdams gyur pa/_/rnam rtog 'od gsal zhal las gzung /_/de ni nam zhig rtogs gyur pas/_/skad cig nyid la ye shes 'char/_/grol

[\[81a.5\]]gsal bar byas pa gang yin des ni srid pa gsum bo'i 'ching ba kun/_/spangs nas srid gsum bde chen ro gcig dpal ldan las 'bras kun gzigs pa/_/zhi las 'jam dbyangs shin tu khros pa gshin rje gshed dpal thob gyur cig_/dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i

[\[81b.1\]]ngo bo nyid/_/spros pa'i dri mas gos pa'i/_/bla ma rdo rje can zhabs 'dud/_/'jig rten gsum na rnyed dka' ba/_/bla ma mchog gi bka' drin gyis/_/skad cig nyid la 'char ba ni/_/bla ma nye bar bsten par bshad/_/shin tu 'jigs pa'i 'dur khrod
[\[81b.2\]]du/_/'jig rten chos la ltos med pa'i/_/rnam rtog kun spangs dpa' bos ni/_/dogs pa med par bsgrub par bya/_/blo gros mchog ldan sgrub ba pa pos/_/gza' skar tshes grangs 'dir med de/_/dkyi+el 'khor la sogs lha rnams dang /_/phyi rol bkod pa 'dir mi dgos/_/
[\[81b.3\]]bsam btan bzlas pa yod ma yin/_/sreg blugs dang ni gtor ma med/_/phyag rgya bcings dang 'khrul 'khor sogs/_/phyi rol g.yeng ba kun spangs te/_/brtse ldan gzhan gyi don sems pa/_/bla ma'i byin rlabs la brten nas/_/skad cig nyid la dngos grub 'gyur/_/thog
[\[81b.4\]]mar bla ma lhar bcas la/_/man+Dal dbus zhing mchod gsol gdab/_/gsang sngags rgyal po rjes dran nas/_/sems ni dag cing las rung 'gyur/_/bla ma rang ni rdo rje sems/_/tha dad par ni mi bya ste/_/bla ma sangs rgyas chos dang ni/_/de bzhin dge 'dun bla ma ste/_/dngos grub go
[\[81b.5\]]'phang mchog 'dod pas/_/kun nas bla ma mnyes par bya/_/sangs rgyas kun dngos rdo rje 'chang /_/rtsod pa'i dus 'dir bdag don du/_/kun dang mthun par ston mdzad pa/_/de ltar shes nas dngos kun gyi/_/bsten bya dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi/_/dngos grub rgya chen snod du 'gyur/_/

[\[82a.1\]]yang med pa ste/_/'di ni mchog gtu bde chen nyid/_/'di nyid gsal zhing stong pa nyid/_/'di las mtshon te shes pa bya/_/'di ni rang bzhin sku gsum dang /_/yi shes lnga yi bdag nyid can/_/sems can rnams ni sangs rgyas nyid /_/sangs rgyas gzhan du bstan

[\[82a.6\]]nad dang sdug bsngal gyis mi gos/_/'dis ni bdud dang nyon mongs 'joms/_/'joms byed bcom ldan 'das zhas bya/_/de las gzhan pa gang yin pa/_/chos kun gnyen por mi 'gyur te/_/thams cad rtog pa yin phyir ro/_/rtog pa'i 'ching bas 'ching bar 'gyur/_/de nyid
[\[82a.7\]]rnal 'byor pas shes nas/_/phyi dang nang dang gzhan rnams kyi/_/spros pa'i dra ba rnam par bcad/_/yul gyi 'dzin pa rnam par bshig_/stong ba nyid la gtad legs na/_/rtog pa'i dra ba spong bar 'gyur/_/rten dang brtan pa rnam par dbye/_/mnyam par bzhag pa goms par bya/_/

[\[82b.1\]]de nas byang chub sems bskyed pa'i/_/bla ma'i man dag bshad par bya/_/bla ma rdo rje 'chang gi sku/_/'og min bde chen der bsgoms te/_/mi phyed bsams pas gsol ba gdab/_/mthar phyin tshe na rang la bstim/_/thog med brtse bas bskyangs pa yi/_/drin can rnams la snying rje
[\[82b.2\]]bsam/_/gnod byed 'di rnams bdag gi ma/_/sngon tshe yang yang phan btags kyang /_/smyon pa bzhin du rang dbang med/_/mi dge'i las kyis mnar med 'gyur/_/de ltar dran pas srid gsum la/_/snying rje mthar phyin 'gyur ba yin/_/phyi nang spyod pa mi srun pas/_/blo gros shin
[\[82b.3\]]tu 'khrugs pa'i tshe/_/bdag dang gzhan du brje ba yi/_/byang chub sems ni dran par bya/_/dus ni bdud dang nyom mongs tshogs/_/'joms shing spros med nyid du 'gyur/_/srog 'gag pa yi sbyor ba yis/_/goms par byed pa'i rnal 'byor bas/_/ji ltar rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyis/_/
[\[82b.4\]]lus 'di rnam dag sbyar bar bya/_/dgang ba'i sbyor bas spyi gtsug nas/_/rkang mthil bar du dgang byas la/_/rngub pa'i sbyor bas zhi bar bya/_/dang par srub cing bsrub bar bya/_/gnyis pa rgya mtsho bskyod pa ste/_/gsum pa bsad pa nor lha gnyis/_/bzhi pa yan lag brkyang bskum
[\[82b.5\]]'di/_/phyigs bzhi g.yo zhing srid gsum bsgrags/_/'di yi sbyor bas goms byas na/_/nad kun las ni grol 'gyur zhing /_/'di ltar rgud dang rgas pa dang /_/'chi bdag thag ring kun rtog 'joms/_/srid pa'i 'ching ba las grol zhong /_/spros med ye shes go 'phang
[\[82b.6\]]'thob/_/dag pa'i bzhi mnyam blang byas te/_/gla rtsi yis ni dug med 'gyur/_/gany+dzi dang ni ba rung /_/sga skya dang ni lhan cig byas/_/bu ram mar dang sbrang rtsir bcas/_/gsang sngags bzlas shing zhag bdun bsgrub/_/dam tshig brtan ldan rnal 'byor pas/_/nang par dus
[\[82b.7\]]su bsnyen pa bya/_/skra dkar gnyer ma la sogs spang /_/dbang po rnams ni mchog tu gsal/_/lus kyi mdog rgyas zo mdog bde/_/mkha' 'gro rnams kyis byin gyis rlobs/_/bde ba chen po'i ting 'dzin dang /_/spros med ye shes go 'phang 'thob/_/rdo rje 'jig byed
[\[83a\]]
[\[83a.1\]]sbyor ba yis/_/rgyal ba'i tshogs su mnyes byas te/_/snying gi kun rdzob sna rtse nas/_/sor bzhi bcal nas dbu mar gzhug_/nor bu'i bar du srog 'dzin pa/_/steng gi dag pas zin pa yin/_/phyag na rdo rje gzung bya ste/_/g.yas pa'i mthil gyis bum pa sbyor/_/

[\[83a.3\]]pas bar chod sel/_/rnal 'byor 'dil sgrub pa ngos/_/du bar sogs mngon shes so/_/rnam rtog dra ba ma lus gcod/_/shin tu spros med go 'phang thob/_/sgrub po'i lam gyi gegs byed pa/_/bar du gcod pa des la ba/_/phyi rol bdud kyis dkrugs pa dang /_/lus la
[\[83a.4\]]sems dang rang rig dang /_/nad dang sdug bsngal rabs pa yis/_/bar du gtsod pa phal cher la/_/sngar gyi man ngag sgoms pa yis/_/mkha' la sprin tshegs 'khrigs pa la/_/mi bzad rung gis bskyod pa bzhin/_/gzhan yang bdud kyi bar chad gang /_/spros med de nyid dbyings
[\[83a.5\]]su bstim/_/rten dang brten pa so sor bya/_/'dzin pa nyid la gtang par bya/_/de ltar goms pas spros med 'gyur/_/dga' dang bde ba dang ba yis/_/phye dang gsang ba mtshan par bya/_/blo yi rtog pa ma zhin/_/sems can lam gyi dpa' bskyed la/_/til mar dar btags ral gri
[\[83a.6\]]bzhin/_/thogs pa chad par gzhim par bya/_/shin tu spros med dru ma'i gsung /_/bla yo yul du gam san yang /_/spros pa rtsub mos bskyod ba'i tshe/_/dro la spros med kyis la rig_/blo ni phal par brtan par gnas/_/de tshe spros pa spros med du/_/ro gcig mnyam pa nyid du thim/_/
[\[83a.7\]]'dred pa srin po 'jigs pa'i chogs/_/dur khro nga ro langs la sogs pa/_/'khun dung rang bab shugs pa 'bod/_/'jig pa rnam pa sna tshogs ba/_/sems las ma gtogs gzhan med pas/_/rang sems skar mda' 'pho ba ltar/_/de yi snying la thim pa yis/_/blo dang zhan
[\[83b\]]
[\[83b.1\]]dang spros med rnams/_/spros med yi shes nyid du 'gyur/_/yang na blo de nyid la gtang /_/bdag gi gces de mchod spyan bya/_/mi bzad gdon dang 'go ba'i nad/_/sdig pa'i rmi lam 'pho ba sogs/_/gza' dang rgyu skar gdon la sogs/_/nad dang mya ngan sdug bsngal dang /_/dgra dang
[\[83b.2\]]'byung ba'i gnod pa bya/_/mi dang mi ma yin pa yis/_/nye bar 'tshe ba sna tshogs pa/_/thag pa'i sbrul ni sangs pa bzhin/_/skyug bro ba dang gtsang sbra dang /_/'dzem bag dang ni ngo tsha dang /_/spros med yi shes kyis gzhom bya/_/bla ma 'dod ltar bsgrub bya ste/_/dga' dang bde dang rangs pa
[\[83b.3\]]dang /_/tshim dang nga rgyal dregs pa dang /_/sgeg dang tshul 'chos rgyan la sogs/_/spros med yi shes ngo bo nyid/_/zhum dang sgyid lug mi mthun phyogs/_/thams cad spros med nyid du 'gyur/_/mi bzad nyon mongs gang yin pa/_/spros med de nyid las gzhan yin/_/de ltar bgrod dang
[\[83b.4\]]bgrang min pa/_/yid du 'ong dang mo 'ong ba/_/shin tu spros med sems kyis ni/_/zhen pa nyid du mi bya'o/_/'jig rten rnams dang mthun pa yi/_/rnam gzhag hrul po bshigs nas kyang /_/dogs pa med pas sems kyis ni/_/dpa' bo seng ge bzhin du spyod/_/de las yon tan
[\[83b.5\]]phun sum tshogs/_/dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin par 'gyur/_/e ma zhi ba chen pa'i chos/_/e ma khro bo 'jigs mdzad pa/_/e ma mya ngan 'das pa mchog_/e ma 'khor bzhi ba nyid/_/e ma 'di ni rab tu mtshar/_/skyon ni gang yin yon tan 'gyur/_/byang chub sems ni mngon
[\[83b.6\]]rtogasabyed/_/dngos po min zhing sgom pa min/_/khams kyang min zhing rnam shes min/_/nam mkha'i dkyil dang mtshungs pa nyid/_/nam mkha' lta bur bdag med ba/_/chos 'di bde ba chen po'o/_/sa yang ma yin chu yang min/_/me min rlung min nam mkha' min/_/rdo rjes
[\[83b.7\]]rims pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/skye ba 'di la rab tu gnas/_/dngos po thams cad dngos med bshad/_/dngos po med ces ma bsgrags pa/_/rnal 'byor sbyor ba dang bral zhing /_/chad pa ma yin rtag pa min/_/yan lag med cing kha dog med/_/thog ma dbus dang mtha' yang spangs//
[\[84a\]]
[\[84a.1\]]dngos po thams cad med par 'gyur/_/mchog tu dga' ba'i mtshan nyid do/_/bsod nams sdig pa dag dang ma 'brel ba/_/mchog tu dga' ba dri med dag pa yi/_/dgon po de nyid gter chen gcig pu ste/_/kun kyang snying rje'i sems nyid mgon 'di yod/_/chos
[\[84a.2\]]rnams ngo bo bde ba chen po'i mchog/_/mchog tu lhan cig skyes dga'i ngo bo ni/_/gzugs med bsod nams med cing sdig pa med/_/skye dang 'gag pa yod pa ma yin no/_/de ltar bla ma'i drin gyis rang nyid yid ches dran phyir gsal byed pa/_/de la nongs gyur dpal ldan bla ma lha mo
[\[84a.3\]]rnams la bzod par gsol/_/rgyal ba sras bcas thugs kyi gsang 'di legs par bkod pa yis/_/bsod nams gang skyes de yis 'gro kun rdo rje 'dzin gyur cig/_/shin tu spros pa med pa'i de kho na nyid gyi man ngag ces bya ba/_slob dpon dpal ldan mthu stobs kyi mgon po thugs
[\[84a.4\]]spros pa med pa'i dbyings las ma g.yos bzhin du/_/sku'i spros pa dpag tu med pas gdug pa can tshar gcod cing /_bcom ldan 'das kyis dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po'i rlabs mdzad pa rdzogs so/_/bstan pa srung ba'i lha rnams
[\[84a.5\]]kyis bu gcig pa ltar bskyangs pas rgyal po gzhan gyi rgol bas glags lta bar mi nus pa'i ljongs chos kyi rgyal po'i sku mkhar nyi ma gzugs su rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Dita dngos grub brnyes pa dang la rban A tsAr+ya dang /_glo bo'i tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur cing
[\[84a.6\]]zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ {D2021}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_rak+ta ya mA ri sA d+ha na bi d+hi/_bod skad du/_gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs kyi cho ga_/dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po la phyag 'tshal lo/_/oM hrIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na hUM hUM phaT phaT swAhA/

[\[102a.2\]]sha'i steng du nyal du gzhug ste/_rmi lam gang cung zad mthong ba snga dro nga la sgos shig ces bya'o/_/gal te mi dge ba'i mtshan ma smra na/_de'i tshe las thams cad pa'i sngags kyis gzhom mo/_/slar de rnams yang dag par bsrungs ma sdom pa 'dzin du gzhug ste/_'khor
[\[102a.3\]]lo phyir mi ldog pa'i dbang /_dam pa dag la stsal nas ni/_/mgon po 'khor lo lha dag gis/_/de nyid slob dpon phrin las dang /_/sangs rgyas kun gyi dam tshig dang /_/sdom pa gsang mchog rtag tu ni/_/sems can kun gyi don bgyid phyir/_/slob dpon dag 'gyur
[\[102a.4\]]gsung du gsol/_/zhes brjod du bcug nas sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad bdag la dgongs su gsol/_bdag che ge mo zhes bya ba dus 'di nas bzung ste/_ji srid snying po byang chub la mchis kyi bar du/_ji ltar dus gsum mgon po rnams/_/byang
[\[102a.5\]]chub tu ni nges mdzad pa'i/_/byang chub sems ni bla med pa/_/dam pa bdag gis bskyed par bgyi/_/tshul khrims bslab pa rnam pa gsum/_/dge ba yi ni chos sdud dang /_/sems can don byed tshul khrims ni/_/bdag gis so sor brtan por bzung /_/sangs rgyas
[\[102a.6\]]chos dang dge 'dun te/_/dkon mchog gsum mchog bla na med/_/sdom pa sangs rgyas rnal 'byor byung /_/deng nas brtsams te gzung bar bgyi/_/rdo rje chen po'i rigs bsdus pa/_/rdo rje dril bu'i phyag rgya yang /_/de nyid kyis ni rab tu gzung /_/slob dpon dag
[\[102a.7\]]kyang gzung bar bgyi/_/rin chen chen po'i rigs mchog gi_/dam tshig yid du 'ong ba la/_/nyin re bzhin du lan drug tu/_/sbyin pa rnam bzhi rtag tu sbyin/_/pad+ma chen po'i rigs dag pas/_/byang chub chen po 'byung ba la/_/phyi dang gsang ba'i theg pa
[\[102b\]]
[\[102b.1\]]gsum/_/dam chos so sor gzung bar bgyi/_/las chen rigs ni bsdus pa la/_/sdom pa thams cad yang dag ldan/_/mchod pa'i las ni ci nus sbyin/_/kun nas so sor gzung bar bgyi/_/sems can kun gyi don bgyid phyir/_/byang chub sems ni bla med pa/_/dam
[\[102b.2\]]pa yang dag bskyed bgyis shing /_/sdom pa ma lus bzung bgyis nas/_/ma rgal ba rnams bsgral bar bgyi/_/ma grol ba rnams bdag gis dgrol/_/dbugs ma phyung ba dbugs dbyung bgyi/_/sems can mya ngan 'das la dgod/_/ces bya ba lan gsum brjod du
[\[102b.3\]]gzhug par bya'o/_/slob dpon gyis sdom pa sbyin pa ste/_slob ma lhag par gnas pa'o/_/de nas dang por slob dpon dang slob ma gzhug pa'i cho gas dkyil 'khor du zhugs te/_dbang thams cad rdzogs par blangs la rjes su gnang ba thob nas/_yol ba'i phyi rol du yon
[\[102b.4\]]phul zhing dbang bskur la/_skal ba dang ldan pa'i slob ma rnam par snang mdzad kyi gzugs su dmigs la/_A khaM bI ra hUM/_zhes pa'i sngags kyis me tog gi phreng ba bzung zhing gdong g.yogs bcings la/_las thams cad pa'i sngags bzlas pa'i chus bsangs la/
[\[102b.5\]]dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa'i don du dri bar bya ste/_kye dga' ba la dga' ba la khyed su yin/_bde chen bdag gi skal bzangs lags/_/zhes pa'o/_/de'i mjug thogs su/_oM sar+b+ba yo ga tsit+ta utrA da yA mi/_zhes pas rnal 'byor gyi sems bskyed par bya'o/_/de nas
[\[102b.6\]]oM su ra te sa ma ya stAM ho sid+hi badzra yathA su khaM/_zhes bya ba 'dis me tog dang bcas pa'i rdo rje snying gar gzhag par bya'o/_/de nas sngar bshad pa'i yi ge lngas yol ba'i nang du bcug la 'di skad ces brjod par byas te/_deng khyed de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs
[\[102b.7\]]su zhugs kyis/_de bas na ngas khyod la rdo rje'i sems bskyed par byas te/_ye shes gang gis khyod de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dngos grub kyang thob par 'gyur na/_dngos grub gzhan rnams lta smos kyang ci dgos/_khyod kyis 'di dkyil 'khor ma mthong ba
[\[103a\]]
[\[103a.1\]]rnams kyi mdun du smra bar mi bya ste/_dam tshig nyams par gyur ta re/_de nas spyi bor rdo rje bzhag la 'di skad ces brjod de/_'di ni rdo rje'i dam tshig ste/_/gal te khyod kyis 'ga' zhig la/_/'di smras na ni spyi bo 'gems/_/de nas snying gar gzhag la/
[\[103a.2\]]de ring rdo rje sems dpa' rang /_/khyod kyi snying la yang dag zhugs/_/gal te tshul 'di smras na ni/_/de ma thag tu dral te gshegs/_/zhes pa 'dis mna' byed du bcug ste/_tsan+dan dang gur kum la sogs pa dang bsres pa'i chu la/_oM badzra u da ka ThaH_zhes bya
[\[103a.3\]]ba'i sngags lan bdun bzlas te/_'di ni khyod kyi dmyal ba'i chu/_/dam tshig nyams na sreg par byed/_/dam tshig bsrungs na dngos grub ste/_/rdo rje bdud rtsi'i chu 'thungs shig_/ces brjod cing 'thung du gzhug go/_/de nas 'di skad ces brjod par byas te/_deng nas
[\[103a.4\]]brtsams te khyod kyi phyag na rdo rje nga yin gyis/_ngas 'di gyis shig ces gang bsgo ba de khyod kyis bya dgos so/_/khyod kyis nga la brnyas par yang mi bya ste/_khyod ya nga ba ma spangs par 'chi ba'i dus byas nas sems can dmyal bar lhang bar gyur ta re zhes so/_/de nas de bzhin
[\[103a.5\]]gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs te/_rdo rje sems dpa' bdag la dbab du gsol zhes brjod du bcug nas/_de'i spyi bor yi ge baM las byung ba'i chu'i dkyil 'khor yongs su zlum po dkar po bum pas mtshan pa der haH'o/_/snying gar laM las byung ba'i dbang
[\[103a.6\]]chen gyi dkyil 'khor gru bzhi pa ser po zur du rdo rje rtse gsum pas mtshan pa de la hUM ngo /_/lte bar ra~M` las byung ba'i me'i dkyil 'khor gru gsum pa dmar po rno zhing 'bar ba de la aH'o/_/rkang pa'i 'og tu yi las byung ba'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor sngon po gzhu'i dbyibs can mtha'
[\[103a.7\]]mar ba dan gyis mtshan pa/_de la dz+haiM drag cing bzod par dka' ba/_'bar ba'i gzugs can rlung gis bskyod bzhin par bsam ste/_ji srid me'i dkyil 'khor gzhan dang mnyam par phyin nas/_de yang des bskyod pas shin tu drag cing 'bar bas dbang chen gyi dkyil
[\[103b\]]
[\[103b.1\]]'khor 'bar bar gyur te/_de las chu'i dkyil 'khor las bdud rtsi'i tshogs 'bar bas tshim par gyur pa'i slob ma rlung gis 'degs pa dang /_rang nyid bsnyems pa dang bcas pa'i khro bo gshin rje 'joms byed kyi sku mi bzad pa/_phyag g.yas kyis rdo rje gsor zhing g.yon
[\[103b.2\]]pas dril bu dkrol bar spos dbul zhing 'bebs pa'i sngags kyis dbab par bya'o /_/de la sngags ni 'di yin te/_oM d+hIHSh+T+r-iHwi kr-i tA na na hUM hUM phaT phaT/_A be sha ya staM b+ha ya ra ra ra ra tsA la ya tsA la ya hUM haHaHdz+hi hUM phaT/_ces bya ba 'dis myur du phebs so/_/de nas
[\[103b.3\]]'dod chags gshin rje gshed kyi gzugs su skad cig gis dmigs la de'i lce la aHdmar po bsgoms te/_tiSh+Tha badzra zhes brjod la/_mgon po rdo rje chos chen po/_/snang ba mtha' yas bde ba che/_/smros shig 'dod chags chos chen po/_/dge dang mi dge legs par
[\[103b.4\]]'dri/_/zhes pa 'dis dri bar bya'o/_/de yang babs na gsung babs pas dge ba dang mi dge ba smra'o/_/thugs babs na/_'jig rten gsum du gtogs pa shes so/_/sku babs pas nam mkha' la 'phar ro/_/de'i tshe de'i mgo bo'i steng du lo las byung ba dbang chen gyi dkyil
[\[103b.5\]]'khor sna tshogs rdo rjes mtshan pas de mnan par bsgoms na mi 'gul bar 'gyur ro/_/dbab pa'o/_/de nas bzung ba'i me tog pra tIts+tsha badzra hoH_zhes pas 'khor lor dor ro/_/lha gang gi mtshan ma'am/_nye ba'i sa gzhi las lhung ba de'i rigs su de bstan par bya'o/_/
[\[103b.6\]]gnas mchog la babs na dngos grub mchog go/_/gnas dkyil la 'breng ngo /_/gnas tha ma la ni tha ma'o/_/dkyil 'khor gyi phyi rol du lhang na dngos grub med de/_gal te dkyil 'khor gyi phyi rol tu lhung na de'i tshe slar dor bar bya'o/_/lan gsum byas nas de nyid du gal te
[\[103b.7\]]ma lhung na de'i tshe dbyung bar bya'o/_/me tog dor ba'o/_/de nas dor ba'i me tog gi phreng ba blangs la/_de'i mgo la bcing bar byas te/_pra ti gr-ih+Na staM i baM satwa ma hA ba la/_zhes brjod byung de nas/_oM de ring rdo rje sems dpa' rang /_khyed kyi mig ni 'byed par brtson/_/rdo rje'i
[\[104a\]]
[\[104a.1\]]mig ni bla med pa/_/thams cad mig ni 'byed par mdzad/_/ces brjod cing gdong g.yogs dgrol lo/_/de nas dkyil 'khor gyi lha rnams kyi so so'i mtshan brjod pa sngon du 'gro bas shar gyi sgo skyong nas brtsams nas gtso bo'i bar du bstan par bya'o/_/
[\[104a.2\]]zhes pa ni dkyil 'khor du gzhug pa'o/_/de nas/_sangs rgyas shes rab chen po yis/_/rdo rje sems dpa' dbang bskur ltar/_/bdag kyang mgon pos dbang bskur zhing /_/mchog kyang bdag la stsal du gsol/_/zhes bya bas gsol ba btab pa dang ldan pa'i slob ma la rdo rje
[\[104a.3\]]tsartsi ka la sogs pa'i bum pa bzung bas dbang bskur bar bsgom zhing /_dbang bskur rdo rje chen po ni/_/khams gsum pa yis phyag byas pa/_/sangs rgyas rnams ni thams cad kyi/_/gsang gsum gnas byung sbyin par bya/_/zhes brjod de las thams cad pa bzlas pa'i
[\[104a.4\]]bum pa nas rdo rje dang bcas pa'i khu tshur gyis chu blangs la/_oM badzra a b+hi Shiny+tsa mi/_zhes brjod cing 'khor los sgyur ba bzhin du bkra shis kyi glu sngon du 'go bas dbang bskur bar bya'o/_/'di ni chu'i dbang ngo /_/de'i mjug thogs su gser dang gos la sogs pa las
[\[104a.5\]]byas pa'i cod pan sngar brjod pa'i sngags kyis mgo bo la bzhag nas nam mkha'i dkyil na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi bdag po'i gzugs kyi cod pan la bzhugs par bsgom par bya'o/_/'di ni cod pan gyi dbang ngo /_/de'i rjes la rdo rje gzung ste/
[\[104a.6\]]sangs rgyas kun gyi rdo rje yi/_/dbang gis de ring khyod dbang bskur/_/'di de sangs rgyas thams cad nyid/_/rdo rje rab tu grub phyir zung /_/zhes brjod de rdo rjes snying ga la sogs par reg la rdo rje lag pa g.yas su sbyin par bya'o/_/'di ni rdo rje'i dbang ngo /_/de nas slob ma'i lag
[\[104a.7\]]pa g.yon du dril bu byin la/_rdo rje dang dril bu gnyis dang ldan pa'i lag pa dag 'khyud pa'i tshul byed du bcug la/_oM badzra a ng+hi pa ti two a b+hi Shiny+tsa mi tiSh+Tha badzra sa ma ya s+t+waM zhes brjod la sbyin par bya'o/_/dril bu'i dbang bskur ba nyid la bdag po'i dbang bskur ba zhes
[\[104b\]]
[\[104b.1\]]byas so/_/de nas rdo rje dang dril bu mgo bor bzung la/_oM badzra satwa s+t+waMa b+hi Shiny+tsa mi badzra nA ma/_a b+hi She ka te sa ma ya s+t+waM/_kye dpal che ge mo rdo rje zhes pa la sogs pa rigs dang rjes su mthun pa'i ming gdags so/_/dbang bskur 'di dag bya ba dang /_spyod pa'i rgyud
[\[104b.2\]]bshad pa dang /_sngags sgrub pa la dbang bar 'gyur ro/_/dbang lnga po 'di nyid cod pan gyi dbang ste/_thams cad du tsartsi ka la sogs pa rnams cod pan la dbang gi tshul du bya ba'i phyir ro/_/de nas cod pan gyi dbang la sogs pa bzung zhing slob dpon gyi sdom pa gzung ba'i
[\[104b.3\]]slob mas/_gang gis bdag ni khyod drin las/_/rang dang gzhan don nus 'gyur ba/_/rdo rje slob dpon gyi ni dbang /_/snying brtse'i gter gyi bdag la stsol/_/zhes pas gsol ba btab pa dang /_ldan pa'i slob ma dkyil 'khor gyi drung du/_rdul tshon dkar po'i pad+ma
[\[104b.4\]]'dab brgyad byas pa'i steng du shing stan la bzhag pa rdo rje tsartsi ka la sogs pa rnams kyis snga ma bzhin du dbang bskur te/_dam tshig gsum 'dzin du bcug nas so/_/de la dam tshig gsum ni 'di yin te/_rdo rje yi ge hUM las rdo rjer bsgoms la/_khams gsum pa yi
[\[104b.5\]]ral gri che/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis phyag byas la/_/las kyi ral gri mchog lta bu/_/bdud las rgyal bar bya phyir zung /_/zhes pas de kho na nyid kyi rdo rje 'dzin du gzhug go zhes pas/_rdo rje'i dam tshig go/_/de nas yi ge a las skyes pa'i dril bu/_shes rab thabs kyi
[\[104b.6\]]rang bzhin khyod/_/rdo rje dril bu rab grub phyir/_/bu yis yang dag gus pas zung /_/khyod kyis slob ma bsdu bar gyis/_/zhes pa 'dis de'i lag par byin no/_/srid pa ngo bo nyid kyis dag_/ngo bo nyid kyis srid bral byas/_/rang bzhin dag mchog sems dpa' yi/_/dam pa'i
[\[104b.7\]]srid pa byed par 'gyur/_/zhes pa 'dis de dag kyang dgrol bar bya'o zhes bya ba/_'di ni dril bu'i dam tshig go/_/de'i mjug thogs su/_yid kyis lus brtan de nyid kyis/_/phyag rgya'i dam tshig rab tu bshad/_/gang gis lus ni thams cad brten/_/de nas phyag rgya
[\[105a\]]
[\[105a.1\]]rab tu bsgrags/_/'di yis rang gis 'dod pa'i lha'i bdag nyid phyag rgya chen por byin gyis brlab po zhes bya ba phyag rgya chen po'i dam tshig go/_/de nas dkyil 'khor gyi de kho na nyid dang /_lha'i de kho na nyid dang slob dpon gyi las dang /_dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa dang /

[\[105a.3\]]mtshungs pa nyid kyis dad pa de'i rnam par dag pa ni shar gyi sgo'o/_/mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa dang ma skyes pa dang /_spong ba dang mi bskyed pa dang /_de bzhin du dge ba'i chos skyes pa dang /_ma skyes pa dag gnas dang bskyed pa'i phyir rtsom pa dang /_las dang so sor rtogs pa
[\[105a.4\]]dang /_bdag nyid dbang du bya ba ste/_brtson 'grus bzhi rnam par dag pa lho'i sgo'o/_/'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang /_sems dang dpyod pa ste/_rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la dran pa gang yin/_de'i rnam par dag pas nub kyi sgo'o/_/dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang /_dran
[\[105a.5\]]pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang /_shes rab ste dbang po lnga rnams la gang bsam gtan pa de'i rnam par dag pas byang sgo'o/_/rtog pa dang dpyod pa dang /_dga' ba dang bde ba dang /_sems rtse gcig pa nyid ces bya bas bsam gtan dang po'i yan lag lnga dang /_rtog pa dang
[\[105a.6\]]dpyod pa spangs pa'i bsam gtan gnyis pa dang /_dga' ba yang spangs shing btang stoms dang dran pa yang dag par ldan pa'i bsam gtan gsum pa dang /_btang snyoms dang dran pa yongs su dag pas sdug bsngal yang ma yin/_tshor ba bde ba yang ma yin pa'i bsam gtan
[\[105a.7\]]bzhi pa ste/_'di rnams kyi rnam par dag pas rta babs bzhi'o/_/dpa' bar 'gro ba dang nam mkha' mdzod dang /_dri ma med pa dang /_seng ge rnam par rtse ba'i ting nge 'dzin bzhi rnam par dag pas stegs bu bzhi'o/_/don dang tshig dang nges pa'i tshig dang /_spobs pa ste /
[\[105b\]]
[\[105b.1\]]gzungs bzhi rnam par dag pas stegs bu la gnas pa'i lha mo'i tshogs so/_/bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par spras pa'o/_/mdo dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa dang /_lung bstan pa dang /_tshigs su bcad pa dang /_ched du brjod pa dang /

[\[105b.3\]]dran pa dang chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa dang /_brtson 'grus dang dga' ba dang /_shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms zhes bya ba byang chub kyi yan lag bdun rnam par dag pas/_dra ba dang dra ba phyed pa dang /_me long dang /_me tog phreng ba dang /_rnam par bkra ba
[\[105b.4\]]dang /_rnga yab 'bar ba'o/_/nang gzugs su 'du shes shing phyi rol gyi gzugs rnams stong pa nyid dang /_mtshan ma med pa dang smon pa med pa'i rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa dang po dang /_phyi rol gyi gzugs med par 'du shes shing nang gi gzugs rnams la de bzhin du

[\[106a.1\]]dang mnyam par ldan pa'o/_/rigs kyi dbye bas 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i ri'i rtse mo mthon po nyi shu 'byed pa'i sna tshogs rdo rje'i rtse mo nyi shu'o/_/rten dang brten pa'i dbye bas kha dog lnga pa'i rtsig pa dang thog go/_/gos pa med pa'i chos gcig dang /_/du ma

[\[106a.7\]]rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs pas sems can gyi don rgyun mi 'chad par mdzad pa'i bsam pa nyid kyis bla na med pa'i lhan cig skyes pa'i ngo bos chos kyi sku yin yang /_longs spyod rdzogs pa'i dang /_sprul pa gnyis su med pa'i sku'i rnam pa'o/_/gzugs kyi phung bo dang
[\[106b\]]

[\[111a.3\]]cung zad med/_/ma 'khrul bla ma'i bka' drin gyis/_/gdod nas grub par shes bya ste/_/lus can kun gyis 'di mthong dang /_/gang gis thos dang dran tsam gyis/_/bsam pa rdzogs mdzad zung 'jug sku/_/de ltar bdag nyid gsal bar blta/_/bdag gi thugs ka'i sa bon las/_/
[\[111a.4\]]sa gsum 'od zer rab 'phros nas/_/mthong thos dran pa'i spyod yul du/_/ma lus lus pa med pa yin/_/brtan g.yo'i dngos po ji snyed pa/_/dpal ldan gshin rje gshegs dmar po/_/khams gsum min 'di gzhal med khang /_/srog chags min 'di rgyal ba rnams/_/phung po khams dang
[\[111a.5\]]skye mched min/_/khams gsum min 'di dkyil 'khor pa/_/rang bzhin 'od gsal ngo bo nyid/_/me long nang gi gzugs brnyan ltar/_/sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin/_/rmi lam ji bzhin goms byas te/_/bar ma'i srid pa rab spyor bas/_/de bzhin gshegs pa'i dngos grub thob/_/dbyibs
[\[111a.6\]]kyi rim pa ste rnal 'byor ro/_/lus can rnams kyi srog gyur pa/_/rlung zhes bya ba las kun byed/_/'di ni rnam shes bzhon pa ste/_/srid dang rnam grol thob byed pa'o/_/bya dra dang ni b+ha ra ta/_/mu sa la dang a tra tas/_/thog mar lus ni sbyang bar bya/_/lus sbyangs pas ni rtsa dang

[\[182a.1\]]'gro ba thams cad 'dren pa ste ye shes sems dpa'o/_/rang rgyal zhes pa ni rten 'brel bcu gnyis lugs las bzlog pa'i tshul gyis bsgom pa'i gang zag ste shes rab che ba dang /_slob dpon 'di bdag 'chad pa dang 'gro ba'i don la mi dga' ba'i gang zag go/_/

[\[188a.3\]]ye shes mig gcig dri ma med/_/ces pa ni ye shes kyi spyan dang ldan pa'i longs sku ste/_dri ma med ces pa theg pa chen po ston pa'o/_/ye shes lus can de bzhin gshegs pa sprul pa'i sku ste/_tshig gi dbang phyug smra ba che/_/zhes pa ni drang don gyi tshig la mkhas pa'o/_/smra ba'i
[\[188a.4\]]skyes mchog smra ba'i rgyal/_/zhes pa ni nges pa'i don gyi tshig la mkhas pa'o/_/smra ba'i dam pa mchog gi gnas/_/zhes pa ni drang don nges don gnyis la mkhas pa'o/_/smra ba'i seng ge zhes pa ni gang zag gis kyang zil gyis mi non pa'o/_/mtshungs pa med ces pa ni 'gran zla med
[\[188a.5\]]pa'o/_/kun du zhes pa ni 'gro ba la'o/_/mchog tu dga' zhes pa bde ba bskyed pa'o/_/gzi brjid phung po blta na sdug_/ces pa ni yid du 'ong ba'o/_/'od bzang 'bar ba dpal gyi be'u/_/zhes pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i thugs so/_/lag na 'od 'bar snang ba po/_/zhes pa ni
[\[188a.6\]]sku'i cha lugs 'gro ba la ston pa'o/_/sman pa che mchog dang 'dra bar 'gro ba'i zug rngu 'byin pas bla na med pa'o/_/sman rnams ma lus ljon pa'i shing /_/zhes pa ni chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong ngo /_/nad do cog ces pa ni nyon mongs pa brgyad khri bzhi stong ngo /_/dgra che ba ni 'joms
[\[188a.7\]]par byed pa'o/_/sdug gu 'jig rten gsum gyi mchog_/ces pa ni 'jig rten gsum gyi 'dul byed du gyur pa'o/_/dpal ldan rgyu skar dkyil 'khor zhes pa ni dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi dkyil 'khor gyi sgo nas 'gro ba'i don byed pa'o/_/phyogs bcu'i zhes pa ni gnas so/_/nam mkha'i
[\[188b\]]
[\[188b.1\]]zhes pa ni rgya'o/_/mthar thug pa zhes pa ni dus so/_/rgya de srid du/_chos kyi rgyal mtshan legs par 'dzugs/_/zhes pa ste gdul bya rnams dge ba la dgod do zhes pa'i don to/_/'gro na zhes pa ni 'gro ba rnams so/_/gdugs gcig ces pa ni tha dad kyis gdung ba'i tshad pa las skyob pa'o/_/
[\[188b.2\]]gcig ces pa ni 'gran zla med pa'o/_/yangs pa zhes pa ni kun la khyab pa'o/_/byams pa zhes pa ni sems can thams cad bde ba dang ldan par 'dod pa'o/_/snying rje zhes pa ni 'gro ba thams cad sdug bsngal dang bral bar 'dod pa'o/_/dkyil 'khor can zhes pa de gnyis dang mi
[\[188b.3\]]'bral ba'o/_/dpal ldan zhes pa ni gzugs sku gnyis so/_/pad+ma zhes pa skyon gyis ma gos pa'o/_/gar gyi bdag ces pa dper na gar ji ltar byas kyang lus las mi gzhan pa de bzhin du ye shes sems dpa' de yang mdzad spyod ci mdzad kyang 'gro ba'i don las mi 'da' ba'o/_/
[\[188b.4\]]khyab bdag chen po ni bshad zin to/_/rin chen ni 'dod dgu 'byung ba'o/_/gdugs zhes pa ni gdung ba las skyob pa'o/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi gzi brjid che/_/zhes pa ni kun la snang ba'o/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi sku 'chang ba/_/zhes pa ni sku gsum dang ldan pa'o/_/sangs rgyas
[\[188b.5\]]kun gyi rnal 'byor che/_/zhes pa ni bden pa ya ma bral ba'o/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi bstan pa gcig_/ces pa ni skye ba med pa'i ngo bor gcig pa'o/_/rdo rje rin chen zhes pa ni rin po che'i dbu rgyan dang rdo rje thod dang ldan pas na dbang bskur dpal zhes bya'o/_/rin chen kun bdag dbang

[\[188b.7\]]rgyas kun gyi thugs che ba/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs la gnas/_/zhes pa ni phyag na rdo rje'i ngo bo bshad pa'o/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi sku che ba/_/zhes pa ni 'jam dpal gyi ngo bo bshad pa'o/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung yang yin/_/zhes pa ni spyan ras gzigs kyi ngo bo bshad
[\[189a\]]
[\[189a.1\]]pa'o/_/rdo rje nyi ma snang ba che/_/rdo rje zla ba dri med 'od/_/ces pa ni bklag pa'i thabs te thabs dang shes rab kyi ngo bo bshad pa'o/_/bklag pa'i thabs ni gnyis te dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i tshul du gdon pa dang /_lha rkyang ba'i tshul du gdon pa'o/_/dkyil

[\[189a.4\]]kha dog sna tshogs zhes pa ni theg pa sna tshogs kyis 'gro ba'i don byed pa'o/_/rdo rje zhes pa ni stong pa nyid kyi don to/_/skyil krung zhes pa ni stong pa nyid la mnyam par gzhag pa'o/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas zhes pa ni de'i sgo nas mya ngan las 'das pa thob pa'o/_/sangs rgyas 'gro ba'i

[\[189a.6\]]so/_/rgyal po zhes pa ni 'khor 'das kyi gtso bor gyur pa'o/_/sgyu 'phrul sna tshogs zhes pa ni thabs du ma dang ldan pa'o/_/chos zhes pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang /_stobs dang mi 'jigs pa la sogs pa dang ldan pa'o/_/de lta bu de su la ldan zhe na/
[\[189a.7\]]sangs rgyas rig sngags 'chang zhes smos te/_spong ba phun sum tshogs pa dang /_ye shes phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa'i ye shes sems dpa' la ldan zhes pa'i don to/_/rdo rje rnon po ral gri che/_/zhes pa ni rtags dang don to/_/rtags ni g.yas pa'i phyag mtshan ral gri'o/_/
[\[189b\]]
[\[189b.1\]]don ni rdo rje ste stong pa nyid do/_/rnon po ni rtog pa ma lus pa gcod pa'o/_/stong pa nyid kyi don de ral gri dang 'dra bas na ral gri'o/_/thogs zhes pa ni 'chang ba'i don to/_/yi ge mchog ste rnam par dag_/ces pa yang rtags dang don to/_/rtags ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i
[\[189b.2\]]po ti bsnams pa'o/_/don ni yi ge mchog ces pa ste a'o/_/rnam par dag ces pa ni skye ba med pa'o/_/theg pa chen po zhes pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'o/_/sdug bsngal gcod ces pa ni 'khor ba las sgrol ba'o/_/mtshon cha chen po zhes pa ni ral
[\[189b.3\]]gri'o/_/rdo rje chos zhes pa ni po ti'o/_/rdo rje zab mo zhes pa ni thugs so/_/dzi na zhes pa ni gsung ngo /_/dzika ces pa ni sku'o/_/rdo rje blo gros zhes pa ni stong pa nyid shes pa'i shes rab po/_/don bzhin rig ces pa ni mtha' dag shes pa'o/_/pha rol phyin pa kun zhes pa ni sa bcu'o/_/
[\[189b.4\]]rdzogs pa zhes pa ni thugs su chud pa'i don to/_/sa rnams zhes pa ni dang po nas sa bcu gcig pa'i bar ro/_/kun zhes pa ni nyan thos dang rang rgyal ba'i sa'o/_/rgyan dang ldan zhes pa ni de dag thams cad ye shes sems dpa' la ldan pa'o/_/rnam par dag pa zhes pa ni don dam
[\[189b.5\]]pa'i bden pa'o/_/bdag med chos zhes pa ni gang zag gi bdag dang chos kyi bdag dang bral ba'o/_/yang dag ye shes zhes bya ba ni chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes so/_/zla 'od bzang zhes pa ni longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'o/_/brtson chen zhes pa ni brtson 'grus dang ldan pa ste

[\[190a.1\]]po mchog ces bya'o/_/rdo rje'i gdan zhes pa ni lha'i gdan bskyed pa'i cho ga yan lag dang bcas pa bstan te/_rdo rje ni stong pa nyid do/_/ma lus ldan zhes pa ni pad+ma dang nyi ma dang zla ba'i gdan dang ldan pa'o/_/ye shes sku rnams ma lus 'chang /_/zhes pa ni ye shes

[\[190b.1\]]kho na nyid mkhyen pa'i ye shes so/_/'byung ba sel zhes pa ni 'khor ba las sgrol ba'o/_/mi g.yo zhes pa ni 'gro ba'i don las mi g.yo ba'o/_/rab tu dang ba'i bdag ces pa ni 'gro ba rnams kyi yid du 'ong ba'o/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas pa'i byang chub 'chang /_/zhes pa ni gzhan don phun

[\[201b.1\]]'dir gsungs pa/_mi 'gyur kun 'gro khyab pa po/_/zhe'am/_sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs la gnas/_/zhes gsungs/_sems can kun gyi yid la gnas/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa lta bu ste/_de la rnam pa bzhi'i tshul gyis khyab pa ni 'di lta ste/_chos nyid dang /_ye shes dang /
[\[201b.2\]]thugs rje dang /_mdzad pa'o/_/de la chos nyid kyis khyab pa ni chos thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa bdag med pa ste/_'di ltar gzhan las/_chos kyi dbyings ni ma gtogs pa/_/chos ni 'ga' yang yod ma yin/_/gsungs pa lta bu'o/_/de bas na chos kyi dbyings ni 'phags pa
[\[201b.3\]]'jam dpal te/_de'i phyir thams cad la khyab pa'o/_/ye shes kyi sgo nas khyab ste/_'di ltar chos kyi dbyings kyi chos can ni rang rig pa tsam ste/_chos thams cad kyang rang rig pa tsam du 'dus pa dang /_ye shes kyi yul du ma gyur ba'i chos nyid kyang med de/_de'i phyir ye shes kyi
[\[201b.4\]]tshul gyis kyang khyab pa'o/_/thugs rjes kyang bya ba ste/_ji ltar dbyings dang ye shes zung du 'brel pa gang na ba de na thugs rje chen po yang rgyun mi 'chad pa yin no/_/de bzhin du mdzad pas kyang khyab ste/_chos de gsum gang du tshogs pa der mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad do/_/de'i phyir sangs
[\[201b.5\]]rgyas rnams kyi thugs dang sems can rnams kyi sems la 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis khyab ste/_chos de dag gang nas ma 'ongs/_gang du yang mi 'gro/_/gar yang gnas par 'gyur ba med bzhin du skal ba dang /_mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can gyi don mdzad par nus pa
[\[201b.6\]]yin no/_/de lta bu'i yon tan brjod pa'i ming thams cad kyang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la 'phags pa 'jam dpal ji ltar na chos thams cad du sprul pa yin zhe na 'di nyid du gsungs pa/_gzugs rnams ma lus snang ba'i dpal/_/sna tshogs gzugs can yid las skyes/_/zhes
[\[201b.7\]]bya ba la sogs pa ji ltar 'gro ba 'dul ba'i dbang gis snod dang bcud du bcas pa'i gzugs sna tshogs su sprul pa dang /_gtsug phud phud bu lcang lo can/_/ral pa muny+dza cod pan thogs/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i skabs su brtul zhugs thams cad 'dzin par sprul pa dang /
[\[202a\]]
[\[202a.1\]]gzugs kyi mtshan nyid kyang longs spyod rdzogs pa'am/_sprul pa'am/_byang chub sems dpa'am/_rang rgyal ba'am/_nyan thos sam/_skye dgu'i bdag po la sogs pa'am/_gzhan yang mdzes pa'i gzugs sam/_mi sdug pa'i gzugs sam/
[\[202a.2\]]rgan po'am/_gzhon pa la sogs pa'i gzugs sam/_gzhan yang nyon mongs pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs sam/_zag pa zad pa la sogs pa'i chos thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan du 'phags pa 'jam dpal mi 'phrul pa med do/_/de bas na de lta bu'i yon tan brjod pa'i
[\[202a.3\]]ming thams cad kyang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na 'phags pa 'jam dpal de chos thams cad la dga' ba yin zhe na 'di nyid du gsungs pa/_dngos don ma lus rnams la dga'/_/stong pa nyid dga' 'dod chags blo/_/srid gsum dga' ba chen po pa/_/zhes bya ba
[\[202a.4\]]la sogs pa gsungs pa lta bu ste/_'gro ba 'dul ba'i dbang gis chos thams cad dga' bar ston pa dang /_snying rje'i dbang gis srid pa la chags pa'i yid dga' ba dang /_shes rab kyi dbang gis stong pa nyid la chags shing dga' ba ste/_de bas na de lta bu'i yon tan gyi dbang du
[\[202a.5\]]gsungs pa'i ming thams cad kyang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na chos thams cad mkhyen pa yin zhe na/_'di nyid du gsungs pa/_shes rab chen pos skad cig la/_/chos kun khong du chud pa po/_/chos kun mngon par rtogs pa po/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa ji skad du
[\[202a.6\]]chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan bstan pa'i dbang du gsungs pa'i ming thams cad kyang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na chos thams cad gsungs pa yin zhe na/_'di nyid du gsungs pa/_smra ba'i skyes mchog smra ba'i rgyal/_/smra ba'i dam pa mchog gi gnas/_/smra
[\[202a.7\]]ba'i seng ge tshugs pa med/_/ces bya ba la sogs pa ste/_ji srid du chos thams cad phyin ci ma log par ston pa'i mnga' bdag yin pas/_de'i dbang du smos pa'i chos thams cad kyi ming yang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na de chos thams cad rnam par dag pa'i
[\[202b\]]
[\[202b.1\]]bdag nyid can yin zhe na/_'di nyid du gsungs pa/_zag pa zad pa dang /_sgrib pa las grol ba dang /_nyon mongs pa zhi bar byed pa dang /_srid pa 'joms pa dang /_'khor ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_chu bo las rgal ba dang /_srid rtsa bton pa la sogs pa zag pa dang
[\[202b.2\]]bcas pa'i chos kyi dri ma dag pa'i sgo nas brjod pa dang /_gzhan dag pa rnam pa bcu gnyis 'chang ba dang /_rnam dag phung po lnga 'chang ba/_pha rol tu phyin pa bcu dag pa dang /_shes pa bcu rnam dag 'chang ba la sogs pa ste/_zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyang mthar phyin pa'i
[\[202b.3\]]sgo nas shin tu rnam par dag pa'i mtshan nyid du ston te/_de ltar chos thams cad rnam par dag pa'i yon tan ston pa'i ming gang smos pa thams cad de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na de chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug yin zhe na/_'di nyid gsungs pa/_chos kyi dbang
[\[202b.4\]]phyug chos kyi rgyal/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa lta bu chos thams cad la mnga' brnyes shing /_de la dbang sgyur ba chos kyi rgyal po dang /_gtso bo dang /_bdag po ston pa'i sgo nas yon tan brjod pa'i ming thams cad kyang de'i mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar na de chos thams cad

[\[202b.6\]]'di ltar de bzhin nyid kyi phyir chos thams cad skyed pa yin pa dang /_thabs dang shes rab kyi phyir sangs rgyas thams cad skyed pa yin pa dang /_'dul ba'i dbang gi phyir sprul pa thams cad skyed pa yin te/_de lta bu la sogs pa yon tan brjod pa'i phyir smos pa'i ming thams cad de'i
[\[202b.7\]]mtshan du 'gyur ro/_/de la ji ltar de chos thams cad las skyes pa yin zhe na/_de chos nyid las skyes pa yin zhes ste/_nam mkha' las byung rang byung ba/_/zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/_/de la ye shes 'ba' zhig las skyes pa zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/_/de sems las skyes pa
[\[203a\]]
[\[203a.1\]]yin te/_sna tshogs gzugs can yid la skyes/_/zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/_/de nyan thos kyi lam dang /_rang sangs rgyas kyi lam dang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi lam thams cad las skyes pa yin te/_nges 'byung sna tshogs las byung ba/_/zhes

[\[203a.4\]]pa bcu'i sgo nas zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos dang /_zag pa med pa'i chos thams cad kyi ming thams cad de'i mtshan du 'gyur ba thun mong du 'gyur ba bstan nas/_da ni khyad par brjod par bya ste/_de la zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos la de'i bdag nyid du ston pa'i tshe/_'di ltar zag pa dang

[\[203b.1\]]mkha' ni gzugs la khyab pa yin gyi brten pa ni ma yin no/_/dper na nam mkha' ni gzugs la khyab pa yin kyang nam mkha'i mtshan nyid gzugs la brten pa ni ma yin te/_de bas na zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos la 'phags pa 'jam dpal brten pa'i tshul nas mtshan mi brjod
[\[203b.2\]]do/_/zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos lta bur sprul zhing 'jug par ston pa'i tshe/_zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos la thugs rje dang 'phrul pa 'jug par ston kyang zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos la ni des bsgos shing byin gyis rlob kyi/_de la zag pa dang bcas pas mi 'dzin cing mi gos
[\[203b.3\]]te/_dper na nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis mi gtsang ba'i sa phyogs su shar ba'i tshe nyi ma'i 'od kyis mi gtsang ba'i sa phyogs su bsgos shing reg par gyur kyang /_dri ma des 'od la bsgos shing byin gyis brlab pa med do/_/de'i phyir thams cad 'jug pas kyang gos pa'i tshul nas mtshan

[\[203b.5\]]brjod pa'i tshe/_zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams ni nyes skyon gyi chos dri ma'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir de bsal zhing zad par byas pa'i sgo nas mtshan brjod pa yin no/_/zag pa med pa'i chos rnam par dag par ston pa'i tshe ni/_de la mi mthun pa'i dri ma thams cad ma lus par gtan
[\[203b.6\]]du zin pa'i phyir rnam par dag pa'i mtshan brjod pa dang /_don dam par gnyis su med pa'i tshul nas brjod pa yin te/_kun rdzob tsam du de dag spang par bya ba yin pas/_spangs shing zad par bya ba'i tshul ni brjod pa ma yin no/_/zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos bskyed par ston pa'i
[\[203b.7\]]tshe/_chos ci yang ma yin pa dang /_shes pa rang rig pa'i sgo nas 'khrul pa'i chos sna tshogs su snang ba'i bdag po'i rkyen du bshad kyi rgyu'i rkyen du mi brjod do/_/de chos thams cad las skyes par bstan pa'i skabs su/_zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos kyi dbang las 'phags pa 'jam
[\[204a\]]
[\[204a.1\]]dpal skye bar bshad kyi de'i rgyu rkyen yin par mi bshad de/_de bas na de de dag gi sgo nas mtshan brjod par mi bya'o/_/zag pa med pa'i chos la khyad par du bstan pa ni de dag las bzlog pa nyid de/_zag med kyi chos kyi mtshan nyid can dang /_chos la brten pa dang /

[\[204a.3\]]gi sgo nas brjod pa dang /_brjod pa ma yin pa yod par bstan pa ste/_'di dag tsam gyis de'i mtshan gang dang gang rnams yin pa mdor bstan pa ste/_rgyas par ni gzhung 'di nyid kyi skabs su bstan pa'i mtshan rnams yan lag dang nying lag tu phye ba de'i mtshan rnams yin no/_/da
[\[204a.4\]]ni de yang dag par ji ltar brjod pa'i tshul bshad par bya ste/_de yang rnam pa gsum mo/_/gsum gang zhe na/_'di ltar mtshan yon tan gyi don du bltas te/_brjod pa'i tshul dang /_mtshan gsang sngags kyi tshul du bltas te brjod pa'i tshul dang /_mtshan gnyis su med
[\[204a.5\]]pa'i don du bltas te brjod pa'i tshul lo/_/de la mtshan yon tan gyi don du bltas te brjod pa'i tshul ji lta bu zhe na/_'di la rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed cing theg pa chen po'i sgor zhugs pa/
[\[204a.6\]]sangs rgyas la shes nas dad pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis thog ma nyid du bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' ni phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid chen po de dag thams cad kyi yon tan phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa/_sangs rgyas thams
[\[204a.7\]]cad kyi thugs rje dang mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa sgrub cing /_sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad kyi re ba yongs su skong ba'i phrin las mdzad pa/_rtag tu sems
[\[204b\]]
[\[204b.1\]]can gyi mdun du bzhugs te/_de bas gang gis 'di'i mtshan brjod pa de la ni bskal pa gang+ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan brjod pas de la dper bzod pa ma yin no zhes dang ba'i dad pa dang /_mos pa sngon du byas te/_de yang sems
[\[204b.2\]]can thams cad kyi don bsgrub pa'i phyir brjod par bya'o zhes smon lam gyis 'phangs pa'i bsam pas byang chub tu sems bskyed nas brjod par bya'o/_/de yang mos pa'i dbang gis 'di ltar yid la byed pas gzhag par bya ste/_bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal ye shes sems
[\[204b.3\]]dpa' ni 'di lta bu'i yon tan can rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang /_thugs rje dang /_byams pa'i mnga' bdag la/_rtag tu gdul bya thams cad kyi mdun na gnas pa'i phyir bdag gis de'i sku khyad par can mdun du yid la byas kyang rung /_ma byas kyang rung ste rtag tu
[\[204b.4\]]mdun na gnas pa'i phyir/_de la brjod pa'i don du bsam pa g.yeng ba med pas mtshan brjod par bya'o/_/gzhan du na bcom ldan 'das kyi rang bzhin de lta bu yin mod kyi/_'on kyang de'i gzugs bzang po khyad par can yid la byas nas/_bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun sum
[\[204b.5\]]tshogs pa la byin gyis rlob par 'gyur ro zhes shes par byas nas/_mdun gyi nam mkha' la rang gi yid las sprul pa'i rin po che'i rang bzhin gyis dpag bsam gyi shing chen po rgyas pa'i grib ma la/_rin po che dang pad+ma'i gdan la zla ba'i dkyil na bzhugs pa'i
[\[204b.6\]]bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i sku kha ba la gur gum gtor ba lta bu sna tshogs kyi na bza' mnabs pa phyag g.yon na ut+pal sngon po rgyas pa bsnams pa/_g.yas pa mchog sbyin can/_'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po chos pa ltar rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan par bsam
[\[204b.7\]]ste/_de'i mtshan mngon par brjod pa'i don g.yeng ba med pa'i yid la byed pas mtshan brjod par bya'o/_/yang na sku mdog dang phyag mtshan ni glegs bam dang /_ral gri dang chos 'chad pa la sogs pa dang /_zla ba'i kha dog dang /_gser btso ma'i kha dog la sogs te ji
[\[205a\]]
[\[205a.1\]]ltar mos pa bzhin du yid la bya'o/_/mchod pa brjod nas 'dod pa'i don la gsol ba btab pa ste/_yongs su dag pa'i zhing khams su gsol nas ldang bar bya'o/_/yang na 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'di ltar bsam par bya ste/_bcom ldan 'das nyid
[\[205a.2\]]snga ma bzhin du bsams pa'i steng gi phyogs su bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la sogs pa phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu byung ba'i tshul gyis bzhugs par bsam mo/_/de'i g.yas kyi phyogs su byang chub sems dpa' byams pa dang /_kun du bzang po dang /
[\[205a.3\]]spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang /_phyag na rdo rje dang /_sa'i snying po dang /_nam mkha'i snying po dang /_sgrib pa rnam par sel ba la sogs te/_bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams khyim pa'i tshul gyis rgyan ma spangs pa'i mtshan du bzhugs par bsam mo/_/
[\[205a.4\]]de'i g.yon phyogs su shA ri'i bu dang /_mod gal gyi bu dang /_rab 'byor dang /_kun dga' bo la sogs te/_dgra bcom pa chen po rnams rab tu byung ba'i tshul gyis bzhugs par bsam mo/_/de'i 'og gi phyogs su lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po la sogs te/_tshangs ris kyi
[\[205a.5\]]lha rnams dang /_tshangs pa chen po dang bcas pa'i gzugs na spyod pa'i lha'i bu rnams kha dog dkar po rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa dang /_brgya byin la sogs pa sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams sna tshogs pa'i rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa bsams te/_de rnams kyi mdun du
[\[205a.6\]]bdag gis phyag 'tshal ba dang /_mchod pa la sogs pa'i yan lag bdun dang ldan pa'i smon lam gyi sgo nas byang chub chen por sems bskyed nas/_de thams cad la mchod pa'i don du bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan brjod par bya'o/_/de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
[\[205a.7\]]pa rnams ni rdo rje rin po che las grub pa'i seng ge'i khri dang /_rin po che pad+ma dang /_nyi ma dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi gdan la mnyam pa'i skyil mo krung dang /_mnyam gzhag gi phyag rgya dang /_chos 'chad kyi phyag rgya can no/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni rin po che dang /
[\[205b\]]
[\[205b.1\]]pad+ma dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la zhabs g.yon pa phab ste skyil mo krung phyed ma dang /_rang rang gi mtshan dang /_chos zhu ba'i phyag rgya can dang /_nyan thos chen po rnams ni rin po che pad+ma'i gdan la chos zhu ba'i tshul du bsam par bya'o/_/rang sangs rgyas rnams ni rang rang gi bzhon pa
[\[205b.2\]]dang /_mtshan ma dang ldan pa'am/_yang na thams cad kyang rin po che'i khri steng na chos zhu ba'i tshul can sha stag go/_/mchod pa rdzogs nas gshegs pa dang /_'dod pa'i don la gsol ba gdab ste rang rang gi zhing dang gnas su gshegs su gsol te ldang bar bya'o/_/spyan
[\[205b.3\]]drang ba ni mi dgos te/_bsams pa tsam nyid kyis byin gyis rlob par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/de dag mtshan yon tan gyi don du bltas te brjod pa yid la byed pa'i tshul yin no/_/yon tan nyid kyi tshul ji lta bu zhig yin zhe na/_pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul dang /_gsang sngags kyi tshul

[\[205b.5\]]thun mong ni dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dang /_bsam gtan dang /_tshad med pa dang /_snyoms par 'jug pa'i las kyis bsdus pa'i mngon par mtho ba'i 'bras bu dang bcas pa rnams dang /_gzhan yang bden pa bzhi dang /_shes pa brgyad dang /_rnam par thar pa la sogs
[\[205b.6\]]pa dge sbyong gi tshul gyi 'bras bu dang bcas pa dang /_de bzhin du phyogs dang /_pha rol tu phyin pa dang /_sa dang /_byang chub sems dpa'i stobs dang /_byang chub sems dpa'i mi 'jigs pa dang /_byang chub sems dpa'i gzungs dang /_ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa rnams
[\[205b.7\]]so/_/thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang /_ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang /_mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang /_gzungs dang /_ting nge 'dzin dang /_thugs rje chen po sum cu gnyis dang /_ma 'dres pa'i dran pa nye bar gzhag pa
[\[206a\]]
